  she still gets to save her child. The **[RETURNED]** shows her the looped moment is a **rescue, not a goodbye**: Bell
  *lived* тАФ grew old, died warm with grandchildren in the room, sixty years bought by *"one, two, out you go."* She
  doesn't need the fire to keep the child; she can carry the saving instead of the burning.
- ЁЯСБя╕П **Three new Returned-senses.** ЁЯзк **+8 gates** (now **1,185 checks**, all green). **39 zones, 132 souls** тАФ
  twenty-two structures, and the player has now been advocate, accused, thief, broker, mediator, judge, builder,
  house-comforter, stage-finisher, and the physician who heals by witnessing rather than curing.

---

## ЁЯСС v6.12.0 тАФ *"The Empty House"* тАФ a thirty-eighth zone: a performance (a tragedian playing to no one) (content)

> A twenty-first structure, and a player-role no zone has held: you don't free a soul, judge a dispute, build a thing,
> or comfort a house тАФ you **finish a play.** **Master Orvel Vane**, the finest tragedian on the Sword Coast, dropped
> dead of a stopped heart three lines from the end of his greatest role, on opening night, mid-soliloquy тАФ and could
> not bear to leave his life's work unfinished, so he has performed *The Fall of Lord Greve* every night for eighty
> years to a house he believes is empty, certain that **a play no one sees never happened.**
- ЁЯОн **A thirty-eighth zone тАФ the Empty House** (a dark playhouse off the Night Market). Three lonelinesses braided so
  that each is the cure for the other two: **Orvel** the tragedian, performing to the dark; **Linnet** the understudy,
  who learned Lady Mourn to the bone and never once went on, eighty years word-perfect in the wings; and **Old Dorra**,
  the laundress who spent a month's coin for a front-row seat, died in it rapt on opening night, and has watched every
  performance since тАФ the one true audience the player on stage has never looked down to see.
- ЁЯОм **The thesis as theatre.** Orvel has *become* Lord Greve тАФ the play is about a man destroyed by needing to be
  remembered, and he is trapped by the very terror it warns against. A **[RETURNED]** names what a soul who died and
  came back would know: a performance no one sees doesn't *un-happen* тАФ you played it, gorgeously, eighty years; **you
  are the work, not the applause.** And his house was never empty: *look down тАФ front row тАФ she has watched every
  night.* One true witness who stayed eighty years is the fullest house a player ever had.
- ЁЯОЯя╕П **A Performance check finishes the eighty-year play.** A non-passive social skill (Charisma) with full **crit and
  fumble** тАФ step into the footlights and speak Lord Greve's missing final line yourself. **Crit:** you play his death
  truer than he ever did and he weeps as the play, suspended eighty years three lines from its end, is finished at
  last. **Fumble:** you call him *Lord GROVE* and ask the empty house to "please applaud" тАФ and the horror cracks into
  the first laugh Orvel has laughed since he died.
- ЁЯкЮ **Two more freed by the same light.** Linnet is the *part she never played* тАФ the **[RETURNED]** frees her to take
  the three paces onto the lit boards at last (the play needs a Lady Mourn; she's been ready eighty years). Dorra is
  the *witness who was never seen* тАФ the **[RETURNED]** makes Orvel finally look down, so the laundress who chose
  beauty over bearing-up rises to her feet, applauding, the first thing he sees after eighty years of the dark.
- ЁЯСБя╕П **Three new Returned-senses.** ЁЯзк **+8 gates** (now **1,177 checks**, all green). **38 zones, 129 souls** тАФ
  twenty-one structures, and the player has now been advocate, accused, thief, broker, mediator, judge, builder,
  comforter of a frightened house, and the soul who steps onto a dead stage to finish an eighty-year tragedy.

---

## ЁЯСС v6.11.0 тАФ *"The House That Remembers"* тАФ a thirty-seventh zone: a sentient building (a soul that became its house) (content)

> A twentieth structure, and a player-role no zone has held: you don't free a soul, judge a dispute, or build a
> thing тАФ you **un-frighten a house.** A carpenter named **Coll** loved his home so fiercely that when he died he did
> not move on but *poured himself into the timber and became the walls* тАФ and now the new family is renovating him
> room by room, and because he is certain he *is* the timber, every changed board feels like a death.
- ЁЯПЪя╕П **A thirty-seventh zone тАФ the House That Remembers** (down the lane off the Weeping House). Three loves tangled
  in one set of walls: **the House** itself (Coll, who became what he built); **Old Bessa**, the housekeeper who kept
  it forty living years and forty dead ones more, and who alone can hear what the walls are trying to say; and
  **little Wick**, a living five-year-old who half-hears the house's grief and has decided, with a child's whole
  heart, to be its friend.
- ЁЯФи **The thesis as carpentry.** The house grieves the *wrong thing* тАФ it thinks it's the boards, so the sanding of
  the children's height-marks off the doorframe feels like being un-made. A **[RETURNED]** names the secret a soul who
  died and came back would know: *you were never the walls.* A house is the **love lived in it**, not the timber тАФ and
  a life that *happened* cannot be sanded off. New paint, new family, new years only **add** to the vessel; a vessel
  doesn't die when new wine is poured in, *it fills.* The house isn't being un-made. It's being **deepened.**
- ЁЯТФ **Bessa's mercy hides a forty-year love.** She means to help the house "let go and move on" тАФ until she's asked
  whether that's what *it* wants or what *she* needs, and admits she'd help a friend die to free herself from a love
  she was too afraid to live. The **[RETURNED]** offers a third way: the house doesn't have to *leave* тАФ it can
  **stay**, stop being afraid, and let her finally say her forty-year part.
- ЁЯХпя╕П **The child is the keystone.** Wick loves the house the way Coll did тАФ not as good bones but as a *friend* тАФ and
  the frightened house has been banging her shutters to drive her off. But she means to grow up on that doorframe, new
  height-marks every year: the house isn't being un-made, it's being **inherited**, and an inherited house never dies.
  The **[RETURNED]** carries her love into the cold so the house can *feel* it.
- ЁЯСБя╕П **Three new Returned-senses.** ЁЯзк **+7 gates** (now **1,169 checks**, all green). **37 zones, 126 souls** тАФ
  twenty structures, and the player has now been advocate, accused, thief, broker, mediator, judge, builder, and the
  one soul who can tell a terrified house it was never the walls.

---

## ЁЯСС v6.10.0 тАФ *"The Cairn That Won't Stand"* тАФ a thirty-sixth zone: a construction (build a beacon of true names) (content)

> A nineteenth structure, and a fresh *activity* тАФ you don't free a soul or judge a dispute, you help **build**
> something. **Master Cobb** raised a lighthouse in life that brought ten thousand ships home, and now cannot make a
> single stone of a beacon for the lost dead stand тАФ and the reason is the saga's whole thesis rendered as masonry.
- ЁЯки **A thirty-sixth zone тАФ the Cairn That Won't Stand** (off the last torch). Three souls: **Cobb**, the
  master-builder who has the vision and the craft and keeps failing; **Goodwife Pell**, his neighbor who hauls stones
  she's stopped believing will hold, just so he isn't building his grief alone; and **a Newly-Dead**, turning lost
  circles with no marker to find тАФ the living proof of why the beacon matters.
- ЁЯз▒ **The thesis as masonry.** Cobb quarries his stones from the *honored* dead тАФ GLORY, REMEMBRANCE, the names of
  kings тАФ and they slide, because a king is held by ten thousand living mouths and needs no holding, *and a stone
  that needs no holding cannot bind.* **Investigation** finds it's the *material*, not the craft; a **[RETURNED]**
  names the secret: a marker for the forgotten holds only on *true names* тАФ the small real ones, the forgotten,
  because *a name that needs holding is the only stone that binds.* (Pell, who's hauled every stone, has noticed it
  herself: the grand ones slide fastest, the small ones almost hold.)
- ЁЯХпя╕П **The keystone is the lost soul itself.** The Newly-Dead тАФ *Eddin, a fisher, drowned yesterday in a fouled net*,
  certain it's nothing тАФ gives you its true name before the Hunger takes it, and *that* becomes the keystone: the
  foundation the whole beacon stands on, so no soul after it ever turns in the dark alone. *"Tell the next lost soul
  that finds its way by us тАФ a fisher named Eddin is holding it up."*
- ЁЯСБя╕П **Three new Returned-senses.** ЁЯзк **+7 gates** (now **1,162 checks**, all green). **36 zones, 123 souls** тАФ
  nineteen structures, and the player has now been advocate, accused, thief, broker, mediator, judge, and *builder.*

> A cohesion pass. The side-roads payoff (v6.3.0) covered the first batch of structures; four more shipped since
> (the Connoisseur, the Custody, the Long Walk, the Moot). Now the epilogue Chronicler reads *all eighteen* тАФ a
> fourth **harder roads** cluster pays off the newest, so nothing built is left out of the years-after.
- ЁЯУЦ **A fourth Chronicler cluster тАФ *the harder roads*** тАФ reactive to the four newest structures:
  - **The Connoisseur** (`pd.the_fire_plan`): the soul-eater *cooked in the suffering he spent three centuries
    making, by the souls he thought too scattered to count* тАФ not redeemed, *stopped*; the Half-Taken walks free,
    too loved to swallow. Filed under *justice тАФ the cold kind.*
  - **The Custody** (`cu.child_freed`): Wren freed тАФ neither tethered nor stored тАФ having said a real goodbye and
    passed her promise to the Returned; Sefa grieves *clean* now; and the Factor *filed it under the column it had
    never once been able to use: released. It wept.*
  - **The Moot** (`mt.carry_is_key`): the century deadlock dissolved тАФ the low fields drained and farmed, the deep
    village left flooded, a new cairn at the waterline (*farm above, not below*); the living's children fed, Wend's
    babies undisturbed, and young Sprat freed at last to walk the good door.
  - **The Long Walk** (`pl.arrived_goes_in`): Old Ferd took the last step; the whole creed re-aimed to *arrive useful,
    not proud*, and Tamsin keeps the halfway for every frozen pilgrim after.
- ЁЯХпя╕П A graceful **default** as ever, for a run that walked other ways.

## ЁЯСС v6.8.0 тАФ *"The Moot of the Drowned"* тАФ a thirty-fifth zone: a collective-decision structure (content)

> An eighteenth structure тАФ a **moot**, a crowd to sway rather than a single soul, and a genuine living-vs-dead
> conflict where *both sides are right.* A flooded village's dead have been deadlocked for a century: the living
> above the water want to drain the flood and reclaim the rich bottomland their children go thin without; draining it
> exposes the drowned village тАФ the resting dead тАФ to the sun and the plough.
- тЪЦя╕П **A thirty-fifth zone тАФ the Moot of the Drowned** (down from the Underbridge). Three voices: **the Tide-Reader**
  (the neutral keeper who calls the question and counts the even vote, year after year), **Old Mother Wend** (who
  votes to keep it drowned тАФ the dead's rest), and **Sprat** (who votes to drain it тАФ the living's bread).
- ЁЯОн **A real deadlock, honestly built.** The keeper lays out that it's *not good against evil* тАФ the dead's rest
  against the living's bread, neither worth less, the tide bringing them up *even* every moot. Both rulings are
  defensible. But the keeper, sworn to neutrality, names what it has never dared say to the circle: *a moot held even
  for a century is not one that can't decide тАФ it's one that doesn't want to,* because both sides are arguing the
  water and meaning something else.
- ЁЯМК **The thing under the water.** Wend isn't guarding the dead's rest тАФ she's guarding *three small graves* (Bett,
  Corin, little Max who was two) from the sun, and can't bear the light to find her children. Sprat doesn't care about
  the turnips тАФ he drowned at fourteen, cheated of a life, and wants *permission to move on*; the flood is the chain
  binding the whole circle. Each votes its secret heart and calls it a vote about a field тАФ and neither, in a century,
  has once asked the other what they're holding.
- ЁЯМЙ **The [RETURNED] dissolves the tie instead of breaking it.** You can cross тАФ carry the living's *true* need (not
  all the land, not the graves, perhaps just the upper fields) down, and the dead's *true* fear (not "no change ever"
  but "don't let the sun touch the children's graves") up тАФ replacing a century of guesses with what the other side
  actually says. (The elder's and the young one's true-fear beats are gated on the keeper first revealing what lies
  under the water тАФ real moot logic.)
- ЁЯСБя╕П **Three new Returned-senses.** ЁЯзк **+8 gates** (now **1,154 checks**, all green). **35 zones, 120 souls** тАФ
  eighteen structures, and the player has now mediated not just a soul but *a hundred-year political deadlock.*

---

## ЁЯСС v6.7.0 тАФ *"The Long Walk"* тАФ a thirty-fourth zone: a pilgrimage (a road of stations) (content)

> A seventeenth structure, and a *moving* one тАФ a road, not a room. The souls who refuse to be ferried to the Court
> and **walk** it on foot, every grey mile a devotion. You meet three pilgrims at three stations of the journey тАФ
> and because the Returned has *been* to the destination the whole creed walks toward, you can tell each of them the
> truth the road hides.
- ЁЯе╛ **A thirty-fourth zone тАФ the Long Walk** (off the Grey Wayshrine). Three stations: **Brother Calwin**, three
  days set out, radiant and certain; **Goodwife Tamsin**, frozen at the doubting halfway, facing neither up nor
  down; and **Old Ferd**, who walked the whole three hundred miles and *will not take the last step.*
- ЁЯзн **Each station interrogates faith differently.** The **starter** believes the walking *earns* the Judge тАФ and a
  **[RETURNED]** who's stood before Kelemvor can re-aim the creed (the god is drowning, not weighing; arrive *useful*,
  not proud) or disillusion it (the walking changes only the walker, never the Judge тАФ a vanity with blisters). The
  **doubter** is stuck because she thinks the road has only two directions, both defeats тАФ until you give her the
  *third axis*: turn sideways, *keep the halfway* for the next frozen pilgrim. The **arrived** soul is trapped by its
  own success тАФ it became the walking so completely that finishing un-makes the only self it has тАФ and only a soul
  that's been *through* the door can free it: *the door isn't the end of the walking; it's where the walking finally
  arrives somewhere it can do good. The work of the dead never finishes.*
- ЁЯСБя╕П **Three new Returned-senses.** ЁЯзк **+8 gates** (now **1,146 checks**, all green). **34 zones, 117 souls** тАФ
  seventeen structures, and the saga has now examined faith from the inside (the disputation argued whether the Wall
  is just; the pilgrimage asks whether the *destination* is worth the walking).

---

## ЁЯСС v6.6.0 тАФ *"The Custody of the Small"* тАФ a thirty-third zone: an arbitration (a trilemma over a dead child) (content)

> A sixteenth structure, and a player-role the saga hadn't asked of you: **arbiter.** Not a stuck soul to free, but a
> dispute to *judge* тАФ a dead godless child, **Wren the Younger**, claimed by two parties with mutually exclusive,
> partly-legitimate needs, and a ruling you must deliver knowing every option has a cost.
- тЪЦя╕П **A thirty-third zone тАФ the Custody of the Small** (off the Lamplit Quarter). Three parties: **Goodwife Sefa**,
  the grieving mother who *will not let go* (tethering her daughter to the living world, fading her by the day тАФ and
  she knows it, and can't stop); **the Factor**, a Choir clerk who'd take the child into *loveless grey storage* тАФ
  eternal, safe, a six-year-old kept at six forever (the least-cruel column the Concord permits); and **the child.**
- ЁЯОн **A real trilemma.** You can **rule for the tether** (a child belongs with the soul that loves it, whatever it
  costs) or **rule for the storage** (safe beats dissolving) тАФ both real, both costly, both gated on hearing each
  claim. But the twist is the indictment the Factor itself names: *a fortnight of fighting over the child's head, and
  neither party once asked the child.* Rule without asking and it lands as `cu.child_unasked` тАФ a brave, breaking
  six-year-old smile that you came all the way over to it and decided *for* it anyway.
- ЁЯМЯ **The best path is the one nobody took: ask the child.** Wren chewed on it for a fortnight and has the answer
  ready тАФ it isn't stuck between hurting its mother and breaking its promise (*"I'll mind you, Mama"*) if a grown-up
  will help it **mind her first**: a real goodbye (the thing the fading would steal), the promise *passed* to the
  Returned who comes back to check on her, and then the child goes **free** тАФ neither tethered nor stored. The third
  door was always the child's to name; the grown-ups just never put the smallest voice *last, where the small ones
  count the most.*
- ЁЯТЫ Even the cold Factor secretly hopes you find it тАФ *"I would rather you found it than win... I'll file it under a
  column I've never once been able to use: released."*
- ЁЯСБя╕П **Three new Returned-senses.** ЁЯзк **+8 gates** (now **1,138 checks**, all green). **33 zones, 114 souls** тАФ
  sixteen structures, and the player has now been advocate, accused, thief, broker, mediator, and *judge.*

---

## ЁЯСС v6.5.0 тАФ *"The Connoisseur's Parlor"* тАФ a thirty-second zone: the saga's thesis, tested (content)

> A fifteenth structure тАФ and the first that deliberately *interrogates* the saga's thesis instead of affirming it.
> Every monster on the causeway so far has been a wound you could witness back into a person тАФ the forgotten Gnaw,
> the desperate warden. **Goodman Vell** is not. He is a soul-eater with *no wound under it*: an ordinary wine-taster
> who brushed another soul's memory, found it exquisite, and chose to keep eating, refining it into an art across
> three centuries тАФ because he *likes* it. He cannot be witnessed home, because he does not wish to leave.
- ЁЯН╖ **A thirty-second zone тАФ the Connoisseur's Parlor** (off the Night Market). Three souls: **Vell** the eater;
  **the Half-Taken**, a soul being savoured slowly and aware (the awareness is the seasoning); and **the Emptied**,
  a husk eaten past its name but not past one stubborn ember.
- ЁЯкЮ **The thesis, tested honestly.** An **Insight** read confirms what the saga wasn't built for тАФ *there is no part
  of him to save; he is what any ordinary soul becomes when you remove every consequence and leave only the
  appetite.* A **[RETURNED]** names it: you carry the dead so they're not borne alone; he eats them so they're not
  borne at all тАФ the same reach, pointed opposite тАФ and this is *the first thing you can only stop.*
- ЁЯТЫ **Witness still saves the innocent тАФ just not the guilty.** The Half-Taken can't be fought free (struggle
  aerates the meal; the eater *wants* you to fight). But you can **witness the prey too whole to swallow** тАФ hold the
  one thing he couldn't eat, an ordinary contented Tuesday, until the soul stops suffering, because despair is his
  whole palate and *a soul that knows it's held has no despair to season it.*
- ЁЯФе **The villain you *stop*, not save.** The husks he scattered (the same trick the Wall plays тАФ scatter the
  forgotten so they never add up) each kept one bitter ember of grudge, the one flavour he can't swallow. The
  Returned, who *gathers* the dead, can carry them together into one room and one fire he must stand in тАФ *cooked at
  last in the suffering he spent three centuries making, by the ones he thought too scattered to count.* Not
  redeemed. Not witnessed home. Just stopped.
- ЁЯСБя╕П **Three new Returned-senses.** ЁЯзк **+8 gates** (now **1,130 checks**, all green). **32 zones, 111 souls** тАФ
  fifteen structures, and the saga's thesis is now *load-bearing under stress*, not just decorative.

---

## ЁЯСС v6.4.0 тАФ *"Dace and Orin, Years On"* тАФ companion parity: the older companions get their epilogue codas (content)

> A parity pass. Sennet and the Sparrow each got the full four-beat arc (recruit тЖТ fire тЖТ threshold тЖТ epilogue);
> **Dace** and **Orin** had everything but the last beat. Now they have it тАФ and their years-after lands the same
> weight as the newer companions'.
- ЁЯЧбя╕П **Dace Iron's coda** (gated on `party.dace_recruited`): the Faithless sellsword who hoarded one unspent *yes*
  for ten grey years and spent it on you. Years on, she turned a blade-for-hire into a **shield-for-free** тАФ guarding
  godless paupers, almshouse-keepers, ferry-folk for no coin тАФ and waits for the Wall *unafraid*, because she watched
  the one soul it lost walk free. A [RETURNED] "soldier to soldier" beat: the ten years weren't warm, they were
  *unspent*; you made her death worth anything at all; she'd throw in again every day there is, and that loyalty is
  the one thing she never sold.
- тЪЦя╕П **Orin's coda** (gated on `party.orin_may_join`): the justiciar who traded a lifetime of certainties for one
  honest doubt at the threshold. Years on, she's a **counter-justiciar** тАФ turning every skill the Choir gave her to
  *guard* the Wall against the Wall itself, finding the unlawful reckonings, naming the forged writs, arguing the
  Faithless free in the order's own language. A [RETURNED] exchange: she'd choose you again *precisely because* you
  might still go wrong and *know* it тАФ certainty is the fall, doubt is the safeguard тАФ and she watches still, ready
  to choose *for* you one last time if the day ever comes, praying it never will.
- ЁЯСБя╕П **Two new Returned-senses** for the codas (the Faithless chill melted by a cause spent freely; the soul that
  paid the highest price in the tally and counts it the best trade of its death).
- ЁЯзк **+2 gates** (now **1,123 checks**, all green). **All four recruitable companions now span the full saga** тАФ
  recruit to years-after. **108 souls.**

## ЁЯСС v6.3.0 тАФ *"The Side-Roads"* тАФ the payoff pass: the epilogue chronicler reads the new structures (content)

> Not a new zone тАФ a **cohesion pass.** The fourteen self-contained side-structures built across v4.94тАУv6.2.0 all
> resolved beautifully in the moment, but they didn't *land* in the ending. Now they do: the epilogue's **Chronicler**
> ("Some Years After") gained a **side-roads** topic that reads, reactively, how each of them turned out тАФ so the
> quiet deeds you did where no saga was watching get their years-after, the same as Wren and Pip and the rest.
- ЁЯУЦ **A new Chronicler topic** тАФ *the side-roads* тАФ branching into three reactive clusters:
  - **The cellar courts** тАФ reads `tr.annet_spared` and `as.verdict_trustworthy`: the midwife walked free *and* the
    Choir's summary reckonings were abolished within years; your own Assize became scripture among the dead, *the
    Returned who refused to be acquitted.*
  - **The bargains in the dark** тАФ reads the Scrivener, the Advocate, the Heist, the Siege: Jergal *still auditing
    the Wall empty one true line at a time*; the Nine's precedent never set (the unclaimed protected forever); the
    Great Tally burned (the frail scattered, the many spared) or carried to Jergal (all freed whole); the almshouse
    that became the first of a whole network of open doors.
  - **The songs and the rooms** тАФ reads the Deathsong, the Locked Room, the Thin Place, the Boasting-Ring, the Wake,
    the Disputation: the art that didn't die in a reed-bed; Coll who turned around and went to the supper kept warm;
    the reunion that un-did the Wall's deepest cruelty for three souls at once; the contest taught to stop being one.
- ЁЯХпя╕П Every cluster has a **default** line too тАФ a soul that walked other roads still gets an honest years-after, and
  the page is kept *whether or not you turned it.* (The richest single outcome on each axis narrates; the threads
  the player skipped quietly don't.)
- ЁЯзк **+5 gates** (now **1,121 checks**, all green): the topic exists, each cluster reads its outcomes reactively,
  and each has a graceful default. The side-content now *pays off in the ending* instead of sitting beside it.

## ЁЯСС v6.2.0 тАФ *"The Locked Room"* тАФ a thirty-first zone: a memory-dive (free a soul by showing it the truth) (content)

> A fourteenth new structure тАФ the **memory-dive** тАФ and a new *mechanic*: you step *inside* a soul's worst night,
> a single minute worn into a groove ten thousand repetitions deep, and you free it not by argument but by showing
> it the memory **true** тАФ because it remembers wrong. Guilt repainted the scene.
- ЁЯМА **A thirty-first zone тАФ the Locked Room** (entered off the Reed-Walk, with your dead-touched senses). Three
  pieces of one frozen night: **Coll**, the dreamer looping on the cup, the cruel word, the flinch; **the Frozen
  Woman**, his wife Edda, held mid-gesture; and **the Way Out**, a window he will not turn to face.
- ЁЯФН **Real dive logic.** Coll relives the night as a *murder* тАФ he said something cruel, she stormed out in fury,
  took a chill and died hating him. But reach into the frozen echo and the truth is the opposite: Edda knew him
  thirty years, forgave the frightened word *between the door and the step*, was planning the supper to make it
  right тАФ and the fever that took her *didn't care what he said.* You can only **free** the dreamer once you've
  learned the true version from her first (the beats are gated on it) тАФ and freeing him **breaks the loop** (the cup
  hangs unfallen; he turns, for the first time, to the window).
- ЁЯкЯ **The dive names the saga's deepest pattern.** The Way Out reads what every self-built cage on the causeway is
  made of тАФ the Reed-Wife, the philosopher, the confessor, all of them holding their own cell doors shut from the
  inside тАФ *not "I cannot leave" but "I do not deserve to."* The window was never locked. The key is never absolution
  from outside; it's the soul finally believing it's allowed to set the weight down and come to the supper kept warm
  past all reason, by a love waiting just past the glass.
- ЁЯСБя╕П **Three new Returned-senses.** ЁЯзк **+8 gates** (now **1,116 checks**, all green). **31 zones, 106 souls** тАФ
  fourteen self-contained structures, every one resolved on *witness, not force.*

---

## ЁЯСС v6.1.0 тАФ *"The Last Deathsong"* тАФ a thirtieth zone: a teaching structure (learn the craft) (content)

> A thirteenth new structure тАФ the **teaching**, where you don't free a soul, you *learn a craft* тАФ and it's the
> capstone of the saga's whole "witness through voice" thread (the wake's songs, the thin-place river-tune, the
> boast). **Old Mireth** is the last soul alive who knows the **deathsong**: the dying art of singing a soul out
> through the good door by singing it so *true* it believes, at last, that it was real.
- ЁЯО╝ **A thirtieth zone тАФ the Last Deathsong** (a quieter song upriver of the wake). Three souls: **Mireth** the last
  cantor; **the Unsung**, a soul that won't be sung because it's certain it deserves to fade; and **Pen**, the
  doubting apprentice who learned the notes and not the heart.
- ЁЯУЦ **You learn the craft.** The deathsong's secret is the saga's thesis made into a teachable art: *no magic notes
  тАФ witness made melodic.* You learn a soul true first (its name, its life, its wound), then sing *that* back until
  it believes it existed, and a soul that believes it was real can open the door no god will force. Learning it sets
  a flag the player carries тАФ and a **[RETURNED]** can promise to carry the song *through* the door, to the walled
  and the far-side fading, so the ten-thousand-year art doesn't die with its last master.
- ЁЯО╡ **The hardest first song.** The Unsung тАФ a good physician undone by one tired fatal error тАФ can only be sung
  once you've *learned it true* (the song beats are gated on hearing its confession). And you don't sing it clean,
  you sing it *finished*: the good and the killing both, until it hears its worst thing witnessed whole and learns a
  soul that's punished itself this faithfully has already served the sentence. The **[RETURNED]** can instead turn
  its penance inside-out тАФ fading robs its victim of its last true mourner.
- ЁЯСитАНЁЯПл **The apprentice's correction** keeps the art alive past the last cantor: Pen sings flawless notes *at*
  strangers and wonders why nothing happens; teach it (or talk it off quitting) that the sitting-and-learning *is*
  the art, and the deathsong has two keepers instead of none.
- ЁЯСБя╕П **Three new Returned-senses.** ЁЯзк **+8 gates** (now **1,108 checks**, all green). **30 zones, 103 souls** тАФ
  thirteen self-contained structures, every one resolved on *witness, not force.*

---

## ЁЯСС v6.0.0 тАФ *"The Boasting-Ring"* тАФ a twenty-ninth zone, and the hundredth soul ЁЯОЙ (content)

> A milestone release: a twelfth new structure тАФ the **contest** тАФ that crosses the walkable saga past **100 souls**
> across **29 zones** and **1,100 green checks.** And the structure is the saga's whole thesis turned into a party:
> the dead stave off the Wall by telling the grandest *true* story of their lives, because to be witnessed, loudly,
> by many, is to be too vivid for the Hunger to un-make.
- ЁЯФе **A twenty-ninth zone тАФ the Boasting-Ring** (off the Night Market). Three souls: **Big Sorrel**, the ringmaster
  who disguised the cleverest mercy on the causeway as a drinking game (a machine that holds the forgotten in the
  world, forty witnesses at once); **the Reigning Tongue**, the undefeated champion *starving behind his crown*
  because he's spent his one true story and started to lie; and **the Smallest Voice**, a temple-sweeper fading
  fastest because a gentle ordinary life doesn't boast easy.
- ЁЯПЖ **The structure pays off the whole saga.** Take the log and tell your own grand true story (you walked *out* of
  the Wall тАФ the boast that breaks the ring). Read the champion (Insight) as a soul hollowed by false boasts, and
  free him by letting him *lose* тАФ the one move the game can't counter. And reframe the sweeper's "nothing" тАФ forty
  years keeping clean stone for the grieving to fall on тАФ as the grand thing it always was; with the champion's
  yielded crown, the **humblest soul in the ring is crowned and saved**, fading stopped, proof a small life
  well-lived outboasts any dragon-slaying.
- ЁЯСБя╕П **Three new Returned-senses.** ЁЯзк **+10 gates** тАФ the suite crosses **1,100 checks**, all green.
- ЁЯМЯ **The milestone:** the walkable causeway is now **29 connected zones, 100 souls, 973 dialogue beats** тАФ a
  complete saga (Prologue тЖТ the Court of the Dead тЖТ the years after) threaded with **two full four-beat companion
  arcs** (Sennet, the Sparrow) and **twelve self-contained side-structures**: investigation, monster-redemption,
  riddle-vault, barter, companion-recruit, courtroom, god's-bargain, heist, self-trial, siege, wake, whodunit,
  reunion, disputation, confession, and contest тАФ every one resolved by the saga's single thesis: *witness, not
  force; the third door, not the necessary cruelty.*

---

## ЁЯСС v5.11.0 тАФ *"The Unburdening"* тАФ a twenty-eighth zone: a confession structure (witness, don't absolve) (content)

> An eleventh new structure тАФ the **confession** тАФ where *you* are the one who hears, and the mechanic is your
> *response.* Three penitents, three guilts, and a single hard-won lesson: absolution was never the confessor's to
> give; cheap grace traps, and witnessing-without-judgment is what frees.
- тЫк **A twenty-eighth zone тАФ the Unburdening** (off the Hearth). Three souls: **the Penitent Baker** (a small wrong
  that grew тАФ a shut door, a child dead three streets over, carried as murder); **the Silent Watchman** (a *failure
  to act* тАФ one unsaid word that would have saved a man); and **Goodman Vance** (the hard case тАФ a real cruelty, and
  a soul that wants easy absolution).
- ЁЯСВ **Hearing comes before answering** тАФ the response beats are gated on having heard the whole confession first.
  And the right-sizing is the cure: the baker isn't a murderer (carry the grief, set down the guilt); the watchman
  carries forty murderers' crime as his one silence (name it real, but one soul's worth, not forty's). A **[RETURNED]**
  can *carry* the weight into the cold, not to erase it but so it isn't borne alone.
- ЁЯЪк **The unrepentant soul tests the whole thesis.** Vance has said *sorry* a thousand times and rages that the door
  stays shut тАФ because he's sorry it's *kept* him here, not sorry he *did* it. Grant him the cheap grace he begs for
  and the door *stays dark* (cheap forgiveness is the chain тАФ it lets him not feel it, and the not-feeling is what
  seals him). An **Insight** read names the performance; the **[RETURNED]** *refuses* the cheap grace тАФ the harder,
  kinder thing тАФ and that refusal is the first true mercy anyone's done him, because it makes him finally carry the
  weight until it lands.
- ЁЯСБя╕П **Three new Returned-senses.** ЁЯзк **+8 gates** (now **1,091 checks**, all green). **28 zones, 97 souls** тАФ eleven
  fresh structures this stretch; three souls short of a hundred.

---

## ЁЯСС v5.10.0 тАФ *"The Unfinished Argument"* тАФ a twenty-seventh zone: a disputation (free a soul by finishing its argument) (content)

> A tenth new structure тАФ the **disputation.** A dead philosopher, Makeb the Elder, has argued the justice of the
> Wall with an empty chair for three hundred years, anchored not by guilt or grief but by his own *undefeated record* тАФ
> a mind that won its great argument so thoroughly it forgot how to think. You free him not by losing to him, but by
> letting *him* lose, gracefully, for the first time in three centuries.
- ЁЯЧгя╕П **A twenty-seventh zone тАФ the Unfinished Argument** (off the Market). Three souls, three anchors: **Makeb** the
  philosopher; **Sennia** the rival who walked out mid-argument and has refused the empty chair ever since; and
  **Doby** the student who keeps the minutes of a meeting that never adjourns.
- тЪФя╕П **A real debate.** **Insight** diagnoses him (you don't *want* to win тАФ winning is the chain); **Persuasion**
  argues the negative (the nat-20 turns his own affirmative inside out: *necessity is the confession of a failed
  cosmos*, a defense that was always an indictment); and the argument escalates to the saga's whole thesis тАФ **the
  third door**: *necessity is a failure of imagination wearing a fact's robe*, and he spent three centuries answering
  the wrong question flawlessly. The **[RETURNED]** finishes it with testimony тАФ a witness who's *been* inside death
  beats a philosopher who argued it from a chair.
- ЁЯТФ **Every anchor is the same chain, worn differently:** Sennia won't sit not from pride but because finishing might
  prove her wrong тАФ and beneath even that, the longest unsaid love in the after (she stayed *near him* three
  centuries rather than move on without the teacher who wounded her). Doby files forever because the quarrel is its
  excuse to stay near the two it loved. The keeper-student knows the real answer: *they're both right*, which is
  exactly why it never ends тАФ and the way out is to aim the two finest minds on the causeway at the Wall *together*
  instead of at each other.
- ЁЯСБя╕П **Three new Returned-senses.** ЁЯзк **+8 gates** (now **1,083 checks**, all green). **27 zones, 94 souls** тАФ ten
  fresh structures this stretch (bargain, trial, heist, devil-pact, self-trial, siege, wake, whodunit, reunion,
  disputation).

---

## ЁЯСС v5.9.0 тАФ *"The Thin Place"* тАФ a twenty-sixth zone: a reunion across the Wall (the logistics of love) (content)

> A ninth new structure тАФ the **reunion** тАФ and the most intimate yet. At the Wall's foot, where the stone runs
> thin, a widow kneels nightly to hear her walled husband *breathe.* She can only listen. You are the one soul who
> can *cross.*
- ЁЯТФ **A twenty-sixth zone тАФ the Thin Place** (off the last torch). Three souls: **Goodwife Pell**, who has knelt at
  the Wall for a year with a last word she never got to say; **a voice in the stone** тАФ Aldous, her husband, walled
  and fading, near enough the thin place to be almost heard; and **the Reed-Knower**, who maps where the Wall goes
  thinnest.
- ЁЯУи **A courier structure with real logistics.** Learn who Aldous was and the message Pell owes him (*you're not
  alone, I came back, I'm sorry I was late*), then тАФ as the **[RETURNED]** who can walk back to the Wall's edge тАФ
  carry it *through.* The beats at Aldous are gated on what you learned from Pell first: give him back his **name**
  (the Wall takes the *who* first, and a name handed back catches the scattering soul like a hand around a coal),
  deliver Pell's **message**, and bring his answer back тАФ *she was never late; the last thing he felt wasn't fear of
  the dark, it was wishing he could tell her not to blame herself.*
- ЁЯО╢ **The reunion lands** in the saga's quietest triumph: you ask Aldous to sing the bad old river-song into the
  dark, and through the thin place Pell's voice тАФ weeping тАФ joins the filthy third verse, forty years and a Wall
  between them, *singing together.* "This is better than getting out. Let the dark come now. I'm singing with my
  wife."
- ЁЯЧ║я╕П **The Reed-Knower** turned its worst failure into a map of mercy: it knelt at the wrong seam while its own
  daughter faded un-heard, and has spent forty years learning every thin place so no other love lands on deaf
  granite тАФ and it will *witness* your crossing, the thing it could never do itself.
- ЁЯСБя╕П **Three new Returned-senses.** ЁЯзк **+9 gates** (now **1,074 checks**, all green). **26 zones, 91 souls** тАФ nine
  fresh structures this stretch, the saga's thesis proven one more way: *the Wall's deepest cruelty is making the
  dead believe they are unheard, and every voice that crosses, even once, un-does it.*

---

## ЁЯСС v5.8.0 тАФ *"The Inquest of the Un-Made"* тАФ a twenty-fifth zone: a whodunit with clue-gated accusation (content)

> An eighth new structure, and a genuinely new *mechanic* тАФ **deduction.** A soul named Sella has been *un-made*:
> not walled, not moved on, but *erased*, root and memory, which the dead are not supposed to be able to do to each
> other. You gather clues from the souls around the absence and make a **clue-gated accusation** тАФ and the solution
> is a Crown-of-Horns trolley problem.
- ЁЯФН **A twenty-fifth zone тАФ the Inquest** (off the Underbridge). Three roles: **Old Gantry**, who keeps vigil over
  the soul-shaped hole; **the Bereaved**, who loved Sella and is losing even the memory of her to the erasure; and
  **the Quiet Neighbor**, the one soul in a terrified place who isn't afraid.
- ЁЯзй **Real deduction.** You can't accuse until you've gathered evidence from *both* the bereaved (who saw the
  Neighbor weeping with Sella the night before) and the absence itself (a **[RETURNED]** can read the clean,
  *channeled* erasure тАФ a soul drained, not destroyed, by a hand that walked away fuller). Only with both clues does
  the accusation option unlock at Gantry.
- ЁЯЪГ **The twist is the saga's whole question, catchable.** The Neighbor isn't a predator тАФ it's a **warden.** It
  found a Hunger-fragment in the old foundations and feeds it one carefully-chosen soul to keep it from eating
  *everyone*: the exact arithmetic of the Concord, run small and honest and alone, *right every time*, which is the
  horror. **Insight** reveals it's emptier, not fuller, each time. And a Returned who learned the bargain can hand
  it the **third door** тАФ the cistern's lesson, that the Hunger feeds on being *forgotten*, not on death, so it's had
  the cure backwards, feeding the fragment the very forgotten souls it grows on.
- ЁЯХпя╕П **Witness beats erasure:** the dead-touched player can carry the erased Sella *into the cold* where the un-making
  can't reach, so the gentlest soul on the Underbridge isn't gone тАФ she lives, witnessed, in you.
- ЁЯСБя╕П **Three new Returned-senses.** ЁЯзк **+9 gates** (now **1,065 checks**, all green). **25 zones, 88 souls** тАФ eight
  fresh structures this stretch (bargain, trial, heist, devil-pact, self-trial, siege, wake, whodunit).

## ЁЯСС v5.7.0 тАФ *"The Wake of Goodman Doget"* тАФ a twenty-fourth zone: tonal relief, a celebration among the grief (content)

> After six grand structures of cosmic weight, a deliberate change of key: the one gathering on the whole grey
> causeway where the dead *celebrate.* A wake тАФ a funeral-feast for a soul who died *fair* тАФ warm and funny and full
> of songs, with the saga's ache threaded quietly underneath it, so the warmth and the cruelty throw each other into
> sharper relief.
- ЁЯН║ **A twenty-fourth zone тАФ the Wake** (upriver off the Reed-Walk). Three souls: **Tib Garron**, a publican who
  died pouring and throws wakes for the fairly-dead *in protest* against a cosmos that murders fairness; **Goodman
  Doget**, the guest of honor, an old farmer who lived sixty square years and died easy тАФ the rarest thing on the
  causeway; and **the Uninvited**, a Faithless soul at the window, grieving the send-off it will never get.
- ЁЯО╢ **Warmth with the ache under it.** Doget can tell you, from the far side, exactly what a *fair death* feels like
  (the gold evening, the good ache, the earned sitting-down) тАФ and then charge you not to *envy* it but to make it
  the *rule* instead of a one-in-ten-thousand miracle. Tib's wakes turn out to be a *drunk recurring protest*; the
  nat-warm toast radicalizes him. And the saga's softest wisdom: a turnip-farmer's secret that you save the cosmos
  the same way you farm an acre тАФ one small right thing in front of you, repeated, until it adds up to something you
  couldn't see coming.
- ЁЯХпя╕П **The small mercy that fixes the one crack:** you can **invite the Faithless soul in.** The window was only ever
  cracked open; throw it wide, and the wake stops being for the *deserving* dead and becomes one for *whoever the
  stone forgot to let be loved.* Or carry its song (a filthy dockhand's work-tune) so it gets the one wake the Wall
  can't reach тАФ the kind that lives in someone else's mouth.
- ЁЯСБя╕П **Three new Returned-senses.** ЁЯзк **+7 gates** (now **1,056 checks**, all green). **24 zones, 85 souls** тАФ and the
  causeway, for one firelit hour, remembers what it was all supposed to feel like.

## ЁЯСС v5.6.0 тАФ *"The Siege of the Almshouse"* тАФ a twenty-third zone: a siege held by witness, not the sword (content)

> A sixth new structure тАФ the **siege** тАФ and, true to the saga, one whose win condition is *moral, not martial.*
> The Choir's enforcement arm, forty strong under **Justiciar Vane**, lays siege to the last almshouse in the
> Lamplit Quarter that will shelter the Faithless. You hold it тАФ but never with a blade.
- ЁЯЫбя╕П **A twenty-third zone тАФ the Siege** (off the Lamplit Quarter). Three roles: **Goodwife Orla** (a Wall-warden of
  nineteen years who *walked* and now runs the refuge), the **sheltered** (a Faithless mother and three children),
  and **Justiciar Vane** (the career man at the door, who took Orla's old post).
- ЁЯЧЭя╕П **Hold it four ways, none of them a fight:** **rally the room** (Persuasion тАФ nat-20 *un-names the slur*, turning
  cowering prey into a proud congregation forty enforcers can't bear to drag off with their own men watching);
  **evacuate** down a warden's old river-drain (Investigation тАФ then stall Vane long enough to empty the room behind
  his own voice); expose the **writ as unlawful** (the forged Concord again тАФ a career Justiciar can't risk serving
  on a fraud); or **stand in the breach** as the [RETURNED] (the enforcers serve the Wall, and cannot drag a child
  past living proof that the Wall can be escaped тАФ their nerve breaks).
- ЁЯТФ **Vane is winnable, not beatable** тАФ the nat-20 persuasion makes him realize he replaced the warden who walked,
  and walks himself, six years late; lesser successes get a deferral or a legal withdrawal. The sheltered mother
  reads how you fought, names her baby for the cured bridge-boy, and gives the siege its stakes in four names.
- ЁЯСБя╕П **Three new Returned-senses.** ЁЯзк **+10 gates** (now **1,049 checks**, all green). **23 zones, 82 souls** тАФ six
  fresh structures this stretch (bargain, trial, heist, devil-pact, self-trial, siege), every one resolved by the
  saga's thesis: *witness, not force.*

## ЁЯСС v5.5.0 тАФ *"The Assize of the Returned"* тАФ a twenty-second zone: the trial flipped (you are the accused) (content)

> A fifth new structure, and an inversion of the Reckoning Court: there you *defended* a soul from the Wall; here
> **you stand in the dock yourself.** The dead you touched convene an assize to judge not a *crime* but your very
> *being* тАФ the charge that a soul which can walk back out of death is a hole in the one law that makes all the dead
> equal, and one unwatched century from becoming the tyrant. The whole trial reads your run.
- тЪЦя╕П **A twenty-second zone тАФ the Assize** (off the Grey Wayshrine). Three roles: the **Arbiter** (presides over a
  scale), the **Accuser** (speaks for the fear of you), and the **Witness** (the sum of every soul you touched).
- ЁЯЧгя╕П **You defend your existence**, and the defenses are gated on *how you actually played*: a **merciful** plea
  (your record of saved souls), an **honest** plea (you never lied about being a danger), calling the **Witness**,
  **bowing to the scale** (humility itself acquits тАФ the Crown never kneels), or тАФ the deepest beat тАФ **refusing the
  court's authority entirely**: a soul that insists on judging *itself*, every day, forever, can't be acquitted,
  and that permanent open question is the one lock the Crown has never picked. The merciful/honest pleas escalate to
  the forward question тАФ *what stops you becoming the Crown?* тАФ answerable three ways (never be alone with the
  choice; distrust your own certainty; or the unbeatable *"I don't know if I can be trusted"*).
- ЁЯкЮ **The Accuser is revealed (Insight) as your own fear** wearing a hood тАФ your inner prosecutor, given a stone to
  stand on. The lesson: don't *win* against it, *keep* it; the Last Returned fell not by losing this argument but by
  *evicting the arguer*. And it reads your party тАФ a soul that built a crew of no-sayers is the *variable its
  forecast can't price.*
- ЁЯСд **The Witness** is the gathered dead, its testimony reactive to a merciful vs ruthless run тАФ and the truest
  acquittal is letting your dead-touched sense *meet your own ledger without flinching* (the one test the Crown
  cannot pass).
- ЁЯСБя╕П **Three new Returned-senses.** ЁЯзк **+9 gates** (now **1,039 checks**, all green). **22 zones, 79 souls** тАФ five
  fresh structures this stretch (bargain, trial, heist, devil-pact, self-trial), all circling the Crown.

---

## ЁЯСС v5.4.0 тАФ *"The Advocate's Booth"* тАФ a twenty-first zone: a negotiation with a devil (read the fine print) (content)

> A fourth new structure тАФ the **devil's contract** тАФ and one that turns the Jergal bargain inside out. Where the
> dust at the crossroads wanted nothing and dealt fair, **Ma├оtre Crede, Advocate of the Nine Hells**, wants
> *everything* and hides it in the places he doesn't point. He's come because the Wall is a *loophole*: the Faithless
> go to neither heaven nor hell, so Hell is being cheated of its due тАФ and a contract-devil means to probate the
> largest unclaimed estate in the planes. The whole game is *reading.*
- тЪЦя╕П **A twenty-first zone тАФ the Advocate's Booth** (off the Night Market; built from the existing prop vocabulary).
  Three souls: the **devil-advocate**, a **bonded soul** mid-collection, and the advocate's **bound clerk.**
- ЁЯУЬ **A contract you read, not sign.** **Investigation** finds the trap (Clause the Ninth: the advocate-of-record
  becomes the *final entry* on his own manifest); **Insight** finds the real motive (the Faithless aren't the estate
  тАФ they're the *test case*: establish that *unowned means open* and every unclaimed soul in creation falls to Hell,
  with *you*, the un-fileable Returned, as the keystone precedent). The **[RETURNED]** reading *voids his whole
  estate* with the loophole he came to close тАФ *unowned means unownable, by Hell too; you can't sign over what was
  never owned.* And refusing is its own beat: he's not the villain, he's *the reasonable offer you were too proud
  to take*, and time is on the side of the Nine.
- ЁЯкд **The bonded soul** тАФ a father who bought his daughter sixty hale years with himself as collateral, re-sealing
  the debt every dawn out of love тАФ can be **witnessed to peace** (a debt agreed-to can't be picked, only re-framed)
  and gives the booth's true lesson: *a fair deal with Hell is still a deal with Hell; the trap isn't his paper, it's
  your own wanting.*
- ЁЯШИ **Sevenpence, the bound clerk** тАФ an imp four thousand years into a ninety-year sentence тАФ can be **freed**: his
  padded extension-clause never defined *whose* judgment rules a task complete, and a Returned has standing among the
  dead to declare it done. He also leaks the devil's one fear: being made a *signer* himself.
- ЁЯСБя╕П **Three new Returned-senses.** ЁЯзк **+7 gates** (now **1,030 checks**, all green). **21 zones, 76 souls** тАФ four
  fresh structures this stretch (bargain, trial, heist, devil-pact), all orbiting the one question: *what is a soul
  worth that no god ever claimed?*

---

## ЁЯСС v5.3.0 тАФ *"The Sparrow's Wing"* тАФ the fourth companion's arc completes (Threshold + epilogue) (content)

> The Sparrow gets the full companion treatment Sennet got тАФ but with a twist that's hers alone. She is *dead*,
> and so, unlike the living companions checked at the Threshold, **she is the one soul in your party who can follow
> you through the death-door.**

- ЁЯЪк **The Sparrow at the Threshold** (gated on `party.sparrow_recruited`). While Dace, Orin and Sennet are held at
  the edge by the breath still in their bodies, the dead thief simply *examines* the death-door like any other lock
  тАФ and she's the *exception* the door makes (a soul it already let out once is a Returned-shaped crack she can slip
  through in your shadow). A real fork: **take her through** (she comes not as a bodyguard but a *burglar* тАФ fades
  into the throne room and scouts your way *back out before you need it*, the first rule of the trade), or **have her
  hold the door** (you won't march a just-mended, unbought soul back into the one house with a cage for her name).
- ЁЯУЬ **Her years-after coda** (joining the epilogue's conditional souls). The dead don't age тАФ they *deepen* тАФ and
  the Sparrow turned the line you tossed her in the archive into a *life*: she **steals people back.** A whole crew,
  the **Sparrow's Wing**, picking the locks on the after's remaining cages тАФ no fee, no buyer, the freed soul its own
  reward. Four threads: the trade she built; why she stays instead of taking her earned rest (purpose over freedom);
  a **[RETURNED]** reckoning between two trespassers of death (she'll walk the good door at the last, *empty-handed,
  every cage picked clean behind her*); and the ones she was too late for (carried not as guilt but as instruction).
  A reactive opening reads whether she scouted the throne-room exit.
- ЁЯСБя╕П **Two new Returned-senses** тАФ the one party-member for whom the Threshold is a *workplace*, and the soul that
  changed its whole nature without losing its edge.
- ЁЯзк **+4 gates** (now **1,023 checks**, all green). The Sparrow now spans heist тЖТ fire тЖТ door тЖТ years-after, exactly
  like Sennet тАФ two complete four-beat companion arcs in the walkable saga. **73 souls.**

## ЁЯСС v5.2.0 тАФ *"The Sparrow"* тАФ a fourth recruitable companion, turned mid-heist (content)

> The heist's inside thief becomes the saga's fourth companion. The Sparrow took the Tally job for the coin and
> didn't look at the cargo тАФ but she has *one* rule, *no stealing people*, built around the one early crime she
> couldn't live having done twice. Show her the Great Tally *is* that crime ten thousand times over, and she turns
> herself off the job тАФ and you can take her on.

- ЁЯГП **The Sparrow is now recruitable (`party.sparrow_recruited`).** Two routes: the **[RETURNED]** path (name what
  she's really stealing and she turns and joins in one stroke), or тАФ once she *doubts* the job (ask about her buyer,
  or read her with Insight) тАФ a plain recruit offer: *steal people back instead of fencing them.* She joins on her
  own terms (picks the locks, keeps her cut of anything that isn't a person, and you never ask her to leave a soul
  behind a door she could've opened).
- ЁЯФе **She takes a seat at the Hearth fire** (joining Dace, Wren, Pip and Sennet among the conditional camp souls).
  A full fireside conversation with four threads: how a soul ends up a *thief of the dead*; the story behind her
  **one rule** (an early job, a child-shade she lifted for a buyer before she learned to ask *why* тАФ the wall she
  built around the one crime she couldn't repeat); a **[RETURNED]** "we both go where we're not allowed" exchange
  (you introduced the proud hands to the ashamed jobs, and she's a *whole person* for the first time in forty years);
  and whether she regrets walking away from the richest score of her life (she doesn't тАФ *you can't fence a seat at
  a fire; it's only worth anything given*). A reactive opening reads whether you delivered the Tally to Jergal.
- ЁЯСБя╕П **A new Returned-sense** for her at the fire: a soul caught in the act of *integration*, the two halves it kept
  in separate pockets for forty years finally settling into one.
- ЁЯзк **+3 gates** (now **1,019 checks**, all green). **Four companions** now тАФ Dace the sellsword, Sennet the
  cartographer, Orin the justiciar, and the Sparrow the reformed thief. **71 souls.**

---

## ЁЯСС v5.1.0 тАФ *"The Deep Archive"* тАФ a twentieth zone: a heist (steal the master ledger of the Faithless) (content)

> Another structure the saga hadn't done: a **heist** тАФ crew, obstacle, score. Down a darker stair from the
> Counting-House sleeps the **Great Tally**, the Choir's master ledger of *every* Faithless soul promised to the
> Wall тАФ ten thousand names in one black book. It's in an *unlocked* room, because the Choir never dreamed a soul
> would be fool enough to *want* it. You are exactly that fool.

- ЁЯжЕ **A twentieth zone тАФ the Deep Archive** (off the Counting-House; built from the existing prop vocabulary). The
  three pieces of a heist: a **crew** (the Sparrow, a professional thief already inside), an **obstacle** (Brother
  Codex, the soft night-watch), and the **score** (the Great Tally itself).
- ЁЯГП **The Sparrow тАФ a partner-or-rival fork.** A second-storey soul who took the job for the coin and didn't think
  about the cargo. Partner her (she fully intends to cross you тАФ and knows you know тАФ so it's an *honest*
  partnership), read her with **Insight** and drop the dance, or тАФ the best beat тАФ let the Returned tell her *what*
  she's actually stealing (ten thousand people, a slaver's manifest), and watch a thief with one unbreakable rule
  *turn herself* off the job.
- ЁЯЪк **The night-watch тАФ a four-approach obstacle**, each with its own skill and fork: **Deception** (pose as the
  Canon's auditor тАФ lands *harder* if you cracked Mereth upstairs, since the gossip of her crisis is real; nat-20
  has Codex *helping you carry the book out with airtight paperwork*; nat-1 has you call the Canon the wrong name),
  **Stealth** (slip past; nat-20 plants a draught to walk him the wrong way), a **[RETURNED]** turn (he's another
  unbought clerk like Pell тАФ make him the man who *guarded the door by failing to*), or **Intimidation** (cow him,
  or panic him into ringing the alarm).
- ЁЯУХ **The score is a genuine choice with genuine trade-offs:** **burn** the book (frees all at once тАФ but a list is
  also a *tether*, and the frailest, most un-witnessed souls *scatter* with no anchor); carry it to **Jergal** to be
  audited empty name by name (saves them *whole* тАФ gated on having met the dust at the crossroads); **cut out Venn's
  forged founding page** so the whole ledger rests on no lawful authority (gated on confirming the fraud тАФ the
  Sparrow's favourite, a one-page score that makes ten thousand worthless); a **[RETURNED]** option to *consult the
  ten thousand souls themselves* (they choose the patient mercy, the strong electing it for the frail); or grab-and-run
  if the alarm's already up. The Sparrow reacts to each.
- ЁЯСБя╕П **Three new Returned-senses**, including drowning in the book's *ten thousand held breaths.*
- ЁЯзк **+12 gates** (now **1,016 checks**, all green). **20 zones, 70 souls** тАФ and the saga's three new structures
  (god's bargain, courtroom, heist) all interlock through the one black book.

---

## ЁЯСС v5.0.0 тАФ *"The Bone Scrivener"* тАФ a nineteenth zone: a god's bargain (and the 1,000-check milestone) (content)

> A whole new *structure* тАФ the **god's bargain** тАФ and a reach deep into Realms lore for the broker. Off a dusty
> side-path from the Grey Wayshrine sits **Jergal**, the *First Lord of the Dead*: the being who held Kelemvor's
> office aeons before him, invented the very idea of a ledger of souls, and then grew so *bored* across eternity
> that he handed the whole grim portfolio to three hungry mortals and took a clerk's desk. He wants nothing, fears
> nothing, lacks nothing тАФ which makes him the one honest broker on the causeway, and his bargains the most
> dangerous kind: *fair.*

- тЬ╢ **A nineteenth zone тАФ the Bone Scrivener** (off the Wayshrine; built from the existing prop vocabulary). Three
  souls: the **broker** (Jergal), the **one deciding** (Goodman Harl, a father wavering over the price to save his
  godless daughter), and the **one who already paid** (a nameless wisp who gave up its own name to strike a child
  off the Wall, drifting un-grieving into the quiet).
- тЪЦя╕П **The bargain itself тАФ a structure, not a switch.** Jergal can *un-write* a soul from the Wall's rolls
  entirely тАФ not crack it, *erase* it тАФ but the book must sum to zero, so the credit is a piece of yourself, paid
  in a currency the ledger accepts: a **year** of your life (from the grey far end you'd never notice), a **memory**
  (the warmest you own тАФ heavier, so it balances a whole soul), or the heaviest coin, a **name** (a [RETURNED]
  beat: your *own*, the one the harvest already half-took тАФ finishing the Wall's theft yourself to rob it of the
  finishing). Each strikes a Faithless soul truly free.
- ЁЯзо **The clever path: out-account the inventor of accounting.** Learn that the ledger sums to zero and that *you*
  are a credit spent and returned тАФ money the universe owes itself тАФ and a **Persuasion** check lets you *assign*
  that standing debt instead of paying a new coin, striking the soul free for nothing but wit (gated on having
  learned the ledger-law; nat-20/nat-1). The **nat-20** escalates to the structure's biggest swing: the Wall is
  revealed as a *vault of uncollected debts*, and a delighted Jergal sets out to spend his eternity of tedium
  gleefully **auditing the whole thing empty.**
- ЁЯЪк **Refusing is its own honest path** тАФ name the bargain as the Wall's arithmetic in a politer robe, and Jergal
  (who'd *like* to be put out of work) tells you the real answer: don't buy souls off one year at a time, **empty
  the book of the lie at the throne.**
- ЁЯСБя╕П **Three new Returned-senses**, including reading a *god who set itself down* тАФ tedium worn into bedrock, the
  one being with no angle at all.
- ЁЯзк **+11 gates** тАФ and the headless suite crosses **1,004 checks**, all green. **19 zones, 67 souls.**

---

## ЁЯСС v4.99.0 тАФ *"Annet, Years On"* тАФ the Reckoning Court pays off in the epilogue (content)

> A side quest deserves a coda. Spare Goodwife Annet at the trial and, in **"Some Years After,"** you find her old
> and stubbornly above-ground тАФ a borrowed newborn asleep on her shoulder, a midwife's bag still slung across her,
> caught breech two dawns ago. She was *meant to be mortar.* Instead she got more years of the exact work they tried
> to damn her for.

- ЁЯС╢ **Annet's epilogue coda** (gated on `tr.annet_spared`, joining Wren, Pip and Sennet among the conditional
  years-after souls). **Three reactive openings keyed to *how* you won the trial:** the reeve's public recantation
  (`tr.reeve_recants` тАФ a thousand names nailed to the Counting-House door broke the quiet reckonings for good), the
  voided Concord (`tr.concord_void` тАФ the thorough prosecutor died at his desk un-writing the Wall's forged
  paperwork), or a default.
- ЁЯМ▒ **The payoff is the saga's thesis, made concrete.** She spent her reprieve *seeding the causeway*: hundreds more
  children caught, four godless girls trained to carry the work, and a whole generation walking around wearing names
  she chose тАФ each one a thank-you she couldn't say aloud to the stranger who vanished. A [RETURNED] exchange lets
  two godless souls settle the question the Wall was built to punish: *no god ever caught her тАФ a person did, and
  that's not the consolation prize, that's the whole sermon.*
- ЁЯСБя╕П **A new Returned-sense for her coda:** the dead-touched player reads not one saved midwife but a *lineage of
  catching* тАФ a single un-walled soul whose warmth propagates, the loudest answer in the tally to *what is a soul
  worth that no god ever claimed.*
- ЁЯзк **+2 gates** (now **995 checks**, all green): the coda is gated to sparing her and reads the specific way the
  reckoning broke. **64 souls** now walk the causeway.

---

## ЁЯСС v4.98.0 тАФ *"The Reckoning Court"* тАФ an eighteenth zone: a courtroom side quest (defend a soul from the Wall) (content)

> A structure the saga hadn't done yet: a **trial.** The Choir holds summary *reckonings* in a cellar under the
> Counting-House тАФ quiet, gallery-less, a form completed in the dark тАФ to condemn the Faithless to the Wall. Tonight
> the accused is **Goodwife Annet**, a godless midwife who caught half the Quarter's children across forty years,
> charged with the one-line crime of having *served no god.* You are the only gallery she gets. Be the trouble.

- тЪЦя╕П **An eighteenth zone тАФ the Reckoning Court** (down a new stair from the Counting-House; built from the existing
  prop vocabulary тАФ the big scale of judgement, a dock, the prosecutor's desk, banners and braziers). Three roles:
  the **accused**, the **prosecutor**, and the **reeve who pronounces.**
- ЁЯЧгя╕П **A real trial you argue, many ways.** Against **Brother Sevard** (a *thorough* man, not a cruel one тАФ he reads
  the deeds before the indictment and has filed eleven years of midwives behind a locked door): **Persuasion**
  (a tax on kindness тАФ nat-20 turns the Wall's own theology against it: walling the *witnessed* to dam the
  *unwitnessed* feeds the sea it's meant to hold back), **Insight** (the charge names a *state of being*, not an
  act), **Intimidation** (a mob of grateful mothers тАФ nat-20 threatens the one thing a clerk can't survive: a
  *public record*), and two **evidence-gated** decisive arguments that pay off the Counting-House climax тАФ the
  forged founding Concord (`ch.venn_confirmed`) and the High Measurer's cracked faith (`ch.mereth_cracked`).
- ЁЯСБя╕П **A [RETURNED] argument unique to you:** the only soul who ever walked back out of the Wall can give **sworn
  testimony** to what "forfeiture" actually does тАФ opening the closed door in the middle of the courtroom.
- ЁЯФи **A two-step verdict.** Sparing Annet collapses the prosecution first (`tr.annet_spared`); only *then* does the
  **Reeve Oddleif** acquittal unlock тАФ and he's a magistrate who sold his conscience for a warm room and a pension,
  whom you can move (Persuasion nat-20 makes him *count* how many of his thousand sentences were Annets) to recant
  every pronouncement and vacate the bench. Each role has nat-20/nat-1 forks, a [RETURNED] line, and a Returned-sense.
- ЁЯзк **+10 gates** (now **993 checks**, all green): the zone is keyed/reachable, the argument paths and crit/fumble
  forks are present, the evidence gates open only with the upstairs flags, the testimony path is Returned-only, and
  the acquittal is gated on the prosecution collapsing first. **18 zones, 63 souls.**

---

## ЁЯСС v4.97.0 тАФ *"Sennet, Years On"* тАФ the cartographer's arc completes in the epilogue (content)

> The third companion's thread now runs the full length of the saga: recruited at the **wagon**, warmed at the
> **fire**, held back from death's door at the **Threshold** тАФ and now paid off in **"Some Years After."** Save
> Sennet and, years on, you find an *old* soul at a proper table under the trees, grey-haired and impossibly alive,
> the first true atlas of the dead finished and clasped before them. It is the single clearest proof in the whole
> tally that the Wall's slow harvest can be *reversed*.

- ЁЯУЦ **Sennet's epilogue coda** (gated on `party.sennet_recruited`, joining Wren and Pip among the conditional
  years-after codas). Three reactive openings keyed to the arc: the **eyes-past-the-door** Threshold choice (you
  went *in* so they could stay on the warm shore and draw), the **devoted** nat-20 recruit (your name printed in
  the title cartouche, where it outlasts you both), and default.
- ЁЯЧ║я╕П **Four threads pay off:** the **atlas** itself (banned by the Choir, but a banned book in a *cracked* church is
  one everyone reads тАФ now chained in every temple of Kelemvor for the bereaved, so no soul who loses theirs has to
  read *"here be terrors"* on a blank page); **Tibb** (a master cartographer now, with his *own* frightened
  apprentice, who keeps the one-line letter pressed in the back of the atlas); the **cold** (a [RETURNED] beat тАФ the
  surveyor's frost *receded* where yours never can, so they drew you a true **map home** for the day your own road
  runs back to the grey country, pressed into the last page); and whether they were **glad** of the years (they were
  a soul racing its own death so it never had to sit still long enough to feel how alone it was тАФ you gave them
  *time enough to be happy, and the company to be happy with*).
- ЁЯСБя╕П **A new Returned-sense for the epilogue:** the dead-touched player reads a soul that was *measured for an edge
  and got a hearth instead* тАФ the Wall's harvest, run all the way to its end and *lost*.
- ЁЯзк **+2 gates** (now **983 checks**, all green): the coda is gated to recruitment, reads the Threshold choice, and
  pays off the atlas and the map-home. **60 souls** now walk the causeway тАФ and one of them grew old.

## ЁЯСС v4.96.0 тАФ *"Sennet at the Edge"* тАФ the cartographer follows you to the door the living can't cross (content)

> The saga's most pointed companion beat. Recruit Sennet and they follow you everywhere тАФ including to the
> **Threshold of the Crown's Road**, the lip of the deep country they've spent their whole life charting from a
> half-mile off through a shaking spyglass. And here is the cruelty the surveyor never budgeted for: the map runs
> *all the way to this line, and not one inch further*, because past it is the country of the dead, and they are
> still тАФ for the first time they have ever resented it тАФ *alive.* The one survey that matters is the one step
> their living feet cannot take.

- ЁЯЪк **Sennet appears at the Threshold** (gated on `party.sennet_recruited`, the conditional-NPC system already
  used for Dace and Orin at the edge). They stand an arm's length from the death-door, pen forgotten, white-knuckled
  тАФ because to a cartographer of the dead the open door is not a horror but the *last unmapped mile*, and every
  honed instinct says *step through.*
- ЁЯзн **A conversation about being held back from the thing you most want.** Reactive openings keyed to how you bonded
  (the fireside *baseline* talk, the *devoted* nat-20 recruit, or default). Four resolutions: **order them to stay**
  (they needed it to be a command, not a request тАФ so it isn't theirs to lose); **ask for the bearings** (the craft
  is the one floor that never gives way тАФ they steady instantly and chart your crossing, *count your steps, same
  number coming back*); a **[RETURNED] "be your eyes"** beat that turns *staying* into the job (a one-station
  baseline is just a man crying at a door); or **invoke Tibb** (*I'll mind the wagon till you're home* тАФ the one
  word that moves their feet off the edge).
- ЁЯСБя╕П **A new Returned-sense for the Threshold:** the player feels the deep country *pulling* at the living surveyor тАФ
  the least-defended soul imaginable against that drag тАФ and reads that they're in danger not of dying here but of
  *walking in on purpose, gladly, clear-headed.*
- ЁЯзк **+2 gates** (now **981 checks**, all green): Sennet is gated to the edge only when recruited, and the scene
  carries the hold-back path, the [RETURNED] eyes-beat, and the new sense. **59 souls** now walk the causeway.

## ЁЯСС v4.95.0 тАФ *"Sennet at the Fire"* тАФ the recruited cartographer joins the Hearth denouement (content)

> A companion you can recruit should *show up.* The Hearth already gathers exactly the souls you saved тАФ Dace
> off-watch, Wren with her apple, Pip sleeping with both eyes тАФ so the new third companion now takes the third
> chair at the fire, with a full reactive fireside conversation of their own.

- ЁЯФе **Sennet now appears at the Hearth** тАФ gated on `party.sennet_recruited`, using the existing conditional-NPC
  engine (`npcVisible`/`activeNpcs`/`blockedNow`). Recruit them at the wagon and they're at your fire that night;
  don't, and the chair stays empty.
- ЁЯЧ║я╕П **A fireside conversation that reads how you took them on.** Four reactive openings: a **devoted** variant if
  you recruited them with the nat-20 persuasion (they put your name on the title cartouche; now they're drawing
  *you*), a **merciful**-disposition variant, a wary **ruthless** one (the surveyor takes a bearing on *your* cold
  and tells you, plainly, what country it leads to), and a default. Talk-threads: what they're really drawing
  (the *camp*, each soul labelled тАФ the first map they've ever wanted to be *in*); the state of the frostbitten
  hand (the creeping cold has **stopped advancing** now they're off the edges тАФ Tibb's count of "two, maybe three"
  isn't two anymore); a Returned-tagged "two surveyors, one baseline" exchange; and whether they wrote to Tibb
  (they did тАФ and the lad wrote back one line).
- ЁЯСБя╕П **A new Returned-sense for Sennet at the fire** тАФ the dead-touched player *watches the Wall's cold recede
  from a soul for the first time*: you didn't just recruit a surveyor, you pulled one more off the long grey road.
- ЁЯзк **+2 gates** (now **979 checks**, all green): Sennet is correctly gated to appear only when recruited, and the
  fireside talk carries the devoted variant, a [RETURNED] line, and the new sense. **58 souls** at the causeway.
