## ЁЯСС v4.26.0 тАФ *"The Song, the Ledger, and the Hand That Stayed Down"* тАФ Crown Wars complete (Pillar 2)

> The founding finishes. The bard who is commanded to make the atrocity *beautiful* тАФ and so writes the
> first dirge in the world; the scribe whose stylus turns a man's spoken cruelty into a permanent fact and
> who insists "I only record"; and, on a hill above it all, the one judge who kept his hand down, exiled and
> erased, who has had ten thousand years to learn what forgiveness actually is.

- ЁЯПЫя╕П **Crown Wars Wave II** (`crownwars_denizens_2.dlg`) completes the origin era:
  - **Singer Lhoris** тАФ commissioned to score the faithless's last walk, and able to make ten thousand years
    of imprisonment sound like a blessing. The artist's complicity: beauty is a gift to the dying *and* an
    anesthetic for the killers, in the same notes. He can weave the victims' *names* into the melody so every
    future dirge is a hidden act of remembrance, or smuggle the truth in its bones down ten thousand years
    (`sq.the_first_dirge`, `act3.truth_smuggled_in_song`).
  - **The Scribe of the First Verdict** тАФ the unremarkable, dutiful woman whose clean hands are the *only*
    thing that makes the cruelty stick: the Wall isn't built of stone, it's built of her ledger, kept
    correctly. The ancestor of the Clerk of the Wall (#49), patient zero of "I only record" тАФ who can leave a
    margin, name the first Faithless in the template, and make the record carry its own refutation forever
    (`act3.wall_is_the_ledger`, `act3.scribe_refuses_inertia`, `sq.scribe_margin`).
  - **The Exile Who Forgave** тАФ the one judge who refused the vote, stripped of name and rank and erased from
    the record, who has sat ten thousand years on a hill above the Wall and learned the secret the whole road
    ahead requires: *forgiveness is never earned, only set down* тАФ a bridge you build alone and then wait on.
    The counterpoint to young Ilfaeril; he can come down off the hill to tell the boy there was another way
    (`act3.forgiveness_is_not_earned`, `act3.refusal_was_possible`, `act3.exile_may_return`).
- ЁЯз╡ **Theme**: how an atrocity is *finished* тАФ scored into beauty, recorded into permanence, and written into
  a story that says "there was no other way." Each NPC is the seed of a present-day counterpart (LhorisтЖТthe
  Drowned Choir, the ScribeтЖТthe Clerk of the Wall, the ExileтЖТIlfaeril's unaccepted forgiveness). The Crown
  Wars (#61тАУ66) are now **fully voiced**.
- ЁЯУИ **Content**: dialogue corpus now **150 conversations ┬╖ 929 nodes ┬╖ 119 skill checks** (up from
  147/905/116). All 606 headless CI checks green; the 22-file `.dlg` corpus compiles clean (zero broken refs,
  dup ids, or orphans) and the viewer regenerates byte-for-byte.

## ЁЯСС v4.25.0 тАФ *"The Day the Wall Was Built"* тАФ the Crown Wars origin (Pillar 2 keystone)

> The saga reaches its thematic floor: ~тИТ10,000 DR, the founding chamber where the Wall of the Faithless
> is *invented* тАФ not by a villain, but by a grieving, kind-eyed judge who calls it mercy; where the very
> first soul is sentenced before the word "Faithless" even has a meaning; and where a brilliant young elf
> named Ilfaeril raises his hand to vote yes, on the worst and most innocent day of a ten-thousand-year life.

- ЁЯПЫя╕П **The Crown Wars open** (`crownwars_denizens.dlg`) тАФ the origin of the central evil, shown as a
  committee of good intentions:
  - **Coronal Aedyn** тАФ the high judge who devised the Wall as *preservation* rather than annihilation, and
    genuinely cannot tell whether he's building a mercy or "the most patient cruelty in the history of the
    world." Confront him and the foundation shows: the Wall is a way to *never have to grieve* тАФ filing
    cheaper than weeping тАФ and *"a crown cannot choose mercy, because mercy is sometimes the refusal to rule"*
    (`act3.wall_born_of_mercy`, `act3.crown_cannot_grieve`, `act3.break_the_crown_known`).
  - **The First Faithless** тАФ *Maerys*, a soldier who drowned pulling a bad singer named Calla out of a river,
    standing in the first dock before the word "Faithless" has been given its terrible meaning. She kept every
    faith that mattered тАФ just not to a god тАФ and you can make the Wall *fail at its very first stone* by being
    the one witness who remembers her name (`act3.first_faithless_remembered`, `act3.died_for_a_song`).
  - **Ilfaeril, the Younger** тАФ your ancient, grief-hollowed companion as an *eighteen-year-old prodigy*,
    certain and clear-eyed and proud, an hour from casting his first vote. His airtight logic has one hole тАФ
    he's been *forbidden to ask the defendant* тАФ and you can send him to the dock, or tell him you've met his
    ten-thousand-year-older self still carrying the wound. The exact moment a companion's grief was born,
    happening live (`act3.ilfaeril_asks`, `act3.ilfaeril_hand_stays_down` / `act3.ilfaeril_raises_hand`).
- ЁЯз╡ **Theme (keystone)**: the Wall was not built by hatred but by *love exhausted past the strength to
  grieve*, and armored in a sincerity no later century dares question тАФ "the hardest evil to end is the one
  done in love." The first Faithless was never faithless; the Wall was a lie from its first stone; and the
  crown at the road's end is the office, not the answer.
- ЁЯУИ **Content**: dialogue corpus now **147 conversations ┬╖ 905 nodes ┬╖ 116 skill checks** (up from
  144/881/112). All 606 headless CI checks green; the 21-file `.dlg` corpus compiles clean (zero broken refs,
  dup ids, or orphans) and the viewer regenerates byte-for-byte.

## ЁЯСС v4.24.0 тАФ *"The Hand in the Margins"* тАФ Netheril complete + the loop's first thread (Pillar 1/2)

> The Seventh Enclave finishes falling тАФ and the mystery of who *you* are takes its first cold shape. A
> fishwife's daughter decides whether the lady she built is worth living in; a proctor recognizes your
> handwriting in a warning older than your grandfather; a slave wins a nineteen-year legal war one hour
> too late; and Naeve, the last daughter of a murdered house, assembles the indictment of her own father.

- ЁЯПЫя╕П **Netheril Wave II** (`netheril_denizens_2.dlg`) completes Act III's first era:
  - **Lady Sabbath of the Seventh** тАФ a fishwife's daughter who clawed up forty tiers and built a flawless
    aristocrat, now choosing whether to *die elegant* or *survive vulgar*; the truest elegance, it turns out,
    is outliving the audience that wanted you gone (`act3.sabbath_survives`).
  - **Proctor Ynn** тАФ eleven years studying a second hand in the margins of Karsus's Folly, a warning the
    magelords *read and ignored* тАФ and he knows *your* handwriting on sight. The first thread of the loop:
    someone with your exact tired script has been writing *"Stop. You do not need to be a god to be enough"*
    in the margins of catastrophes longer than you've been alive (`act3.returned_annotator`,
    `act3.loop_glimpsed`).
  - **The Bondsman** (Castian) тАФ collared at eleven, named after a dog, who spent nineteen years learning law
    and quietly engineered a clause that *inverted the bond* тАФ and discovers, an hour from the end, that he
    never wanted to *own* his master; he wanted to be *seen* (`act3.bondsman_freed_master`).
  - **Naeve** *(pre-recruit)* тАФ the Seventh Enclave's last daughter, building an indictment out of grief she
    won't let herself feel, proving the apocalypse was a *murder with signatures* тАФ including her father's,
    the man who once named her the stars. A companion who joins not to be saved but to give the indictment
    *legs* (`act3.naeve_will_join`, `act3.naeve_knows_annotator`).
- ЁЯз╡ **Theme / plot**: the through-line of the Wall meets the through-line of *you* тАФ the warning unheeded,
  the record that has no room for the part that hurts (that the guilty were *beautiful first*), and the dawning
  shape of the Returned as the one condemned to write *stop* in margins the powerful refuse to read.
  Netheril (#53тАУ60) is now **fully voiced**.
- ЁЯУИ **Content**: dialogue corpus now **144 conversations ┬╖ 881 nodes ┬╖ 112 skill checks** (up from
  140/848/107). All 606 headless CI checks green; the 20-file `.dlg` corpus compiles clean (zero broken refs,
  dup ids, or orphans) and the viewer regenerates byte-for-byte.

## ЁЯСС v4.23.0 тАФ *"The City That Fell Politely"* тАФ Act III opens: Netheril, тИТ339 DR (Pillar 2)

> Karsus reaches for godhood, the Weave begins to die, and the Seventh Enclave starts its long fall out
> of the sky. Four souls meet the apocalypse exactly in character: a steward who serves canap├йs as a
> *vigil*, a boy who could stop it and won't because no one ever asked his name, an engineer who lies
> beautifully to buy four hundred calm goodbyes, and the one "broken" child the dying Weave cannot touch.

- ЁЯПЫя╕П **Act III opens in Netheril** (`netheril_denizens.dlg`) тАФ the floating-city apocalypse, told from the
  inside:
  - **Steward Vael** keeps the last table of the Seventh Enclave as the floor cants three degrees тАФ not from
    denial but from *love*, the only grammar he was ever given; press him and the house-name falls away to
    *Corin*, the indentured boy who'd have kept *bees* (`act3.witnessed_fall`).
  - **Karsus's Apprentice** stands frozen at the sanctum door, able to end the apocalypse with one word and
    unable to, because the man casting it is *the only person who ever wanted him in the room.* Give him back
    his name тАФ *Eshe* тАФ or reframe obedience as loyalty to the *saner* master, and the door opens
    (`act3.apprentice_opens_door`).
  - **The Mythallar-Keeper** has told four hundred souls everything is *fine* for three hours тАФ mercy and
    cowardice wearing the same smile. A *third path* exists between the pretty lie and the panic: the quiet
    truth, told to the few who can act (`act3.keeper_quiet_truth`); behind her composure is Joss, the
    apprentice she sent to fetch a lens instead of home to his mother (`act3.find_joss`).
  - **The Weave-Deaf Child** тАФ *Sefris* тАФ sits perfectly calm while every arcanist bleeds from the ears,
    because the "defect" that made her worthless in a magocracy is the one thing the dying Weave can't reach.
    The broken girl found the way down: the non-magic cargo-gliders the lords were too proud to take
    (`act3.glider_escape`).
- ЁЯз╡ **Theme**: hubris ends an age, and the people who meet the end with grace are never the magelords тАФ
  they're the servant, the foundling, the liar choosing mercy, and the child a proud world threw away.
  The thing called *broken* was built, in secret, for the hour the world breaks.
- ЁЯУИ **Content**: dialogue corpus now **140 conversations ┬╖ 848 nodes ┬╖ 107 skill checks** (up from
  136/816/101). All 606 headless CI checks green; the 19-file `.dlg` corpus compiles clean (zero broken refs,
  dup ids, or orphans) and the viewer regenerates byte-for-byte.

## ЁЯСС v4.22.0 тАФ *"The One Who Came Before, and the Song That Won't Stop"* тАФ Candlekeep & the Fugue, complete (Pillar 2)

> The library's last secrets and the grey's most beautiful sorrow. The Returned who reached the crown
> and lost. The cat who has outlived every reader. A candle hunting a forbidden name, a furious girl who
> refuses to be your reason, a grief made into light, and three drowned voices holding eleven thousand
> names aloft by never falling silent.

- ЁЯУЪ **Candlekeep Wave III** (`candlekeep_denizens_3.dlg`) finishes the library: **the Sealed-Stacks
  Revenant** тАФ *a previous Returned*, walled into the lore for almost winning the *wrong* way, who reveals
  the crown at the road's end is the **trap, not the prize** (`act2.break_the_crown_known`), and spent forty
  years rewriting his own cautionary warning into a *map*; **the Cat Who Reads** (Margin) тАФ the one unjudged
  creature in Candlekeep, who guards the dangerous book not with claws but by *remembering every reader the
  books forgot* (Speak-with-Animals and Handle-Animal paths); and **Scrivener Pol** тАФ a terrified copyist
  whose sister's debt was paid months ago, who kept copying the sealed truth anyway and became a
  *whistleblower* without admitting it (`sq.pol_pages`, `act2.wall_provenance_pages`).
- тЪЦя╕П **The Fugue Plane, Wave II** (`fugue_denizens_2.dlg`) completes the grey: **Wickless** тАФ a candle-spirit
  lit at Hollowmere's festival "for the person we're not allowed to talk about," who didn't *forget* its
  forbidden name but *hid it from itself*, holding one walled soul a candle's-width into the light
  (`act2.forbidden_name_carried`); **Maerin** тАФ Aldric's daughter, fading and *furious*, who refuses to be
  flattened into anyone's grief and demands to be carried *sharp* тАФ cruel-over-a-carved-fish, unfair-to-walruses,
  recruitable as a companion who comes back to be *furious in person* (`sq.maerin_recruit`,
  `act2.maerin_will_return`); **the Mournlight** тАФ ten thousand forbidden mournings made into light, the
  **golden-path key** that can only be carried by hands holding a grief *they were never allowed to feel*
  (`act2.golden_path_key`); and **the Three Shades of a Drowned Choir** тАФ who discovered a name *sung* is a
  name the Wall *cannot file*, imprisoned eleven thousand names in a song they can never end, and learn the
  way out is not to sing *harder* but *wider* тАФ until the whole world sings the Faithless (`sq.spread_the_song`).
- ЁЯз╡ **Theme**: the crown is the office, not the answer тАФ you win by *breaking* it, not wearing it; a name
  *carried*, *sung*, or *grieved* is a name the Wall can't keep (`act2.cataloguing_defeats_the_wall` reinforced
  from three new directions). Candlekeep (#35тАУ44) and the Fugue Plane (#45тАУ52) are now **fully voiced**.
- ЁЯУИ **Content**: dialogue corpus now **136 conversations ┬╖ 816 nodes ┬╖ 101 skill checks** (up from
  129/759/90). All 606 headless CI checks green; the 18-file `.dlg` corpus compiles clean (zero broken refs,
  dup ids, or orphans) and the viewer regenerates byte-for-byte.

## ЁЯСС v4.21.0 тАФ *"The Margins and the Grey"* тАФ Candlekeep Wave II + the Fugue Plane opens (Pillar 2/3)

> The scholars who read *you* like a disputed passage тАФ and, beyond the last page, the grey afterlife
> where the dead stand in line and a clerk has been stamping FAITHLESS for ten thousand years on the
> authority of a god who quit.

- ЁЯУЪ **Candlekeep Wave II** (`candlekeep_denizens_2.dlg`): **Brother Tym the Indexer**, cross-referencing
  every soul in the Wall against the Catalogue of the Living and going mad *pleasantly* тАФ he'll set you on
  `sq.tym_index` when he notices the one name that appears in both; **Mistress Ekko, Tutor of Dead Languages**,
  who teaches you to read your own half-formed true name (it spells *"the one who returns"*) and weeps at the
  spelling; and **Magister Cole**, who is certain the Returned are a *textual error* and means to correct you тАФ
  until you turn the argument around and convince him the *Wall* is the unauthorized interpolation.
- тЪЦя╕П **The Fugue Plane opens** (`fugue_denizens.dlg`): **the Doorman of the Crystal Spire**, who sorts the
  freshly dead by faith and suffers a small crisis when *you* arrive breathing; **Petitioner 9,000,001**
  (Edwy, who sold pears), who has stood in line so long he has forgotten his own name тАФ the queue, he'll tell
  you, is "the Wall with better manners"; **the Last Honest Psychopomp**, a reaper quietly *hiding* forty-one
  fading Faithless souls instead of delivering them to the masonry; and **the Clerk of the Wall**, Jergal's
  abandoned subordinate, still stamping FAITHLESS out of pure inertia тАФ who lets slip that the Wall has **no
  author** at all, and hands you `sq.wall_ledger`.
- ЁЯз╡ **Theme deepened**: the Wall can only take what *nothing else has kept* тАФ so cataloguing, remembering, and
  naming defeat it (`act2.cataloguing_defeats_the_wall`); the Wall is an *agreement*, not a law
  (`act2.wall_is_agreement`), and an orphaned one (`act2.wall_has_no_author`). Reading your own name sets
  `act2.true_name_meaning`; converting Cole sets `act2.wall_is_the_corruption` / `act2.wall_unauthorized`.

## ЁЯСС v4.20.0 тАФ *"The Gate Filled, the Library Opened"* тАФ Wave IV + Candlekeep's scholars (Pillar 3/4)

> The Upper City's idle cruelty, the Docks' practical mercy, a corpse who cheats at dice тАФ and the first
> of Candlekeep's magnificent obsessives.

- ЁЯПЫя╕П **Wave IV finishes the Gilded Gate** (`gate_denizens_4.dlg`): **Duke Aldwin the Absent** (governs by
  committee so no decision is ever *his* тАФ and can be shamed into the first signature in years); **Ysolde de
  Lancie** (a bored patrician shopping for immortality, who can be sold a *use* instead); **Archivist Threnn**
  (keeps two ledgers тАФ the survivable lie for the patriars, the unbearable *true* count for the dead, because
  *someone* has to write the names down right); **Old Marrow** (a corpse who keeps coming up from Grud's
  graveyard to cheat gently at dice, staying square with a grieving friend the harvest can't take from him тАФ

  read everything, remembers all of it, and reads a single *blank page* for the only silence he has тАФ
  warns you the Crown speaks in your own voice); **Brother Faolan of Acquisitions** (will do anything for the
  *Catalogue of the Unwritten* тАФ because his own unwritten poems are in it); **Henwick the Misfiled** (a man
  catalogued *as a book* sixty years ago, now immortal and unharvestable тАФ the living key: *the Wall can only
  take what nothing else has kept*).

## ЁЯСС v4.19.0 тАФ *"The City, Crowded"* тАФ 12 more denizens (Waves IIтАУIII) (Pillar 3/4)

> More souls for the Gilded Gate. Comedy, menace, the companions' faces, and the men who ferry the dead.

- ЁЯОн **Twelve more fully-voiced NPCs** across two packs (`gate_denizens_2.dlg`, `gate_denizens_3.dlg`):
  **Hessa Dock-Eye** (the one-eyed smuggler running an underground railroad for the Faithless she'd deny to
  the gallows); **Father Brisk** (a Kelemvorite at the exact midpoint of Garrow's road, performing perfect
  empty rites); **Madame Eyes** (a fraud fortune-teller whose cards keep coming up *true* for you тАФ and keep
  repeating, because she's read you in other lives); **Pell the Honest Beggar** (who'll waste your coin on
  drink and says so); **Brindle Quillfeather** (a gnome whose useless "empathy detector" turns out to map the
  harvest); **the Twins Who Aren't** (two strangers who started with a con and grew a brother inside it);
  **Doctor Sallow** (a cowardly plague-doctor afraid not of the fever but of *failing*); **Wrenna Alleywind**
  (Roen's estranged Harper sister); **Quill** (Varra's devil тАФ a courteous broker secretly *rooting* for the
  collateral to beat him); **Justiciar Veld** (the church's true believer, defending a load-bearing wall:
  *if the Wall is wrong, he's a murderer with good penmanship*); **Senna the Glassblower's Widow** (rebuilding
  a memorial the church keeps smashing); **the Ferryman of Chionthar** (a Charon who learns the snare on the
  near bank is the *church's* addition, not the god's toll).
- ЁЯФБ Heavy reactivity: lines gate on `companion.roen.recruited` / `companion.varra.recruited` /
  `act1.fist_ally` / `prologue.garrow_doubt`, and seed companion- and faction-quest hooks (WrennaтЖФRoen,

  **73 skill checks**). Compiler-validated, no id/class collisions; suite holds at **606 checks**, all green.

## ЁЯСС v4.15.0 тАФ *"Words at Scale"* тАФ a dialogue compiler + the first banter flood (Pillar 3/4)

> The bottleneck on BG3-scale writing wasn't ideas тАФ it was that every conversation is verbose hand-C#.
> So: a DSL and a compiler, and the words start to pour.

- тЬНя╕П **`.dlg` тЖТ C# dialogue compiler** (`tools/dlg-compile.py`) тАФ author branching dialogue in a clean,
  readable DSL (`node:` / `* choice -> target`, `[INSIGHT 13]` skill checks, `?? fail`, `| if тАж`, `| fx
  appr.roen +5`), and it generates `Assets/Scripts/Content/<Name>.cs` in the **exact** pattern the runtime
  and `extract-dialogue.py` expect (regular escaped string literals, canonical field names). Writing in the
  DSL is ~5тАУ10├Ч faster than hand-C# and makes the story bible's existing scripts importable. The compiler
  **validates before it emits**: every choice/auto/start reference must resolve, no duplicate ids, no
  unreachable nodes тАФ authoring errors are caught headlessly, before Unity ever sees them.
- ЁЯТм **First content flood тАФ companion campfire banter** (`play/dialogue/campfire_banter.dlg`) тАФ **8 new
  two-hander conversations / 44 nodes**, on-voice for the whole cast (Garrow's grey mercy, Roen's honest
  dishonesty, Varra's infernal debt, Naeve's Netherese grief, Ilfaeril's ten-thousand-year weariness,
  Maerin's "a free gift from no one"), with Insight/Arcana/History/Persuade checks, approval shifts, and
  story-flag writes. The game's conversation total rises **52 тЖТ 60** (158 тЖТ **202 nodes**, 13 тЖТ **18 skill
  checks**), all live in the Dialogue Viewer.
- ЁЯзк **`dlg.test.js`** runs the real compiler against fixtures and pins the DSL contract (skill/ability
  mapping, `appr.`/`rep.`/`SET`/`CLEAR`/`>=` тЖТ the right `FlagClause`/`FlagOp`, fail branches, `END`,
  *regular* strings not verbatim) and that validation rejects dangling refs + duplicate ids тАФ **14 checks**.
  `dialogue_viewer.test.js` still green (20). Headless suite now **606 checks**, all green; the generated
  C# round-trips cleanly through `extract-dialogue.py`. *(The C# compile itself is verified on your machine.)*

## ЁЯСС v4.14.0 тАФ *"Hold the Thought"* тАФ Concentration (Pillar 1: the cost of a buff)

> 5e/BG3's quiet balancing rule: a buff isn't free тАФ keep it up only while you can keep your focus.

- ЁЯза **Concentration** in `play/crown_combat.html` тАФ **Mirror Image** is now a **concentration** spell. While
  Naeve sustains it (+4 AC), **any damage she takes forces a Constitution save** тАФ DC **10, or half the
  damage if higher** тАФ and on a failure the spell **drops**. Suddenly her glass-cannon screen is a thing you
  have to *protect*, not just cast: peel the foes off her, or watch the mirrors shatter. (The reaction it
  pairs with тАФ Shield тАФ can still save the hit outright, so the two interact exactly as in BG3.)
- ЁЯзк **`conc.test.js`** lifts the page's real `concentrationDC` / `concentrationHolds` and proves the DC rule
  across the rounding edges (1тЖТ10, 20тЖТ10, 21тЖТ10, 22тЖТ11, 40тЖТ20) and the hold/break comparison, plus the
  wiring (Mirror Image flagged `concentration`, damage triggers the save, a failed save strips the effect,
  no roll without damage) тАФ **15 checks**. The smoke run now **casts Mirror Image and tests concentration**
  across 400 games, **0 errors** (heroes win 60.5% тАФ Naeve spends the odd turn shielding herself, still in
  band). Headless suite now **592 checks**, all green.

## ЁЯСС v4.13.0 тАФ *"We Carried Each Other Out"* тАФ the Rescue deed (Pillar 1 ├Ч 3 ├Ч 4)

> The new downed system, threaded straight through the deed loop: pull a fallen comrade back and win, and
> the whole game remembers it тАФ in voice, in the Chronicle, in the ending.

- ЁЯдЭ **Rescue deed** тАФ reviving a downed ally *(v4.12.0)* and going on to win now earns **`deed.combat.rescue`**,
  which flows through the entire deed pipeline built across v4.7тАУv4.10 with no new plumbing: the **Chronicle**
  records it, a **deed-reactive victory bark** voices it (Garrow: *"We carried each other out. That is the only
  victory that has ever counted."* тАФ and a rescue is now the **most resonant** deed, spoken first), the Save
  Inspector's **Combat Chronicle** panel lists it, and the Endings Explorer gives it a **conduct line** *and* a
  **BG2-style epilogue slide**. *How* you held your party together follows you to the last page.
- ЁЯЧгя╕П **Revive bark** тАФ the moment you Help an ally up, a companion calls it (Garrow: *"On your feet тАФ I have you.
  Stay with me."*, Roen, Varra) тАФ a new `revive` bark beat, present-aware and rate-limited like the rest.
- ЁЯзк Verified across the existing suites rather than a new file: **`deeds.test.js`** (+ rescue earns/omits the flag,
  stacks to 5, labelled), **`deedbark.test.js`** (+ Garrow speaks it, first priority), **`barks.test.js`** (+ the
  `revive` beat exists and `reviveAlly` fires it), and the cross-page drift test still pins the new label across
  Combat тЖФ Save Inspector. Smoke still **400 games, 0 errors** (heroes win 73.0%). Headless suite now **577
  checks**, all green.

## ЁЯСС v4.12.0 тАФ *"Not Dead Yet"* тАФ Downed, death saves & Help (Pillar 1: the marquee mechanic)

> BG3's most-felt rule: a hero at 0 HP doesn't die тАФ they go **down, dying**, and the table holds its breath.

- ЁЯй╕ **Downed + death saves** in `play/crown_combat.html` тАФ when a hero drops to 0 HP they no longer die
  outright; they fall **unconscious and dying**, rolling a **death save** each turn (a pure d20: 10+ a
  success, under a failure, a **1** counts double, a **natural 20** snaps them back up at 1 HP). **Three
  successes** stabilises them (out of the fight but safe); **three failures** is death. Downed heroes still
  hold their tile (you can't walk through a body) and are drawn **prone and ghosted** with live **тЬУ/тЬЧ pips**.
- ЁЯдЭ **Help (revive)** тАФ a conscious hero standing beside a fallen ally can spend their action on the new
  **ЁЯдЭ Help** button to drag them **back up at 1 HP**. Real triage: save your friend, or press the attack?
- ЁЯТА **The loss condition is now BG3's** тАФ the party is defeated only when **every** hero is down or dead,
  not the instant one falls. A single hero can hold the line while the others fight to revive the fallen.
- ЁЯзк **`downed.test.js`** lifts the page's real `deathSaveStep` and proves every transition (success/
  failure/nat-1-double/nat-20-revive, the 3-success stabilise and 3-failure death, tally clamping, a
  missing tally), plus the wiring (heroes go down not dead, downed bodies occupy + render + take their
  save-turn, Help revives to 1 HP) тАФ **21 checks**. The smoke run now **goes down, rolls saves, and
  revives** across 400 games, **0 errors** (triage costs tempo, so heroes win **73.0%** тАФ still in band).
  Headless suite now **572 checks**, all green. (Barks test updated for the refactored death path.)

## ЁЯСС v4.11.0 тАФ *"Hold, or Loose"* тАФ per-reaction stances (Pillar 2: QoL)

> BG3 lets you set each reaction to ask or auto; here you can **arm or hold each reaction independently** тАФ
> keep your Shield up while you stop spending your turn on opportunity attacks.

- тЪФЁЯЫбЁЯМА **Per-reaction stances** in `play/crown_combat.html` тАФ the single тЪб Reactions switch is now a *master*
  over three independent stance toggles: **тЪФ OA**, **ЁЯЫб Shield**, **ЁЯМА Counter**. A reaction fires only if the
  master **and** that reaction's stance are on, so you can, say, hold your opportunity attacks (to bait a
  foe past you safely) while keeping Naeve's Shield and Counterspell armed. Stances persist across restarts,
  default to all-on (zero behaviour change out of the box), and dim when the master is off.
- ЁЯзк **`stance.test.js`** lifts the page's real `reactionAllowed` gate and proves a reaction needs **both**
  master and stance (master-off kills it, stance-off holds it, kinds are independent, unknown/missing inputs
  are safe), plus the wiring (the three gates consult their stance, the toolbar toggles, the re-render) тАФ
  **16 checks**. The Shield/Counter/QoL tests were updated to the new gate. Smoke still **400 games, 0
  errors** (default all-on). Headless suite now **551 checks**, all green.

> The deed loop's final mile: *how* you won a fight now echoes in the **epilogue the game writes for you**.

- тЪ░я╕ПЁЯХКя╕П **Deeds reach the ending** in `play/endings_explorer.html` тАФ the Endings Explorer now folds the combat

> The deeds don't just go in a ledger тАФ your companions *react* to them, in voice, the moment the fight ends.

- ЁЯЧгя╕П **Deed-reactive victory barks** in `play/crown_combat.html` тАФ the instant a battle is won, the companion
  who's standing speaks to *how* you won it: **Naeve** savours a **Counterspell** unwoven, **Roen** grins at a

  companion still alive can voice it. Fires right after the Chronicle records the deed, turning v4.7.0's

## ЁЯСС v4.7.0 тАФ *"The Chronicle Remembers"* тАФ Deeds in combat (Pillar 1 ├Ч 4: tactics feed the story)

> The superiority twist: BG3's combat is spectacular but *self-contained*. Here, **how** you win writes
> itself into the story.

- ЁЯУЬ **Deeds in combat** in `play/crown_combat.html` тАФ every victory is now appraised and recorded as
  **story flags** the wider game can read. Win without losing a hero тЖТ **flawless**; lose one тЖТ **hard-won**.
  Spare every foe (non-lethal) тЖТ **merciful**; give no quarter тЖТ **ruthless**. Cast a foe off the
  high-ground ledge to their death тЖТ **a ledge kill**; unravel the boss's spell with Counterspell тЖТ **the
  weave unwoven**. On victory the **Chronicle** narrates the deeds earned and writes them to
  `localStorage` as `coh.combat.deeds` тАФ the **reverse** of the flag bridge the combat already *reads*
  (`coh.combat.flags`), closing the Pillar 1 тЖФ 4 loop: the save shapes the barks, and now the fight
  shapes the save.
- ЁЯзк **`deeds.test.js`** lifts the page's real `deedFlags` mapping and proves a battle summary earns exactly
  the right flags (flawless xor hard-won; merciful/ruthless only on a pure finish; the ledge + counter
  deeds; **nothing** on a loss; up to four stacking on a clean sweep; every flag has a Chronicle label),
  plus the wiring (ledge-kill & countered-boss tracking, the summary counts, the `recordDeeds` call, the
  `coh.combat.deeds` write) тАФ **16 checks**. Smoke still **400 games, 0 errors**. Headless suite now
  **488 checks**, all green. (Tactics help documents deeds.)

## ЁЯСС v4.6.0 тАФ *"The Weave Unravels"* тАФ Counterspell (Pillar 1: reactions)

> Shield's offensive twin: don't survive the boss's spell тАФ *deny* it.

- ЁЯМА **Counterspell** in `play/crown_combat.html` тАФ **Naeve** gains the reaction's offensive half. When the
  boss **casts a spell** (its **Wail of the Returned**, now flagged `isSpell`), she can spend her reaction
  to **unravel it before it resolves** тАФ the spell **fizzles entirely**: no damage, no Frighten, nothing.
  It's a **once-per-battle** charge (a precious high-level slot), draws from the **same reaction** as Shield
  and opportunity attacks (so it's Counter *or* Shield *or* an OA that round), and is gated by the **тЪб
  Reactions** toggle. Together with Shield *(v4.5.0)* this is the working core of BG3's reaction system тАФ
  a defensive *and* an offensive reaction, sharing one honest economy.
- ЁЯзк **`counter.test.js`** lifts the page's real `canCounter` predicate and proves it triggers on exactly an
  enemy spell with a ready counterer (not a plain attack, not a friendly cast, not once the charge or the
  reaction is spent, not while down, not without the spell known), plus the wiring (the Wail's `isSpell`
  flag, Naeve's `knowsCounter`/`counterReady`, the `useAbility` intercept, the reaction+charge spend, the
  full fizzle) тАФ **15 checks**. The smoke run now **Counterspells across the 400-game auto-play**; still 0
  errors. Headless suite now **472 checks**, all green. (Tactics help + the Reactions toggle now list it.)
- тЪЦя╕П **Balance** тАФ making Counterspell a once-per-battle charge keeps heroes at **81.5%** win (an at-will
  counter that neutered the boss's only AoE spiked it to 89.8%).

## ЁЯСС v4.5.0 тАФ *"Not Today"* тАФ the Shield reaction (Pillar 1: reactions)

> BG3's defensive reaction, and the start of a real reaction UI: the blow that *would* have landedтАж doesn't.

- ЁЯЫб **Shield** in `play/crown_combat.html` тАФ **Naeve** gains the arcanist's classic reaction. When a foe's
  attack roll would land on her **by 4 or less**, she spends her **reaction** to raise a Shield for **+5
  AC** and turns the blow **fully aside** тАФ no damage, no rider. It never saves against a **crit** or a
  comfortable hit (you can't bluff a clean strike), fires **once per round**, and draws from the **same
  reaction** as opportunity attacks (Shield *or* an OA, not both), all gated by the existing **тЪб Reactions**
  toggle. The first defensive reaction тАФ the bones of BG3's full reaction UI.
- ЁЯзк **`shield.test.js`** lifts the page's real `shieldNegates` predicate and proves +5 AC turns aside
  exactly the hits it should (lands-by-0..4 yes; by-5, a comfortable hit, a miss, or any crit тЖТ no), plus
  the wiring (Naeve's `knowsShield`, the attack-roll/hero/`reacted`/`reactionsOn` gate, the clean early
  return) тАФ **15 checks**. The smoke run now **Shields across the 400-game auto-play**; still 0 errors.
  Headless suite now **457 checks**, all green. (Tactics help + the Reactions toggle now mention Shield.)

## ЁЯСС v4.4.0 тАФ *"The Long Way Down"* тАФ Shove off a ledge (Pillar 1: environmental kill)

> BG3's most-screenshotted moment: don't kill them тАФ let the *floor* do it.

- ЁЯки **Shove off a ledge** in `play/crown_combat.html` тАФ **Shove** now reads the terrain. Win the
  Strength contest while the foe is on the **high-ground mound** and you push them *off* it: instead of
  a one-pace nudge they **fall**, taking **2d6 per level of drop** and landing **Prone** (a new
  condition that grants attackers **advantage** next turn). A shove on level ground still just pushes
  them a pace, and shoving a foe **into** the high ground is never a fall тАФ the drop is measured, not
  assumed. This braids three earlier systems тАФ **Height** *(v3.89.0)*, **Shove** *(v3.87.0)*, and the
  surface-into-which-you-shove combo тАФ into one finisher.
- ЁЯзк **`ledge.test.js`** lifts the page's real height map and the marked `fallDrop` / `fallDamageAvg`
  helpers and proves a highтЖТlow shove registers a fall (drop 1), a level shove and a lowтЖТhigh shove do
  not, and the damage scales 2d6/level, plus the wiring (the Prone condition, the drop measurement, the
  2d6├Чdrop hit, the Prone application, the plummet log) тАФ **14 checks**. Smoke still **400 games, 0
  errors**. Headless suite now **442 checks**, all green. (Tactics help now documents the ledge kill
  and the throw.)

## ЁЯСС v4.3.0 тАФ *"A Flask, Well Thrown"* тАФ Throw (Pillar 1: ground-target utility)

> The BG3 zoning tool тАФ lob a flask where you *want* the fight to be, not just where a foe stands.

- ЁЯлЩ **Throw** in `play/crown_combat.html` тАФ Roen gains **Alchemist's Fire**, a thrown flask (a new
  `targeting:"throw"` ability kind). Arm it and every tile within **range 5** lights up **orange** тАФ
  click **any passable tile**, empty ground included, and the flask **vaults walls and units** to land
  there: it **bursts on every foe in the blast** (Dex save for half, 1d6 fire) **and seeds a fire
  surface**, igniting any oil/grease it touches. Unlike every prior surface ability тАФ which had to
  target a *foe* тАФ Throw lets you **pre-place a hazard** on empty ground a foe is about to cross.
- ЁЯзк **`throw.test.js`** lifts the page's real `inThrowRange` predicate and proves a flask reaches any
  tile in range (empty included) but never your own feet, plus the full wiring (the thrown ability,
  `doThrow`'s burst-via-`burstHits` + surface seed + re-check, the tile-target click path, the range
  highlight, label, and hint) тАФ **18 checks**. The smoke run now **throws a flask every game**; still
  **400 games, 0 errors**. Headless suite now **428 checks**, all green.

## ЁЯСС v4.2.0 тАФ *"The Netherese Hand"* тАФ an arcanist joins (Pillar 1 ├Ч 3: BG2 wizardry)

> The Infinity-Engine power fantasy: a glass-cannon mage who never misses, drops a fireball
> in a crowd, and steps behind a wall of mirror images. *Baldur's Gate II* in a single hero.

- ЁЯкД **Naeve, a Netherese arcanist** тАФ a 4th playable hero in `play/crown_combat.html` (INT 18, AC 13,
  22 HP, `spr_naeve` mage sprite). A true glass cannon with three classic spells, each a **new ability
  kind** in the engine:
  - тЬ╢ **Magic Missile** тАФ `autoHit`: a 3d4 **force** bolt that *never rolls to hit*. The forecast shows a
    flat **100% ┬╖ 7.5 dmg**, the BG2 reliability staple.
  - ЁЯФе **Fireball** тАФ `enemyburst`: target a tile and it **bursts through every foe in radius 1** (Dex save
    for half, 3d6 fire) **and leaves a fire surface** behind, chaining into the surface combos.
  - ЁЯкЮ **Mirror Image** тАФ `selfbuff`: weave it on yourself for **+4 AC for 3 rounds**, the duelist's screen.
- ЁЯзк **`bg2.test.js`** lifts the page's real `burstHits` and `autoHitDamage` helpers and proves a fireball
  hits exactly the live foes in radius (never allies, never corpses) and that never-miss damage is the
  exact expected value, plus full wiring of Naeve, the three spells, and the resolve/forecast/targeting/
  UI paths тАФ **24 checks**. Smoke still **400 games, 0 errors**. Headless suite now **410 checks**, all green.

## ЁЯСС v4.1.0 тАФ *"Leap of Faith"* тАФ Jump (Pillar 1: verticality)

> The BG3 traversal tool тАФ vault the pillar, clear the gap, get out of reach.

- ЁЯжШ **Jump** in `play/crown_combat.html` тАФ a new movement action (ЁЯжШ button / <kbd>J</kbd> hotkey):
  arm it and the leap-range tiles light up **cyan**; click a clear, passable tile within **range 3**
  and your hero **vaults over walls and units** to land there. It spends your move but **provokes no
  opportunity attack** (you're leaping away), and a clean landing is still **undoable**.

  range (vaulting whatever's between), never your own tile or out of range, plus the wiring (clear/

## ЁЯСС v3.99.0 тАФ *"Carry It In"* тАФ Save тЖТ Combat handoff (the crossover, made visible)

> v3.98 made the companions react to your flags. This lets you *see it*: load a save, watch them speak to that run.

- ЁЯФЧ **Save тЖТ Combat handoff** тАФ the **Save Inspector** gains an **"тЪФя╕П Open in Combat тЖТ"** button that
  stages the run's set flags into `localStorage["coh.combat.flags"]` and opens the Combat tab, which
  reads them on boot and feeds the **story-flag-reactive barks**. So a save with a Varra romance or a
  resolved quest *visibly* changes what your party says mid-fight тАФ the same localStorage bridge the
  Endings Explorer already uses.
- ЁЯзк `save_inspector.test.js` extended (now **19 checks**): the `toCombat` stager + button, and that the
  Combat page reads the *same* key and routes it into `pickFlagBark`. Headless suite now **373 checks**,
  all green (smoke still 400 games, 0 errors).
- ЁЯОп `docs/ROADMAP_BG3.md` тАФ the Pillar 3 ├Ч 4 crossover is now end-to-end and demonstrable.

## ЁЯСС v3.98.0 тАФ *"She Remembers"* тАФ story-flag-reactive barks (Pillar 3 ├Ч 4)

> The reactivity that out-reacts BG3: the *same* combat beat speaks differently depending on
> how your run has gone.

- ЁЯза **Story-flag-reactive barks** in `play/crown_combat.html` тАФ a companion's line now *changes with
  your run's `GameFlags`*: a **romance-aware** crit ("That one was for you, love"), a **quest-resolved**
  kill ("No fine print on that one"), a **left-the-faith** spare, an **NG+** wink ("We've done this
  beforeтАж skip the speech"). Flag-conditioned lines take priority over the generic ones; the run's
  flags are fed in via `localStorage["coh.combat.flags"]` (so a save's romance/quest state drives the
  voice), defaulting to the generic barks.
- ЁЯзк `barks.test.js` extended (now **23 checks**): the `pickFlagBark` rule тАФ a set flag with the speaker
  present yields the special line, nothing if the flag's unset or the speaker's absent, plus the

## ЁЯСС v3.91.0 тАФ *"Take It Back"* тАФ Undo Move (Pillar 2: Quality of Life begins)

> The first comfort BG3 players lean on constantly. No more fat-fingered, turn-ruining clicks.

- тЖй **Undo Move** in `play/crown_combat.html` тАФ a new action: take back the active hero's move and
  get the movement **refunded**, as long as the move **triggered nothing irreversible** (no surface
  effect applied, no opportunity attack provoked, and you survived). If a step into fire or out of a
  foe's reach happened, the move is *committed* (BG3-honest) and Undo greys out.
- ЁЯзк **`qol.test.js`** lifts the page's real `canUndoMove` predicate and proves a clean move is
  undoable while a dirty/lethal one isn't, plus the wiring (snapshot, dirtied-by-surface/OA, restore,
  cleared on act/turn) тАФ 10 checks. Smoke still **400 games, 0 errors**. Headless suite now **331
  checks**, all green.
- ЁЯОп First **Pillar 2 (Quality of Life)** entry on [the BG3 roadmap](docs/ROADMAP_BG3.md).

## ЁЯСС v3.90.0 тАФ *"No Free Retreat"* тАФ opportunity attacks & Disengage (Pillar 1 continues)

> Positioning gets teeth: you can't just walk away from a foe anymore.

- тЪФя╕П **Opportunity attacks** in `play/crown_combat.html` тАФ moving **out of an adjacent foe's reach**
  provokes a **free melee strike** from that foe (once per round, for *both* sides тАФ enemies provoke
  when fleeing too). Fully reprojected into the iso board with the lunge animation + combat log.
- ЁЯПГ **Disengage** тАФ a new action: spend it and your movement this turn **draws no opportunity
  attacks** (the tactical-retreat option). Reaction state resets at the start of each unit's turn.
- ЁЯзк **`opportunity.test.js`** lifts the page's real reach-test and proves OAs fire **only when
  leaving reach** (not when staying, shuffling, approaching, or passing by), plus the wiring
  (Disengage, once-per-round, turn reset) тАФ 11 checks. Smoke still auto-plays **400 games, 0 errors**,
  balance intact. Headless suite now **321 checks**, all green.
- ЁЯОп `docs/ROADMAP_BG3.md` тАФ opportunity attacks marked shipped.

## ЁЯСС v3.89.0 тАФ *"The High Ground"* тАФ height advantage (Pillar 1 continues)

> "I have the high ground." Now it actually matters.

- тЫ░я╕П **Height advantage** in `play/crown_combat.html` тАФ a contested **raised mound** in the middle of
  the arena. Striking from **higher ground grants advantage**; striking from **below, disadvantage**.
  Folded consistently into the hit math (`resolve`), the XCOM-style **forecast**, and the incoming-
  **threat** readout тАФ so the % you see already reflects the ground you're standing on. High tiles
  are gilded with a тЦ▓ marker, units **stand taller** on them, and the Selected panel flags *тЦ▓ high
  ground*.
- ЁЯзк **`height.test.js`** lifts the page's real elevation helpers and proves highтЖТadvantage,
  lowтЖТdisadvantage, levelтЖТneither, plus the wiring into hit math / forecast / view (9 checks). Smoke
  still auto-plays **400 games, 0 errors**, balance intact. Headless suite now **310 checks**, all green.

> The other combo every BG3 player learns: **water + lightning**. Soak them, then shock them.

- тЪб **Electrified water** in `play/crown_combat.html` тАФ Garrow's new **Hallowed Water** conjures a
  water surface (and douses fire); Varra's new **Storm Bolt** (lightning) **arcs through any water**

## ЁЯСС v3.87.0 тАФ *"Give Ground"* тАФ the Shove maneuver (Pillar 1 continues)

> The combo BG3 players reach for first: shove a foe **into your fire**, or **into a wall**.

- ЁЯл╖ **Shove** in `play/crown_combat.html` тАФ a universal action (its own button): a **Strength
  contest** (attacker STR vs the defender's best of STR/DEX) that pushes the foe **one tile
  directly away**. Push them onto a **hazard surface** and they suffer it (shove-into-fire = the
  BG3 environmental kill); push them into a **wall** and they take impact damage. Pairs directly
  with v3.86.0's surfaces.
- ЁЯзк **`shove.test.js`** lifts the page's real push-direction helper and proves it pushes a foe
  one tile away in **all 8 directions**, plus that the maneuver is wired (contest, shove-into-
  surface combo, wall impact, the UI button) тАФ 9 checks. The smoke harness still auto-plays full
  games with zero errors. Headless suite now **299 checks**, all green.

## ЁЯСС v3.86.0 тАФ *"The Battlefield Reacts"* тАФ environmental surfaces (toward "BG3 but superior")

> The first pillar of the [BG3 roadmap](docs/ROADMAP_BG3.md): BG3's signature combat feature,
> done our way. The ground itself is now a weapon.

- ЁЯФе **Environmental surfaces** in `play/crown_combat.html` тАФ lay **oil** (Roen's *Oil Flask*),
  then **ignite** it (Garrow's *Firebrand*): fire **spreads** through grease tile-to-tile,
  **burns** anyone standing in it (Burning DoT), and **water douses** it. Surfaces (fire / grease /
  poison / ice / water) apply on enter and at the start of each turn, spread & decay per round,
  and are rendered as animated tiles with their own flickering torch-glow on the iso board.
- ЁЯзк **`surfaces.test.js`** lifts the page's *real* surface logic and proves the combos:
  greaseтЖТfire ignition, fire spread, water dousing, decay, and in-bounds safety (11 checks). The
  smoke harness auto-plays **400 full games** through it with zero errors and balance intact.
  Headless suite now **290 checks**, all green.
- ЁЯОп **`docs/ROADMAP_BG3.md`** тАФ the honest plan for "similar to BG3 but superior in QoL, plot,
  characters & gameplay mechanics": what we build here vs. what needs Unity/art/budget, shipped
  one verified pillar increment at a time.

## ЁЯСС v3.85.0 тАФ *"In Motion"* тАФ the figures fight, not just stand

> The isometric board was still a diorama. Now the sprites *move*: they turn to face
> their foe, lunge when they strike, recoil when struck, and breathe at rest.

- ЁЯд║ **Attack choreography** in `play/crown_combat.html` (procedural, no new frames):
  - **Lunge** тАФ a striker eases toward its target along the iso vector and back
  - **Recoil** тАФ the struck figure jolts away from the blow
  - **Facing** тАФ each sprite flips horizontally to face whoever it's fighting
  - **Idle breathing** тАФ every living figure has a gentle, phase-offset bob so the board
    is never frozen (a little stronger on the active hero)
- All driven off the existing turn flow + frame clock; the engine, forecasts, conditions,
  VFX and lighting are untouched.
- ЁЯзк `iso.test.js` now also asserts the choreography is wired (lunge/recoil/facing/breathing);
  the smoke harness still auto-plays full games through the animated `draw()`. Headless suite
  now **279 checks**, all green. Preview + bundle rebuilt.

## ЁЯСС v3.84.0 тАФ *"The Tilt"* тАФ the playable board goes isometric

> The genre's defining look. The Skirmish stops being top-down and becomes a real
> **isometric crypt** тАФ diamond grid, raised stone walls, depth-sorted sprites.

- ЁЯзн **Isometric renderer** in `play/crown_combat.html` тАФ a 2:1 diamond projection: floor
  tiles are stone diamonds, **walls are extruded 3-D blocks**, and everything (walls, units,
  props) is **depth-sorted back-to-front** so nearer things correctly occlude. The combat
  logic stays on the square grid untouched; only the view + mouse-picking are reprojected.
- ЁЯЧ┐ **Environmental props** dress the crypt тАФ real CC0 feature tiles (a dark altar behind the
  boss, flanking statues, a sealed door) as billboards.
- ЁЯй╕ **Persistent decals** тАФ blood/scorch is left on the tile where each combatant falls.
- тЬи The whole juice layer (projectiles, impacts, slashes, crit bursts, torch lighting,
  death wisps, idle-bob) is reprojected into iso. All rules/forecasts/SFX unchanged.
- ЁЯзк **`iso.test.js`** lifts the page's real projection math and proves click-picking
  round-trips for **all 140 tiles** (centres + interior samples), that the projection is
  injective and in-bounds тАФ objective coverage for the one thing a screenshot can't show.
  `cc0_art.test.js` updated; the smoke harness still auto-plays full games through the iso
  `draw()`. Headless suite now **278 checks**, all green. Preview + bundle rebuilt.

## ЁЯСС v3.83.0 тАФ *"The Quickening"* тАФ the combat comes alive (VFX), real art everywhere

> "PLEASE DO MORE." Done: the fight stops being static. Bolts fly, steel sparks, the
> screen kicks, torches breathe тАФ and the Bestiary now wears the same real sprites.

- тЬи **Combat juice** in `play/crown_combat.html` (pure-canvas, no assets, works in the bundle):
  - **Projectiles** streak attacker тЖТ target for ranged/spell hits, with an **impact burst** on
    arrival; **slash arcs** for melee; **crit bursts** with radial sparks.
  - **Screen shake** on hits, harder on crits and kills; **death wisps** rise from the slain
    (fitting, for the Returned).
  - **Dynamic torch lighting** тАФ warm pools follow the heroes, cold necrotic glow the Returned,
    with a living **flicker**; the active hero gives a gentle **idle-bob**.
  - Damage-typed colours (fire/cold/radiant/necrotic/forceтАж); every rule, forecast & SFX
    unchanged.
- тШа **Bestiary now uses the real monster art** тАФ `tools/make-compendium.py` matches **35/37 foes**
  to the same DCSS sprites the board uses (keyword map, token fallback for the rest).
- ЁЯЫбя╕П Render path stayed headless-safe (the smoke harness auto-plays full games through the new
  `draw()` every run); `cc0_art.test.js` now gates the VFX/lighting/shake wiring. Suite **270 checks**,
  all green. Preview refreshed (`play/combat_preview.png`), hub + bundle rebuilt.

## ЁЯСС v3.81.0 тАФ *"One File"* тАФ the whole game in a single portable HTML

> "Can you give me a functioning HTML of all of this, including dialog trees?" тАФ yes:
> **`play/crown_of_horns.html`**, one self-contained file, no server and no other files.

- ЁЯУж **`play/crown_of_horns.html`** (~1.1 MB) тАФ a tabbed shell that bundles all nine browser
  pages and renders each in an isolated `<iframe srcdoc>` so their scripts/styles never
  collide: **Combat** (the real playable engine), **Dialogue** (every branching tree, Map +
  Walk), **Endings**, **Compendium** (Grimoire/Bestiary/Conditions/Codex/Atlas), **Cast**,
  **Flag Graph**, **Saga Map**, **Save Inspector**, **Analytics**.
- ЁЯФЧ In-bundle cross-links are rewired to switch tabs and carry the deep-link hash тАФ the Saga
  Map's "ЁЯТм conversation" chips jump straight to that conversation in the Dialogue tab, etc.
  The bundle is itself deep-linkable: `crown_of_horns.html#dialogue:ilfaeril.quest.resolution`.
- ЁЯз░ `tools/make-all-in-one.py` regenerates it from the standalone pages (JSON-embedded, lazy
  srcdoc load).
- ЁЯзк `all_in_one.test.js` (14 checks: all 9 pages embedded & parse, marquee payloads intact,
  shell + rewiring + deep-links wired) added to CI. Headless suite now **263 checks**, all green.
- ЁЯПа Hub gains a prominent button to the single-file build.

## ЁЯСС v3.78.0 тАФ *"The Wiring"* тАФ the whole saga's flag graph, browsable

> The narrative engine runs on one `GameFlags` brain. This release renders that brain: a
> dependency graph of every story flag тАФ what sets it, what gates on it тАФ harvested from
> three independent sources and merged.

- ЁЯХ╕я╕П **Flag Dependency Graph** (`play/flags_explorer.html`) тАФ pick any of the **167 story flags**
  to see a bipartite map of what **writes** it (dialogue choices, quest resolutions, deeds, era
  content) and what **reads** it (ending gates, codex unlocks, dialogue conditions), each edge
  colour-coded by source. An **overview** panel surfaces the 27 domains, the most-connected *hub
  flags*, and the orphans тАФ **write-only** (set but ungated: future headroom) and **read-only**
  (gated on but set by runtime systems like combat/losses/rests).
- ЁЯз░ `tools/extract-flags.py` merges three harvests: **C# `GameFlags` calls** (GetBool/GetInt = read,
  Set/AddInt = write) across `Assets/Scripts`, the **dialogue clause data** (`FlagClause`
  conditions/effects), and the **codex unlock flags** тАФ into `play/flags-data.json`
  (**515 read/write edges**). `tools/make-flags-explorer.py` renders the page.
- ЁЯзк `flags_explorer.test.js` (19 checks, incl. a parse-only JS compile and the marquee
  ending-gate тЖТ Endings+codex dependency). Headless suite now **210 checks**, all green.

## ЁЯСС v3.76.0 тАФ *"The Conversation"* тАФ every branch, mapped and playable

- ЁЯТм **Dialogue Tree Viewer** (`play/dialogue_viewer.html`) тАФ every conversation in the game as an
  auto-laid-out node-link graph: speakers, choice edges, **skill-check edges** (ability + DC, with the
  fail branch drawn dashed), and the story flags each line sets. Click any node for its full line and
  effects. Toggle to **Walk** mode and play the conversation тАФ pick choices, roll the checks, and watch

  (nodes / choices / `FlagClause` conditions+effects / `checkAbility`+`checkDC`+`failNodeId`) into
  `play/dialogue-data.json`. Reactive witness lines whose text is computed from flags are *marked*,
  not invented. `tools/make-dialogue-viewer.py` renders the page.
- ЁЯУК Coverage: **52 conversations ┬╖ 158 nodes ┬╖ 147 choices ┬╖ 13 skill checks**, straight from the source.

  page) added to CI. Headless suite now **180 checks**, all green.

  pads, click-free (whole-cycle partials), no melody to grate.

## ЁЯСС v3.69.0 тАФ *"Every Step Optimal"* тАФ A* pathfinding, proven least-cost

> The grid A* that moves every unit тАФ hub click-to-move and tactical combat alike тАФ is now proven not
> just *correct* but *optimal*: cross-checked against a brute-force Dijkstra oracle over 3,000 random
> weighted maps, so it can never quietly return a longer-than-necessary route.

- ЁЯзн **A* optimality pinned** тАФ `play/pathfind.js` ports `Pathfinding.cs` 1:1 (4-connected, `moveCost`-
  weighted, Manhattan heuristic, step-onto-occupied-goal-but-never-through-bodies) and ships a Dijkstra
  oracle. `pathfind.test.js` (8 checks): straight line, wall detour, unreachable, unwalkable/occupied
  goal, difficult-terrain preference, `start==goal`, **plus a 3,000-map fuzz asserting A* cost == the
  Dijkstra optimum** (and agreement on unreachability). The fuzz caught an edge case on its first run.
- ЁЯзк Headless verification suite now **139 checks** + the 400-game smoke, all green.

## ЁЯСС v3.68.0 тАФ *"Quests Kept"* тАФ the campaign spine, pinned headless

> Quest progression is the spine of the campaign, and its trickiest behaviour тАФ objectives that complete
> the instant a flag flips, completion vs. *failure* precedence when both land at once тАФ lived only in
> PlayMode, where this repo's CI can't reach. That reactive brain is now pinned in fast headless CI.

- ЁЯзн **Quest state machine pinned** тАФ `play/quests.js` + `quests.test.js` (15 checks, CI-gated) model
  `QuestManager`/`Quest`: explicit start (once), objectives that fire only when *their* flag flips true
  while Active, `completionFlag` тЖТ Completed, `failureFlag` тЖТ Failed, **failure beats completion when both
  are true** (the C# checks failure first and `continue`s), Active-only reactions, quest isolation, and
  export тЖТ import across managers (the save path).
- ЁЯзк Headless verification suite now **131 checks** + the 400-game smoke, all green.

## ЁЯСС v3.67.0 тАФ *"The Save Holds"* тАФ pinning the serialization contract

> The least glamorous, most important kind of test: proof that your 20-hour run survives a save/load.
> `SaveSystem` flattens the story brain (GameFlags) into the parallel key/value lists JsonUtility needs;
> a one-element desync there would silently corrupt every save. That contract is now nailed down.

- ЁЯТ╛ **Save round-trip pinned** тАФ `play/save.js` + `save.test.js` (CI-gated): `GameFlags тЖТ flattened
  DTO тЖТ JSON тЖТ back` is lossless across empty state, both bool values, int edges (`0`, `┬▒2┬│┬╣`), 250
  keys with **key/value-list lockstep assertions**, dotted/spaced/unicode keys, re-save freshness, and
  double-round-trip stability. Plus 3 on-disk `SaveSystemTests` (re-save overwrites not stacks, a
  200-flag round-trip, int edge values).
- ЁЯзк Headless verification suite now **116 checks** + the 400-game smoke, all green.

## ЁЯСС v3.66.0 тАФ *"The Odds Against"* тАФ threat forecasts, asset tooling, and the state of the game

> The forecast learns to look both ways: alongside "what are my odds of killing it," the HUD can now
> answer **"what are the odds it kills *me*?"** тАФ exact incoming damage and down-chance from every foe
> in reach, computed by convolving real damage distributions, not guessed. Plus the operational answer
> to "what do I need to ship this?": an asset-completeness checker and an evidence-based report.

- ЁЯЫбя╕П **Threat forecasts** (`ThreatForecast`): mean incoming damage and the true probability the target
  drops this round (miss/crit/save-for-half all modeled). Pinned by `ThreatForecastTests` with a
  40k-seed Monte-Carlo cross-check against the real resolver, mirrored in `play/threat.js` (CI-gated),
  and live in the playable demo ("тЪа incoming ~14 ┬╖ 38% down").
- ЁЯз░ **`tools/asset-check.sh`**: scans `Resources/` against the exact names the engine loads and reports
  what's present vs missing per category тАФ run it after dropping in any pack.
- ЁЯЧ║я╕П **`docs/STATE_OF_THE_GAME.md`**: a full flow audit found the game **complete in code** (23/23
  systems wired, zero stubs, boot тЖТ creation тЖТ hub тЖТ quests тЖТ combat тЖТ 5 eras тЖТ 6 endings); the real
  remaining gaps are a human Unity run, audio+VFX (0%), and a distributable build.

## ЁЯСС v3.65.0 тАФ *"The Odds Made Plain"* тАФ Unity 6.4, the verified slice, and combat forecasts

> The engine moves to **Unity 6000.4.9f1**, the codebase gets its first full audit, and the game
> learns to tell you the truth before you swing: an **XCOM-style forecast** тАФ hit %, crit %, expected
> damage, kill % тАФ on every target, computed from the same math the dice roll. Alongside it, the
> combat and narrative cores now run **outside Unity** in a browser-playable slice, pinned by 100+
> ported tests so nothing can drift silently again.

- ЁЯОп **Attack forecasts** (`AttackForecast`): analytic hit/crit/damage/lethal preview mirroring
  `AttackResolver` exactly тАФ proven by a Monte-Carlo cross-check (40k seeded rolls per matchup) in
  `AttackForecastTests`. Toggleable via the new `ShowHitChance` setting.
- ЁЯОЫя╕П **QoL settings**: `ShowHitChance`, `ConfirmEndTurn`, `AutoEndTurn`, `AutosaveEnabled` (the
  campaign autosave now respects it), and `ScreenShake` тАФ PlayerPrefs-persisted like the rest.
- ЁЯзн **Unity 6.4 migration**: every deprecated lookup replaced (`FindAnyObjectByType`, no-arg
  `FindObjectsByType`, `GetInstanceID` dropped), both `CS0252` reference-comparison warnings fixed,
  `ProjectVersion.txt` тЖТ 6000.4.9f1 so CI tests on the engine the project ships on.
- ЁЯй║ **The audit**: `CampaignBootstrap` no longer leaks its `OnFlagChanged` handler across
  defeat-restarts (zombie handlers could recruit stale companions into a new run); one-shot
  handlers in `EncounterBuilder`/`PrologueBootstrap`; `BreachDemo` unsubscribes too.
- тЪЦя╕П **Balance canary retuned**: the reference Brute (Str 16, HP 34) brings the oracle into its own
  design bands тАФ **Hero 70% [OK] ┬╖ Duelist 53% [OK]** (was 95/89 HIGH/HIGH).
- ЁЯХ╣я╕П **`play/` тАФ the verified slice**: a browser-playable skirmish (Garrow, Roen, Varra vs the
  Returned) on a seed-faithful port of the combat rules, plus ports of endings, epilogue,
  inventory, and progression. **104 ported checks**, a prose-parity gate, a 500-playthrough fuzz,
  and a 400-game DOM smoke тАФ wired into a new `combat-slice` CI workflow that re-runs whenever
  `Assets/Scripts/**` changes.
- ЁЯзк **Epilogue coverage**: `EpilogueTests` (17 tests) pins the BG2-style payoff тАФ slide gating,
  quest-outcome priorities, loved-and-lost, the anchor rule, the Chronicle.

## ЁЯСС v3.64.2 тАФ *"The Skull Still Choosing"* тАФ Aldric's fate, named at the forge

> The third cross-era callback, and the tightest loop in the saga: the **Time of Troubles** is the year
> Myrkul dies and his skull is beaten into the **Crown of Horns** тАФ the very relic the gentle heretic
> **Aldric Morn** carries on his shelf in Act I. A new echo at that forge names what *you* saw of Aldric
> over tea, and turns it into a warning about the thing inside the crown.

- тЪТя╕П **A Keeper of the Bone Crown** (second echo in the Time of Troubles) reads your Act-I read of Aldric
  back to you, most-specific-first:
  - **Sensed the Crown using him** (`aldric.crown_doubt_planted`): "you caught the leash for what it was тАФ
    do not unsee it."
  - **Named him a monster** (`aldric.named_monster`): "hate the relic, not the hand it chose for being kind."
  - **Saw the grieving father** (`aldric.grief_seen`): "love the size of his is the *door* the Crown was built
    to walk through."
  - **Made him say the count** (`aldric.cost_revealed`): "the crown keeps a *different* ledgerтАж the line where
    the price is *him.*"
  - **Merely met him** (`aldric.met`): "the hammer here and the whisper there are the same throat."
  - **Never met him**: pure foreshadow тАФ "a gentle hand will be offered this very crown and told it is a *means.*"
- ЁЯз▒ **Reusable plumbing:** `SimpleEra` now supports a **second independent echo slot** (`echoGraph2` /
  `echoLabel2`), so any era can name more than one upstream thread. The Spellplague can pick up a second echo
  later for free.
- ЁЯЫбя╕П **Validated + tested:** the new graph is registered in `ContentValidator` (`era.echo_toot_crown`) and
  `EraEchoesTests` grows to **16 tests** (every branch + priority ordering). **29 suites ┬╖ ~201 tests.**
  Structural check green (165 C# files).

---

## ЁЯХпя╕П v3.64.1 тАФ *"The Pulled and the Paid"* тАФ the Breach, named downstream

> A direct extension of v3.64.0's cross-era callbacks: the single heaviest choice in the game тАФ the
> **Breach** at the Wall of the Faithless тАФ now echoes in the late eras, the same way the Crown Wars
> Verdict does. Also closes a reactivity gap: *walking away* from the Wall was previously invisible.

- тЪЦя╕П **The Breach echoes forward.** Both late-era figures (the Time of Troubles **gravedigger** and the
  Spellplague **half-unmade soul**) now layer a third conditional thread on top of the Verdict + Netheril
  ones, keyed to what you did at the Wall:
  - **Pulled Maerin free** (`fugue.pull_maerin`): named as a *trade-death* тАФ "the Wall never gives without
    takingтАж carry them both, the pulled and the paid."
  - **Walked away** (`fugue.left_maerin`): named as counted restraint тАФ "you did the arithmetic out loudтАж
    it deserves a marker," and the soul that *would have been the cost* thanks you for it.
- ЁЯй╣ **Closed a reactivity gap (ROADMAP Tier 3 "every major choice leaves a trace"):** declining to pull
  Maerin set **no flag** before тАФ the restraint was unwitnessed. It now sets `fugue.left_maerin`, so the
  choice is reactable (and is, immediately, by both echoes).
- ЁЯЫбя╕П **Tests:** `EraEchoesTests` grows to **10 tests** (added pulled/left/neither coverage for both eras).
  **29 suites ┬╖ ~195 tests.** Structural check green (165 C# files).

---

## тП│ v3.64.0 тАФ *"The Source Remembers"* тАФ Cross-Era Callbacks (the time-travel earns its keep)

> *A choice in -10,000 DR, spoken aloud in 1385 DR.* The saga's whole conceit is that you walk the
> hinge-points of history тАФ so a verdict at the source should be **named** downstream, with its cost
> made visible. ROADMAP Tier 3 ("no choice forgotten") / DESIGN pillar V. **The last open Tier-3
> reactivity item lands.**

- ЁЯкж **New `EraEchoes` content** тАФ the *world itself* (not a companion) reacting to an upstream choice:
  - **Time of Troubles (1358 DR):** a **grey gravedigger** working the godless dead while the gods bleed
    speaks the **Crown Wars Verdict** back to you. Argue the damnation *down* (`crownwars.verdict_spared`)
    and the unclaimed get a resting-place "because of that single afternoon тАФ the Wall was only ever a
    wall, never a furnace." Let it *pass* (`crownwars.verdict_passed`) and "the source remembers, even
    when the river forgets."
  - **Spellplague (1385 DR):** a **half-unmade soul** in the blue fire тАФ held together only by being
    *witnessed* тАФ thanks you (spared) or forgives you (passed) for that same verdict, ten thousand years on.
  - Both echoes append a **second thread** if you witnessed **Netheril's fall** (`netheril.cleared/arrived`)
    тАФ the soot of the first apocalypse, the returned shades who "fell once before."
- ЁЯзй **Reusable wiring:** `SimpleEra.echoGraph` (+`echoLabel`) places the beat as a Talk marker, mirroring
  the existing `witnessGraph` pattern; `CampaignBootstrap` wires both late eras. Built **live from the
  flags**, with a graceful neutral fallback if you witnessed neither upstream era.
- ЁЯЫбя╕П **CI-guarded:** both echo graphs registered in `ContentValidator` (broken-reference gate) and a new
  **`EraEchoesTests`** EditMode suite (**8 tests**) locks each branch тАФ spared / passed / default /
  Netheril-thread тАФ so the no-compiler sandbox still guards the reactivity. **29 suites ┬╖ ~193 tests.**
- ЁЯЯв Structural check green (**165 C# files**). Roadmap Tier 3 reactivity is now complete.

## ЁЯОи v3.63.0 тАФ *"Status & Ledger"* тАФ Condition Icons + Asset License Ledger (ASSETS)

- тШая╕П Added a **12-icon status-effect set** mapped **1:1 to the `Condition` enum** (poisoned, prone,
  stunned, incapacitated, restrained, blinded, frightened, charmed, burning, blessed, hasted, slowed)
  тЖТ `Assets/Art/Sprites/Status/game-icons/`, named to the enum for direct wiring. CC BY 3.0,
  attributed in `ATTRIBUTIONS.md` (game-icons set now **57** icons total).
- ЁЯУТ Added **`UNITYASSETS.MD`** тАФ an asset **license ledger & buy-later shopping list**: what's already
  in the repo (free, $0) vs. a curated, priced list of **paid** packs to license before launch
  (~$340 art/audio). Documents the legal "test in-editor under your account now, license before
  launch" workflow тАФ **paid/unlicensed assets are NOT committed** (infringement, esp. on a public repo).
- ЁЯЯв No code change; structural check green.

  instead of shooting point-blank тАФ proper kiting that makes archers and casters play like archers and
  casters (and yes, it provokes an opportunity attack, just like it would for you). `EncounterController.FindRetreatCell`.
- ЁЯЯв 134 scripts / ~19.7k LOC, all clean. (Phase B: smarter enemy AI тАФ kiting)

## ЁЯЫб v2.51.0 тАФ *"Take Cover"* тАФ Half-Cover for Ranged Attacks (CODE)

- ЁЯЫб **Cover** тАФ a ranged attack against a target with another creature directly between it and the shooter
  (along an orthogonal or perfectly diagonal line) is made against **+2 AC** (half cover), with a *"COVER"*
  pop on a resulting miss. Deterministic aligned-line check (`AbilityRunner.HasRangedCover`), folded into
  `AttackResolver` via a `targetAcBonus`. Positioning now matters for archers and casters too. Phase B cover тЬЕ.
- ЁЯЯв 134 scripts / ~19.2k LOC, all clean.

- ЁЯза An enemy that **can't reach any target** on its turn and is **below 35% HP** now takes a defensive Dodge
  (attacks against it have disadvantage until its next turn) instead of idling тАФ making a fleeing, wounded
  foe harder to finish when you can't close the gap either. Uses the dodge stance directly (does *not* trip
  the player's "Master Tactician" tracking). `EncounterController.RunEnemyTurn`.

  healing consumable from the party stash onto the active unit, spending the action. `PlayerCombatInput.TryQuaff`.

  Disengage/Shove/Quaff + opportunity attacks + flanking + round tracking + AoE-aware, focus-fire enemy AI +

## ЁЯки v1.87.0 тАФ *"Shove"* тАФ The Shove Action (CODE)

- ЁЯки **Shove action** тАФ spend your action (key **V**, or the new HUD *"ЁЯки Shove"* button), then click an
  adjacent enemy: a **contested Strength check** pushes them one tile directly back if the space behind them
  is open. `TurnManager.TryShove` (uses `GridUnit.PlaceAt`). Battlefield control тАФ break a flank, open a
  lane, or shove a foe off a wounded ally. Pairs with opportunity attacks and flanking.
- ЁЯЯв 131 scripts / ~17.5k LOC, all clean. (Phase B: action variety тАФ Shove)

## ЁЯОп v1.84.0 тАФ *"Mind the Cluster"* тАФ AoE-Aware Enemy Targeting (CODE)

- ЁЯОп **Enemy casters now aim area attacks smartly** тАФ when an enemy's chosen ability is an `AreaBurst`, it
  centers the blast on the reachable party member whose tile catches the **most** of your party (tiebreak
  by proximity), instead of just hitting the nearest/weakest single target. Clumping up against a Fireball-
  toting foe now actually punishes you. `EncounterController.ChooseTarget`.
- ЁЯЯв 131 scripts / ~17.4k LOC, all clean. (Phase B: smarter enemy AI тАФ AoE avoidance pressure)

## тЪУ v1.81.0 тАФ *"The Waterfront"* тАФ The Chionthar Docks (CONTENT)

- тЪУ **A third explorable Lower City room** тАФ `DocksScene`, the Chionthar Docks: a reputation-reactive
  dockhand (smuggling offer at high standing, cold shoulder at low), a wary smuggler who warms if you

  bury. Wired into `BaldursGateHub` (`onEnterDocks`) + `CampaignBootstrap.EnterDocks`. The district keeps
  growing navigable.
- ЁЯЯв 131 scripts / ~17.4k LOC, all clean. (Phase C: multi-room Lower City)

---

## ЁЯй╣ v1.80.0 тАФ *"Clean Slate"* тАФ Reset Combat-Transient State Each Encounter (FIX)

- ЁЯй╣ **Bugfix:** the new per-combat flags (Dodge / Disengage / Help-advantage / last-reaction-round) lived
  on the `CharacterSheet` and weren't cleared between fights, so e.g. a unit that used its reaction in round
  1 of one battle could be denied its round-1 opportunity attack in the *next* battle. `TurnManager.StartCombat`
  now resets all four for every participant. Each encounter starts genuinely clean.
- ЁЯЯв 130 scripts / ~17.3k LOC, all clean.

---

## тЬЕ v1.79.0 тАФ *"Trust, but Verify"* тАФ Validator Covers Abilities/Classes/Camp Content (CODE)

- тЬЕ **`ContentValidator` extended** to sanity-check more data-only content: every ability (AreaBurst has a
  radius, heals have heal dice, no negative slot/range), every class's per-level kit resolves with no null
  entries, and camp **banters** / **night-talks** have unique ids/keys, both speakers, and non-empty lines.
  Catches the bug class the sandbox can't (no Unity compiler) тАФ `ValidationDemo` reports PASS/FAIL on Play.
- ЁЯЯв 130 scripts / ~17.3k LOC, all clean.

---

## ЁЯУЦ v1.78.0 тАФ *"A Growing Spellbook"* тАФ Per-Level Class Kits (CONTENT + CODE)

- ЁЯУЦ **Classes now grow as they level.** `startingAbilities` was already a per-level unlock list but each
  class had only one entry; now every class has a curated kit that unlocks with level:
  - **Fighter:** Longsword тЖТ Second Wind (bonus-action self-heal) тЖТ Javelin тЖТ Greataxe
  - **Wizard:** Fire Bolt тЖТ Ray of Frost (slows) тЖТ Thunderwave (Con-save burst) тЖТ Fireball
  - **Cleric:** Mace тЖТ Cure Wounds тЖТ Bless тЖТ Guiding Bolt тЖТ Sacred Flame
  - **Rogue:** Dagger тЖТ Shortbow тЖТ Shortsword ┬╖ **Ranger:** Shortbow тЖТ Dagger тЖТ Longsword ┬╖ **Barbarian:** Greataxe тЖТ Javelin
- тЮХ New abilities (Second Wind, Ray of Frost, Sacred Flame, Guiding Bolt, Healing Word, Thunderwave,
  Javelin, Shortsword) and a **Slowed** status. Leveling up now meaningfully changes your options.
- ЁЯЯв 130 scripts / ~17.3k LOC, all clean. (Phase B: more abilities/spells)

## ЁЯз╣ v1.77.0 тАФ *"Tidy Bar"* тАФ Combat HUD Action Button Layout Fix (CODE)

- ЁЯз╣ **HUD layout fix** тАФ the four new action buttons (Defend/Dash/Help/Disengage) were overlapping the
  bottom-centered ability bar; they now stack in a clean right-edge column above End Turn. No behavior
  change, just readability.
- ЁЯЯв 130 scripts / ~17.2k LOC, all clean.

---

## тЖФ v1.76.0 тАФ *"Flanked"* тАФ Flanking Advantage (CODE)

- тЖФ **Flanking** (optional 5e rule) тАФ a melee attacker gets **advantage** when an ally stands on the tile
  directly opposite them across the target. Pure positional check (`AbilityRunner.IsFlankingMelee`), folded
  into `AttackResolver` via an `extraAdvantage` input and logged with a *"is flanked!"* note. Rewards
  pincering a foe тАФ and pairs with the new opportunity-attack / positioning layer.
- ЁЯЯв 130 scripts / ~17.2k LOC, all clean. (Phase B: cover & flanking)

---

## ЁЯе╛ v1.75.0 тАФ *"Disengage"* тАФ The Disengage Action (CODE)

- ЁЯе╛ **Disengage action** тАФ spend your action (key **X**, or the new HUD *"ЁЯе╛ Disengage"* button) so your
  movement this turn provokes **no opportunity attacks**. `TurnManager.TryDisengage()` тЖТ
  `CharacterSheet.IsDisengaging` (cleared at your next turn start, honoured by `Reactions`). Makes the new
  opportunity-attack layer something you can play around тАФ the action economy now has a real retreat option.
- ЁЯЯв 130 scripts / ~17.2k LOC, all clean. (Phase B: action variety тАФ Dodge/Dash/Help/Disengage complete)

---

## тЪб v1.74.0 тАФ *"Don't Turn Your Back"* тАФ Opportunity Attacks (CODE)

- тЪб **Opportunity attacks** тАФ leave an adversary's melee reach (move from an adjacent tile to a non-adjacent
  one) without Disengaging, and that adversary spends its **reaction** (one per round) to make a free melee
  strike. New `Reactions.OnMoveCompleted`, hooked into both player and enemy movement; resolved via the new
  `AbilityRunner.ApplyOne` (which bypasses the action economy). `CharacterSheet.lastReactionRound` /
  `IsDisengaging` track the rules. Positioning suddenly matters.
- ЁЯЯв 130 scripts / ~17.2k LOC, all clean. (Phase B: reactions)

---

## ЁЯМА v1.73.0 тАФ *"D├йj├а Vu"* тАФ A New-Game+ Camp Moment (CONTENT)

- ЁЯМА **New-Game+ night-talk** тАФ on a fresh run after finishing the saga (`ng.plus`), Naeve тАФ the woman who
  will one day become the Lady in the Margins тАФ gets an uncanny fireside moment: she feels the loop turn
  under her, *"I have run this proof before."* Ties the New-Game+ system to the story's deepest twist.
- ЁЯЯв 129 scripts / ~17.1k LOC, all clean.

## ЁЯФв v1.72.0 тАФ *"Round Count"* тАФ Combat Round Tracking (CODE)

- ЁЯФв **Round counter** тАФ `TurnManager.RoundNumber` increments each time the initiative order wraps; logged
  at each round boundary and shown in the combat HUD's initiative header. Readability groundwork for
  duration/reaction features (status durations are already round-based).
- ЁЯЯв 129 scripts / ~17.1k LOC, all clean.

---

## ЁЯдЭ v1.71.0 тАФ *"Help"* тАФ The Help Action (CODE)

- ЁЯдЭ **Help action** тАФ spend your action (key **T**, or the new HUD *"ЁЯдЭ Help"* button), then click an
  adjacent ally: their **next attack roll is made with advantage**. `CharacterSheet.HasHelpAdvantage`
  (consumed on the recipient's next attack-roll ability), `TurnManager.TryHelp()`, help-targeting mode in
  `PlayerCombatInput` (Esc cancels). Completes the Dodge/Dash/Help action trio.
- ЁЯЯв 129 scripts / ~17.1k LOC, all clean. (Phase B: action variety)

## тПй v1.69.0 тАФ *"Pacing"* тАФ Combat Speed Setting (CODE)

- тПй **Combat speed slider** (0.5├ЧтАУ2.5├Ч) in Options, persisted via PlayerPrefs тАФ scales how quickly enemy
  turns play out (`GameSettings.CombatDelay`, applied to `EncounterController`'s turn pacing). For players

## ЁЯза v1.68.0 тАФ *"Focus Fire"* тАФ Smarter Enemy Targeting (CODE)

- ЁЯза **Enemy AI target selection** тАФ instead of always charging the *nearest* hero, enemies now focus-fire
  the **lowest-HP foe they can actually reach and strike this turn** (finishing kills, concentrating
  damage), breaking ties by proximity; they fall back to closing on the nearest only when nothing is in
  reach. `EncounterController.ChooseTarget`. Combat reads sharper and punishes leaving a wounded unit exposed.
- ЁЯЯв 129 scripts / ~17.0k LOC, all clean. (Phase B: smarter enemy AI)

## ЁЯТи v1.67.0 тАФ *"Dash"* тАФ The Dash Action (CODE)

- ЁЯТи **Dash action** тАФ spend your action (key **F**, or the new HUD *"ЁЯТи Dash"* button) for extra movement
  equal to your speed this turn. `TurnManager.TryDash()`, surfaced in the combat HUD + Help (H) overlay.
  Builds on the Dodge action's economy pattern (Phase B: action variety).
- ЁЯЯв 129 scripts / ~17.0k LOC, all clean.

  Return to Title) on its own root object, instead of stranding you on a dead battlefield.

  after a win тАФ permanent loss stays reserved for the Breach.

## ЁЯЫб v1.65.0 тАФ *"Defend"* тАФ The Dodge Action (CODE)

- ЁЯЫб **Dodge / Defend action** тАФ spend your action (key **G**, or the new HUD *"ЁЯЫб Defend"* button) and
  attack rolls against you are made at **disadvantage** until your next turn. Implemented as
  `CharacterSheet.IsDodging` (cleared at the dodger's next turn start), `TurnManager.TryDodge()`, factored
  into `AttackResolver`'s advantage math, and surfaced in the combat HUD + Help (H) overlay.
- ЁЯЯв 128 scripts / ~16.9k LOC, all clean. (ROADMAP near-term item #2 тЬЕ)

## ЁЯХпя╕П v1.30.0 тАФ *"The Almshouse of the Unclaimed"* тАФ A Second Explorable Lower City Room (CODE)

  builders), reached by a hub door once the prologue's cleared. Three reactive beats, all read live from
  the flags each entry:

    doubt, the widow's true comfort, the allies pledge, high standing), wary if you took Vane's cut.

    child pulled behind a skirt, or a fevered hope you caused by speaking for the Unmade).

    in a child's hand: *"MA, WHO SANG."* The whole argument of the game, written by people who never
    heard your name.

  (`almshouse.token`); it earns a dedicated **`EndingResolver`** slide and a Chronicle line тАФ the poor get

  **+4 approval** with Garrow and Ilfaeril (you stopped a martyrdom before it started).

## ЁЯзо v1.28.0 тАФ *"Front to Back"* тАФ Isometric Depth Sorting for Sprites (CODE)

> A small correctness fix that makes the v1.22 sprite seam actually *look* right: when art is present,
> units now layer by depth instead of fighting over who's drawn on top.

- ЁЯзо **`IsoDepthSorter`** тАФ added to each skinned unit's sprite; sets `SpriteRenderer.sortingOrder =
  -(x+y)*100` from world position every `LateUpdate`, so a unit lower/nearer on the iso diamond draws in
  front, and the order updates correctly as units move.
- ЁЯФМ Wired automatically by `UnitSpriteSkinner` (no extra setup); pure no-op until art exists.
- ЁЯУД `docs/ASSET_INTEGRATION.md`: unit-sprite row + checklist now note the live skinner + depth sort.
- ЁЯЯв 114 scripts / ~15.2k LOC, all clean. Drop in sprites and the battlefield reads with real depth.

## ЁЯФК v1.27.0 тАФ *"Give It a Sound"* тАФ The Audio Seam (SFX + Music) (CODE)

> The last sense the game was missing. Same philosophy as the sprite, portrait, and VFX seams: silent
> until you drop a clip in a folder, then it *just plays.*

- ЁЯФК **`AudioSystem`** тАФ one-shot **SFX** from `Resources/SFX/` and looping **music** from
  `Resources/Music/`, self-bootstrapping a hidden persistent driver, no-op when a clip is missing. Master
  volume already rides `AudioListener.volume` (set from the Options slider), so it's governed for free.
- тЪФя╕П **Combat sound** тАФ `AbilityRunner` plays **impact SFX by damage type** (`hit_fire`, `hit_ice`, тАж,
  falling back to `hit`), plus `heal` and `miss` тАФ right beside the floating numbers and hit VFX.
- ЁЯО╡ **Music per mode** тАФ the director's single `SwapMode` chokepoint swaps the loop by mode: **Hub,
  Combat, Camp, Fugue, Court, Vault, Explore**. A mode with no track keeps the current music rather than
  cutting to silence.
- ЁЯУД `docs/ASSET_INTEGRATION.md`: SFX & Music rows moved to **LIVE**, with the exact clip names.
- ЁЯЯв 114 scripts / ~15.1k LOC, all clean. Drop a folder of audio and the cube-game has a soundtrack.

> The art seam reaches conversations. Every line of the game already flows through one dialogue box тАФ
> now that box can wear a face the instant you give it one.

  (full speaker name тЖТ first word тЖТ the unit's map sprite), cached, returning null when no art exists.

  with a graceful skill-fail branch and **two outcome-gated aftermath NPCs** (an empty table vs. a busy one).
