## ЁЯзк v1.23.0 тАФ *"Trust, but Verify"* тАФ A Content-Integrity Validator (CODE)

> The sandbox has no Unity compiler, so the one bug class that can slip through is a mistyped node id in
> a conversation. This closes that gap: a smoke test that proves every dialogue link resolves.

- ЁЯзк **`ContentValidator`** тАФ walks every reachable authored `DialogueGraph` (all five personal quests via
  their `PersonalQuest` graphs, the three Act II side quests + crier + aftermaths, Aldric's tea, the
  Lady's two riddles) and reports **broken `nextNodeId`/`failNodeId`/`autoNextNodeId`/`startNodeId`,
  duplicate node ids, and empty/no-node graphs** тАФ each with the exact graph + node.
- тЦ╢я╕П **`ValidationDemo`** тАФ one-click: runs it on Play and prints a **PASS/FAIL** report to the Console
  *and* on-screen (graph count, node count, every issue). Run it after editing dialogue.
- ЁЯЯв 113 scripts / ~14.6k LOC, all clean. The authored narrative now has a regression net.

---

## ЁЯОи v1.22.0 тАФ *"The Art Seam"* тАФ Cubes Become Sprites the Moment Art Arrives (CODE)

> The cleanest possible on-ramp from "systems made visible" to "looks like a game": you don't touch a
> line of logic тАФ you drop a PNG in a folder.

- ЁЯОи **`UnitSpriteSkinner`** (on the campaign director) scans `GridUnit`s and, when `WorldArt` finds a
  matching sprite in `Resources/Sprites/`, **hides the placeholder cube and parents a camera-facing
  sprite billboard** (a new `CameraBillboard`) тАФ keeping the collider so selection still works. No art
  present тЖТ no change (graceful, exactly like the VFX system).
- ЁЯЧВя╕П **Sensible lookup** тАФ full display name тЖТ first word тЖТ faction, so **one `Sprites/Enemy.png`
  re-skins every foe at once**, while `Sprites/Garrow.png` upgrades her alone. No per-unit wiring.
- ЁЯУД Updated `docs/ASSET_INTEGRATION.md` тАФ ┬з2 goes from "PLANNED" to **"HOOK READY"** with the exact
  drop-in convention.
- ЁЯЯв 111 scripts / ~14.4k LOC, all clean. The seam between code and art is now a single folder.

## ЁЯФв v1.21.0 тАФ *"Numbers That Fly"* тАФ Floating Combat Text (CODE)

> The natural partner to the nameplates: now you don't just see *who's* hurt, you see the hit land.

- ЁЯФв **`FloatingCombatText`** тАФ damage numbers, **+heals** (green), **MISS/RESIST** (grey), oversized
  golden **crits**, and condition names pop off the target, drift upward, and fade, with a cheap shadow
  for legibility. Self-bootstraps a hidden driver on first use; pure IMGUI, world-space, zero art.
- ЁЯОп **Emitted at the source of truth** тАФ `AbilityRunner` fires the right popup straight off the resolved
  `AttackResult` (after difficulty scaling), so it's correct everywhere combat happens: campaign, eras,
  demos. No per-encounter wiring.
- ЁЯЯв 110 scripts / ~14.3k LOC, all clean. With v1.20's nameplates, a cube-fight now reads at a glance.

## ЁЯкз v1.20.0 тАФ *"Faces in the Fray"* тАФ World-Space Nameplates & HP Bars (CODE)

> The biggest *visible* upgrade yet, and a pure win for previewing in Unity: the colored cubes stop being
> anonymous. Now you can read a fight at a glance.

- ЁЯкз **`UnitNameplates`** тАФ a floating **name + faction-colored HP bar** over every `GridUnit`, projected
  to screen each frame, with the **active combatant highlighted** (gold тЦ╢ + outlined bar) and downed units
  greyed as "(down)". HP bar shades green тЖТ amber тЖТ red as it drops. Toggle with **N**.
- ЁЯФМ **Wired in where it matters** тАФ added to the persistent campaign director (covers hub, combat, eras,
  every mode) and to `DemoBootstrap` (the flagship combat demo). Drop-in for any scene; it finds units itself.
- тЭФ Added to the **Help** card and controls legend.
- ЁЯЯв 109 scripts / ~14.2k LOC, all clean. The systems-made-visible game just became *readable* at a glance.

## тЪФя╕П v1.19.0 тАФ *"Knocked Out, Not Dead"* тАФ Combat Consequences & a Breathing Bond (CODE)

> The last open roadmap item тАФ approval that moves *in play* тАФ plus a fix to an unintended cruelty: a
> companion downed in some random skirmish should not be gone forever. Only the Breach gets to do that.

- ЁЯй╣ **Stabilize-after-victory** тАФ when the party wins, any **downed (0-HP) companion is pulled back from
  the brink** (revived to ┬╝ HP), with a line in the log. Random battles no longer risk a permanent
  companion loss; **permanent death stays reserved for the Breach**, exactly as the story intends.
- тЭдя╕П **Combat-time approval nudges** тАФ surviving a fight together moves the meter: every fielded companion
  gains **+1 approval** on victory, and **+3** for anyone you had to pull back from the brink. Lives at the
  single combat-end chokepoint (`EncounterController.AwardExperience`), so it applies to **all** combat тАФ
  campaign, eras, demos тАФ keeping affinity breathing across the whole saga, not just in set-piece dialogue.
- ЁЯЯв 108 scripts / ~14.0k LOC, all clean. **The full companion roadmap is now complete.**

## ЁЯХпя╕П v1.18.0 тАФ *"The Faithless Choir"* тАФ The Unmade Comes to the Lower City (CODE)

> Act II stops being only personal errands and starts braiding into the *main* plot: the villain faction
> gets a face on a street corner, and your answer to it follows you to the Court.

- ЁЯХпя╕П **New side quest тАФ "The Faithless Choir"** (`ActTwoContent`) тАФ Brother Sere preaches the Unmade to
  the Gate's grieving poor, holding *you*, the Returned, up as proof the Wall can fall. A **trilemma**:
  **[Religion DC 15] give him doubt** (you've stood at the Wall; the cure is another atrocity тАФ the
  nuanced best, +Ilfaeril/Garrow), **set the Fist on him** (suppress тАФ Kelemvor тЖС, Lower City тЖУ, the
  grief just goes underground), or **speak for the Unmade** (`choir.sympathizer` тАФ the Choir remembers
  who spoke for it; тИТIlfaeril). With a graceful skill-fail branch.
- ЁЯз╡ **Reactive everywhere** тАФ Tamsin the crier gains three new conditional lines for your Choir stance;
  the Journey screen's Lower City section and the Chronicle both track it; and `EndingResolver` adds a
  **Faithless-Choir epilogue slide** (doubt тЖТ he sits with the dying; suppressed тЖТ it surfaced harder;
  spoken-for тЖТ they called you theirs).
- ЁЯЯв 108 scripts / ~13.9k LOC, all clean. The Lower City now reaches *up* into the central question, not
  just sideways into errands.

## ЁЯУЦ v1.17.0 тАФ *"The Chronicle of the Returned"* тАФ A Run Summary, Any Time (CODE)

> A sprawling, reactive saga is hard to hold in your head. Now you never have to: one keystroke shows
> you the whole shape of your playthrough, and the ending recaps it as a capstone.

- ЁЯУЦ **`ChronicleScreen` (press C)** тАФ a persistent, press-anytime overlay (beside Options/Help) listing
  the run at a glance: **eras walked; who's still at your side, taken by the Wall, or walked away; quests
  resolved (N/5); hearts given; bonds broken; Lower City standing; the Lady's riddles; endings unlocked;
  difficulty.** Pure read of the flags via the new `EndingResolver.Chronicle()`.
- ЁЯМЕ **Recap at the close** тАФ the **ending screen** now has a *"Read the Chronicle of the Returned"*
  expander, so the Court of the Dead leaves you with the whole journey, not just its last image.
- тЭФ Added to the **Help** card (`H`) and the controls legend.
- ЁЯЯв 108 scripts / ~13.7k LOC, all clean. The saga is now legible in a single keystroke.

## ЁЯПЩя╕П v1.16.0 тАФ *"The Quarter Pays Its Debts"* тАФ Lower City Standing Reaches the Ending (CODE)

> The Act II reputation you build now follows you all the way to the Court of the Dead тАФ the small good
> (or its absence) gets the last word it deserves.

- ЁЯдЭ **A reputation payoff** тАФ once `reputation.lowcity` тЙе 5, **Tamsin the crier** offers a one-time
  pledge (`lowcity.allies`): the Gate's poor, godless, and grieving will stand with you at the end. Gated
  via a `RequireIntAtLeast` conditional choice, so it only appears when earned and only once.
- ЁЯМЕ **It lands in the finale** тАФ `EndingResolver` adds a **Lower City epilogue slide**: a moving "they
  were there, with bread and lanterns and a hundred small refusals to look away" for high standing or the
  pledge тАФ and a quiet, cutting "you spent them like coin" for negative standing.
- ЁЯУЬ **Legible** тАФ the Journey screen's **Lower City** section now shows the pledge ("the quarter stands
  with you тАФ they'll be there at the end").
- ЁЯЯв 107 scripts / ~13.5k LOC, all clean. Act II's small kindnesses now echo in the last accounting.

## ЁЯзн v1.15.0 тАФ *"Never Lost, Never Stuck"* тАФ Help Card & Autosave-on-Rest (CODE)

> Two small comforts that make a sprawling systems-game approachable: you can always find out what a key
> does, and you never lose much progress.

- тЭФ **Help overlay** (`HelpOverlay`) тАФ press **H** anytime, in any mode, for a scrollable reference card:
  world controls, battle controls, every hotkey screen (J/P/K/I/O/B), and saving. Lives on the persistent
  director object, so it's always one key away.
- ЁЯТ╛ **Autosave on long rest** тАФ resting at camp now autosaves (`CampScene.onRested` тЖТ the director's
  `Autosave`), the natural CRPG checkpoint, with a "progress saved" note at the fire. Decoupled via a
  callback, so demos that use the camp don't touch the save file.
- ЁЯЯв 107 scripts / ~13.4k LOC, all clean.

## ЁЯОЪя╕П v1.14.0 тАФ *"Your Table, Your Rules"* тАФ Difficulty Modes (CODE)

> Some players are here for the tactics; some are here for the story and want the dice to get out of the
> way. Now both are first-class.

- ЁЯОЪя╕П **Story / Normal / Hard** (`GameSettings.Mode`) тАФ chosen in the Options screen (off the menu or
  in-game with **O**), persisted via `PlayerPrefs`. **Story** softens enemy damage (├Ч0.6) and buffs the
  party (├Ч1.35); **Hard** sharpens enemy damage (├Ч1.4) and nerfs the party a touch (├Ч0.9); **Normal** is
  the intended 5e balance.
- ЁЯОп **One chokepoint, applies everywhere** тАФ scaling lives in `AbilityRunner` between resolve and apply,
  keyed off the target's faction, so it covers **all** combat: the campaign, every era, and every demo тАФ
  no per-encounter wiring.
- ЁЯЯв 106 scripts / ~13.2k LOC, all clean. The table now flexes to the player at it.

## тЪУ v1.13.0 тАФ *"What You Stand To Lose"* тАФ Romance тЖФ the Breach & the Finale Anchor (CODE)

> Love stops being a side-quest with a happy slide and becomes the highest-stakes choice in the game.
> Whoever you let yourself love is now who the Wall reaches for тАФ and who the whole ending is *about.*

- тЪ░я╕ПЁЯТФ **The Wall takes what you love** тАФ `ChooseBreachVictim` now, once Varra is safe (pact broken),
  is drawn to a **committed romance** (`romance.<id>.turn`) among the Breach candidates before falling
  back to a volunteer or the least-loved. Romancing someone makes the Breach a genuine stake for *them.*
- тЪУ **The finale anchor** тАФ `EndingResolver.AnchorId()` picks the face the cosmos rests on: the deepest
  romance (consummated тЖТ committed тЖТ the turn), or, lacking one, the companion you let in closest by
  approval. Every ending now closes on an **anchor beat** keyed to whether they're beside you, **lost to
  the Breach**, or **driven away** тАФ three very different last words.
- ЁЯТФ **The cruelest epilogue** тАФ a dedicated *"the one you loved, taken by the Wall"* slide (a bespoke
  Varra variant: "the receipt collected before you ever got to burn it"), separate from the generic loss
  slide, so a romanced Breach death lands with its full intended weight.
- ЁЯЯв 106 scripts / ~13.1k LOC, all clean. The game's tenderness and its cruelty now share one mechanism.

## ЁЯПЩя╕П v1.12.0 тАФ *"The City Watches Back"* тАФ Act II Side Content & a Reactive Lower City (CODE)

> Act II stops being a corridor between eras and starts being a *place.* The first pass at the hub's
> connective tissue: a world that reads your choices back to you, and small moral side quests whose
> stakes are reputation and conscience rather than loot.

- ЁЯПЩя╕П **`ActTwoContent`** тАФ a Lower City content layer the hub places by flag-gate (active quest vs.
  resolved aftermath), the same way it gates Roen/Varra recruitment.
- ЁЯУ░ **Tamsin, the street crier** тАФ a living "news of you" board: her lines appear only as you *earn*
  them, via **conditional dialogue choices** (`DialogueChoice.conditions`) read live off `GameFlags` тАФ
  the widow you helped, the Faithless man you freed (or didn't), the falling city you walked, the verdict
  you argued down, a romance the quarter is scandalised by, a companion who walked out.
- тЪЦя╕П **Two thematic side quests**, dialogue-resolved (no grind):
  - **"The Widow's Coin"** тАФ Mhaere's son was taken in the harvest, denied rest. A **kind lie**, the
    **hard truth** (Garrow approves), or an **[Insight DC 14]** *true* comfort that reframes remembrance
    as resistance to unmaking (the best тАФ ties straight to the game's central question).
  - **"The Fist and the Faithless"** тАФ a sergeant ordered to hand a godless beggar to the Doomguides.
    **[Persuasion DC 14]** free him (Garrow тЖС, Kelemvor тЖУ), **bribe** the paperwork away, or **uphold the
    law** (Kelemvor тЖС, Garrow & Ilfaeril тЖУ). Each moves `reputation.lowcity`.
- ЁЯУЬ **Journey legibility** тАФ the **J** screen gains a **Lower City** section (standing + each side
  quest's outcome), so the new content reads as clearly as it plays.
- ЁЯОм **`ActTwoDemo`** тАФ one-click: walk the hub, resolve a side quest, then re-ask the crier and watch the
  city's tale of you change.
- ЁЯЯв 106 scripts / ~13.0k LOC, all clean. The hub now *reacts.* (Next: deeper Act II тАФ multi-room areas,
  Fugue-side beats, and tying side reputation into the finale.)

## ЁЯТФ v1.11.0 тАФ *"The Bonds That Break"* тАФ Rupture / Betrayal Arcs (CODE)

> The dark mirror of the romances. If love is a stake, this is the bill: drive a companion's approval into
> the ground тАФ keep crossing the one line their whole self is built on тАФ and the bond *frays.* The same
> data-first shape as the romances, pointed the other way.

- ЁЯТФ **Rupture engine** (`RuptureContent`) тАФ five companions (Garrow, Roen, Varra, Naeve, Ilfaeril), each
  with a value-line that, crossed too often (approval тЙд тИТ25), triggers a **camp confrontation** in their
  own voice тАФ desecration for Garrow, betrayed trust for Roen, the receipt for Varra, reckless reaching
  for Naeve, vengeance-wearing-mercy for Ilfaeril.
- ЁЯЬН **Three outcomes, and amends has teeth** тАФ **make amends** (only lands if you've earned *standing* тАФ
  `HasStanding`: a night-talk shared or a romance spark; you can't talk back someone you never bothered
  to know тЖТ `rupture.<id>.mended`, approval floored back up), **patch it over** (they stay, guarded тЖТ
  `rupture.<id>.uneasy`), or **let them walk** (`rupture.<id>.broken` + `companion.<id>.left`, removed
  from the party via `Party.Remove`). A thin amends that lacks standing collapses to patch-or-part.
- ЁЯФе **Surfaced at the fire** тАФ `CampScene` shows an urgent **"A Bond Frays"** section above everything
  else when `RuptureContent.Pending()` finds a cratered, present, unresolved companion.
- ЁЯМЕ **The Court remembers** тАФ `EndingResolver` adds a **walked-away epilogue slide** for any
  `companion.<id>.left` ("you'll never know how it ended for them тАФ that is its own kind of loss").
- ЁЯОм **`RuptureDemo`** тАФ one-click: a party with every bond cratered; two seeded with standing (amends can
  land), two without (words alone won't do it).
- ЁЯЯв 104 scripts / ~12.5k LOC, all clean. Love and its opposite now both have mechanical weight.

---

## тЪЩя╕П v1.10.0 тАФ *"Quality of Life"* тАФ Options & a Legible Quest Log (CODE)

> A polish pass that makes the game *yours* to tune and the saga *legible* at a glance тАФ the connective
> tissue a real player feels even when they never think about it.

- тЪЩя╕П **Options screen** (`GameSettings` + `SettingsScreen`) тАФ three knobs, persisted via `PlayerPrefs`
  and applied live: **ambient-banter toggle, master volume, dialogue text-speed** (or instant). Reachable
  off the main menu **and** in-game at any time with **O** (a persistent overlay above the mode root).
- тМия╕П **Typewriter dialogue** тАФ `DialogueScreen` now reveals lines at the chosen chars/second, with a
  one-click "show the rest" to skip the reveal; honors the Instant-text setting. Wired to the live setting,
  so dragging the slider in Options changes the feel immediately.
- ЁЯФЗ **Banter respects the setting** тАФ `AmbientBanter` now checks `GameSettings.BanterEnabled` (the **B**
  quick-mute still works too).
- ЁЯУЬ **Quest-log beat tracking** тАФ the Journey screen (**J**) now shows each companion quest's **current
  beat** (thread opened тЖТ at the scene тЖТ fought тЖТ *resolved-how*, e.g. "doctrine on trial", "contract
  burned") and a new **Bonds** section tracking each romance's furthest stage (a spark тЖТ trust тЖТ the turn
  тЖТ committed тЖТ the last night).
- ЁЯЯв 102 scripts / ~12.1k LOC, all clean. The companion content now *reads* as clearly as it plays.

## ЁЯТЮ v1.9.0 тАФ *"The Slow Burns"* тАФ All Four Romance Arcs (CODE)

> The companions stop being people you fight beside and become people you stand to *lose.* Four full
> romances, each an **argument about one of the game's themes** тАФ so falling in love is also taking a
> position on what the game is about. Built data-first, the way the personal quests were.

- ЁЯТЮ **Romance engine** (`RomanceContent`) тАФ a reusable, data-driven arc table on a shared six-stage
  spine: **Spark тЖТ Trust тЖТ Turn тЖТ Crisis тЖТ Choosing тЖТ The Last Night.** Each beat is gated by **both** an
  approval threshold **and** progression тАФ the previous stage, and for the **Crisis**, the companion's
  *resolved personal quest* (the romance literally runs through their quest). Mirrors `CampContent`: pure
  data, no scene boilerplate.
- ЁЯОн **Four arcs, four themes** тАФ **Garrow** (faith: something can be holy in a cruel cosmos), **Roen**
  (belonging: the bravest thing is to *stay*), **Naeve** (guilt: are you allowed to be loved after what
  you did), **Varra** (worth: you are more than your price). Key-beat dialogue drawn from
  `docs/story/16_ROMANCE_SCRIPTS.md`, each with a **deepen-or-stay-platonic** choice (holding is
  non-destructive тАФ the beat waits for you).
- ЁЯФе **Played at the fire** тАФ `CampScene` gains a **"Grow Closer"** section beside the night-talks,
  surfacing the best-eligible beat (`RomanceContent.Best()`); choosing someone moves their approval.
- ЁЯЬН **Love is a stake, not a collectible** тАФ pursuing two romances past the **Turn** is gently
  disallowed (`CommittedElsewhere`); a single, in-character commitment.
- ЁЯМЕ **Epilogue payoffs** тАФ `EndingResolver` adds a bespoke slide per consummated romance, including the
  game's most devastating beats: **Garrow gives you your own last rite in Break the Loop**, **Naeve
  derives the rewritten Law beside you in Jergal's Keyhole**, **Roen at the niche with no joke left**,
  and **Varra burning the receipt** for her soul at last.
- ЁЯОм **`RomanceDemo`** тАФ one-click tour: all four companions, gates pre-seeded, every arc open to walk.
- ЁЯЯв 100 scripts / ~11.8k LOC, all clean. **The companion pillar is whole: recruit тЖТ banter тЖТ approval тЖТ
  camp тЖТ personal quest тЖТ romance тЖТ epilogue.**

---

## ЁЯХКя╕П v1.8.0 тАФ *"The Vote"* тАФ Ilfaeril's Personal Quest (& the Companion Pillar Complete) (CODE)

> The fifth and final companion arc on the v1.5.0 template тАФ and with it, **all five companions now have
> a playable personal quest, end to end.** Ilfaeril faces the one soul he owes across ten thousand years,
> and the choice you help him make is the one his whole being turns on: *is atonement allowed to end?*

- ЁЯХКя╕П **Ilfaeril's quest тАФ "The Vote"** (`IlfaerilQuestContent`) тАФ an ancient elven reliquary, its lock
  keyed to **Maerith of the Singing Vale**, one of the souls his Crown-War council voted to *unmake* тАФ
  the verdict that hardened into the **Law of the Faithless.** Its waking draws the **Choir of the
  Unmade**, who revere him as their first witness and offer to end his guilt by proving he never should
  have felt any. Three hand-written conversations (arrival / the Pale Cantor / the resolution).
- ЁЯЬН **A moral trilemma** keyed to his wound (*atonement is not self-erasure; he is allowed to stop
  paying*): **refuse her forgiveness** and guide the lost forever (+10, devotion that is also a kind of
  hiding), **accept it** and let himself be more than his worst vote (+20, the Oath of Redemption
  fulfilled), or an **[Insight DC 16]** gambit that hears her forgiveness for what it is тАФ *not a door,
  a sword held hilt-first* тАФ and turns it into a **commission to tear the Wall open for the rest of her
  people** (+30, forgiveness that puts a man back to work) тАФ with a graceful fail branch. *(First quest
  to gate on Wisdom/Insight rather than Cha/Int.)*
- тЪФя╕П **The Choir, come for the witness** тАФ a five-enemy encounter (the Pale Cantor, two Choir Heralds,
  two Unmaking Acolytes) routed through the director, returning to the crypt for the resolution on victory.
- ЁЯМЕ **Epilogue payoff** тАФ `EndingResolver` adds an **Ilfaeril slide** keyed to his choice (commission /
  forgiven / penance), alongside the other four.
- ЁЯкЭ **Hub thread now playable** тАФ Ilfaeril's reliquary hook (`CompanionQuests`) flips to `playable =
  true` with a `followLabel`; also fixed a pronoun slip in its tease (canon: *he* renounced his house).
- ЁЯОм **`IlfaerilQuestDemo`** тАФ one-click preview of all three resolutions.
- ЁЯЯв 98 scripts / ~11.3k LOC, all clean. **The companion-quest pillar is complete: five for five.**

---

## тЬи v1.7.0 тАФ *"After the Sky Fell"* тАФ Naeve's Personal Quest (CODE)

> The fourth companion arc, again almost pure content on the v1.5.0 template: Naeve goes home to a
> fragment of Netheril that never finished falling тАФ and the choice you help her make is the one her
> whole wound turns on: *some mistakes can only be carried, not erased.*

- тЬи **Naeve's quest тАФ "After the Sky Fell"** (`NaeveQuestContent`) тАФ a shard of dead Weave hums her
  home's exact note: a piece of the **Seventh Enclave**, held aloft a thousand years past its death by a
  failing **mythallar**. The echo of the **Steward Vaelin** tells her the truth тАФ *her own* wardstone
  saved this fragment by sentencing it to fall slowly, and keeping it frozen has been draining the last
  live Weave in the world. Three hand-written conversations (arrival / Vaelin's echo / the resolution).
- ЁЯММ **A moral trilemma** keyed to her wound (*her genius ended a world; she must learn to carry, not
  erase*): **freeze the shard in stasis** and keep the last of Netheril whole (+10, a tomb she calls a
  home), **let it finish falling** and carry the grief instead of the wreckage (+20, acceptance), or an
  **[Arcana DC 16] gambit** that opens the wardstone and gives its live Weave *back to the present* as a
  seed instead of a shroud (+30, "an arithmetic that builds") тАФ with a graceful fail branch that
  collapses to the two plain choices. (A faint *you-are-a-loop* foreshadow hides in the margin note.)
- тЪФя╕П **The last protocol** тАФ a five-enemy encounter (a Mythallar Ward, two Arcane Sentinels, two
  Weave-wraiths) routed through the director, returning to the core for the resolution on victory.
- ЁЯМЕ **Epilogue payoff** тАФ `EndingResolver` adds a **Naeve slide** keyed to her choice (rekindled /
  released / preserved), alongside Roen's, Varra's, and Garrow's.
- ЁЯкЭ **Hub thread now playable** тАФ Naeve's shard hook (`CompanionQuests`) flips to `playable = true`
  with a `followLabel`, opening the quest through the existing generic hub wiring.
- ЁЯОм **`NaeveQuestDemo`** тАФ one-click preview of all three resolutions.
- ЁЯЯв 96 scripts / ~11.0k LOC, all clean. **Four playable companion quests; one to go.**

---

## тЪЦя╕П v1.6.0 тАФ *"A God-Shaped Hole"* тАФ Garrow's Personal Quest (CODE)

> The third companion arc, built almost entirely from content on the v1.5.0 template: Sister Garrow is
> summoned to a Kelemvorite tribunal for heresy, and the choice you help her make is the one the whole
> saga is really about тАФ *what is a soul worth that no god ever claimed?*

- тЪЦя╕П **Garrow's quest тАФ "A God-Shaped Hole"** (`GarrowQuestContent`) тАФ a black-edged writ calls Sister
  Garrow to a Doomguide tribunal to answer for failing to lay her fallen mentor and for travelling with
  **the Returned** тАФ a soul no god claimed. **Justiciar Veld**, who taught her catechism, means to make
  her recant or be cast out; the trial is rigged, the verdict pre-written, so it becomes a fight. Three
  hand-written conversations (arrival / the Justiciar's charge / the resolution).
- ЁЯЬН **A moral trilemma** keyed to her wound (*obedience that felt like betrayal*): **recant to keep the
  grey** and do the work from inside (+10, a brittle, sorrowful faith), **walk away from the faith
  entirely** and lay the dead under no one's law (+20, Faithless and unafraid), or a **[Religion DC 16]
  gambit** that puts Kelemvor's *own canon* on trial тАФ proving the Faithless judgment is itself the
  heresy (+30, the seed of the rewritten Law) тАФ with a graceful fail branch that collapses to the two
  plain choices.
- тЪФя╕П **The Justiciar's tribunal** тАФ a five-enemy encounter (Veld, two templar inquisitors, two grey
  enforcers) routed through the director, returning to the temple for the resolution on victory.
- ЁЯМЕ **Epilogue payoff** тАФ `EndingResolver` adds a **Garrow slide** keyed to her answer (reformer /
  apostate / brittle keeper), alongside Roen's and Varra's.
- ЁЯкЭ **Hub thread now playable** тАФ Garrow's summons hook (`CompanionQuests`) flips to `playable = true`
  with a `followLabel`, so the existing generic hub wiring opens the quest with no bespoke code.
- ЁЯОм **`GarrowQuestDemo`** тАФ one-click preview of all three resolutions.
- ЁЯЯв 94 scripts / ~10.8k LOC, all clean. **Three playable companion quests; the template keeps delivering.**

---

## тЪЦя╕П v1.5.0 тАФ *"The Bill Comes Due"* тАФ A Reusable Quest Engine & Varra's Arc (CODE)

> The personal-quest pattern becomes a *template*: one data-driven scene now runs every companion's
> arc, and Varra's is the first new quest built on it тАФ an infernal contract, not a sibling rescue.

- ЁЯзй **`PersonalQuestScene` + `PersonalQuest`** тАФ Roen's bespoke scene is refactored into a **reusable,
  data-driven stage**. The arc shape (arrive тЖТ examine тЖТ confront тЖТ fight тЖТ moral call тЖТ leave) is now
  code; *what* happens is config. Each remaining companion quest is mostly **content, not boilerplate.**
- тЪЦя╕П **Varra's quest тАФ "The Bill Comes Due"** (`VarraQuestContent`) тАФ her patron calls the contract she
  signed at **six years old**, early. In a deconsecrated chapel, the cambion broker **Quill** who sold
  her waits to collect. A fight (Quill + contract-devils + imps of the fine print) and a **moral
  trilemma**: **carry her debt yourself** (+25, she sleeps for the first time in 20 years), **let her
  burn it freely** (+15, her choice, her clock), or an **[Arcana DC 16] loophole** that binds her
  *patron* instead (+30, the best outcome) тАФ with a graceful fail branch.
- ЁЯМЕ **Epilogue payoff** тАФ `EndingResolver` adds a **Varra slide** keyed to your call (patron-bound /
  debt-taken / freed), alongside Roen's Wrenna slide.
- ЁЯкЭ **Generic hub threads** тАФ the hub now places a "follow the thread" marker for **any** playable,
  started-but-unresolved companion quest (`CompanionQuests.playable`), wired through a single
  `onEnterPersonalQuest(id)` callback. Roen's old bespoke wiring is gone.
- ЁЯОм **`VarraQuestDemo`** тАФ one-click preview of all three resolutions.
- ЁЯз╣ Removed the now-redundant `RoenQuestScene` (folded into `PersonalQuestScene`).
- ЁЯЯв 92 scripts / ~10.6k LOC, all clean. **Two playable companion quests; a template for the rest.**

---

## ЁЯЧбя╕П v1.4.0 тАФ *"The Honest Lie"* тАФ Roen's Personal Quest, End to End (CODE)

> The first companion thread becomes a *playable arc*: a silent Harper safehouse, a sister who lied
> for two years to keep her brother off the Wall, a Doomguide cell, and a moral call that follows you
> all the way to the epilogue. The hook from v1.3.0 now has a quest on the end of it.

- ЁЯЧ║я╕П **`RoenQuestScene`** тАФ a bespoke arc on the SimpleEra pattern with its own beat order: **arrive** at
  the safehouse (auto-dialogue), examine the scene, **corner Wrenna** for the reveal, fight, then make
  the call. State-driven by `roen.quest.cleared` (the fight) and `quest.roen.resolved` (the choice).
- ЁЯУЬ **`RoenQuestContent`** тАФ three hand-written conversations (Arrival, the Wrenna reveal, the
  Resolution) with a real **moral trilemma**: **forgive** her (Roen **+20** approval, Wrenna saved),
  **condemn** her by the rules (**тИТ15**, a Harper intel boon), or a **[Persuasion DC 15] gambit** to
  turn her into a double agent (best outcome: **+25**, both boons) тАФ with a graceful fail branch.
- тЪФя╕П **The Doomguide cell** тАФ a six-enemy encounter (knights, enforcers, a zealot, an interrogator)
  routed through the director, returning you to the safehouse for the resolution on victory.
- ЁЯМЕ **Epilogue payoff** тАФ `EndingResolver` now adds a **Wrenna slide** keyed to your call, so the
  safehouse choice echoes in the Court of the Dead (saved / double-agent / turned-in variants).
- ЁЯкЭ **Hub thread** тАФ once you've examined the cipher hook, a *"Follow the cipher"* marker opens the
  quest; it closes once resolved. Wired into the director (`EnterRoenQuest` / `StartRoenFight`).
- ЁЯОм **`RoenQuestDemo`** тАФ one-click preview (skips the battle) to tour all three resolutions.
- ЁЯЯв 89 scripts / ~10.0k LOC, all clean. **The first companion quest is fully playable.**

## ЁЯз╡ v1.3.0 тАФ *"Threads to Pull"* тАФ Approval in Play & Companion Personal-Quest Hooks (CODE)

> The affinity loop closes end-to-end: kindness now *moves the meter in normal play*, and opening
> someone up at the fire hangs a thread in the world тАФ the start of their personal quest.

- тЭдя╕П **Approval-shifting dialogue** тАФ the Roen and Varra recruit conversations now **grant approval**
  through `companion.<id>.approval` (warmer choices give more), so the meter rises in ordinary play тАФ
  not just demos. The kindness тЖТ approval тЖТ camp night-talk loop now runs **without scaffolding.**
- ЁЯз╡ **Companion personal-quest hooks** (`CompanionQuests`) тАФ once a campfire **night-talk** opens a
  companion up, a pointer to their **Act II personal quest** appears in the hub (Roen's Harper cipher,
  Varra's matured invoice, Garrow's heresy summons, Naeve's shard of dead Weave, Ilfaeril's reliquary).
  Examining it **starts the quest** (`quest.<id>.started`) and reads its hand-written tease.
- ЁЯкЭ **`Interactable.onExamined`** тАФ examine markers can now fire a code callback (used to flag quest
  starts); a small, reusable hook for any "inspecting this *does* something" beat.
- ЁЯУЬ **Journey tracker** now lists a **Companion Threads** section тАФ which personal quests you've opened
  and started тАФ so the new content is legible at a glance (press **J**).
- ЁЯЯв 86 scripts / ~9.5k LOC, all clean.

## ЁЯФе v1.2.0 тАФ *"The Fire's Low"* тАФ Camp, Long Rest & Approval-Gated Night-Talks (CODE)

> The quiet half of a CRPG. A place to rest your wounds and refill your magic тАФ and a campfire
> where the companion who trusts you most finally says what they've been carrying.

- ЁЯФе **`CampScene`** тАФ a campfire mode reached from a **new hub marker**: a **long rest** restores the
  fielded party to **full HP** and **refreshes all spell slots**, and a **"sit with someone"** beat
  offers a night-talk from whichever companion is closest to you.
- ЁЯТм **Approval-gated night-talks** (`CampContent`) тАФ five hand-written monologues (Roen, Varra, Garrow,
  Naeve, Ilfaeril), each unlocked only once that companion's **approval crosses a threshold** *and*
  they're **fielded**. One per companion; listening itself earns a little more approval. The new
  approval meter (v1.1.0) now *pays off.*
- ЁЯОм **`CampDemo`** тАФ one-click: a battle-worn party at the fire with approval pre-seeded and a wounded
  companion, so you can watch the rest heal them and hear a night-talk immediately.
- ЁЯЯв 84 scripts / ~9.3k LOC, all clean.

## ЁЯУЦ v1.1.0 тАФ *"What You've Witnessed"* тАФ The Codex, Companion Sheets & Ambient Banter (CODE)

> The world starts talking back. A compendium that fills in as you witness the saga, full stat
> blocks for your companions (with how much they *like* you), and idle chatter on the road.

- ЁЯУЦ **`CodexScreen`** (press **`K`**) тАФ a lore & bestiary compendium with a category rail (The Premise,
  The Four Masks, Bestiary, Lore & History) and a reading pane. Entries live in **`CodexContent`** and
  are **gated by `GameFlags`** тАФ you only know what you've witnessed, so the Codex *grows as you play*
  (Aldric unlocks at tea, the Unmade at Netheril, the Last Returned at the Crown Wars, the Lady at the
  Reader's BoonтАж). Shows **N/total discovered.**
- ЁЯЫбя╕П **Companion sheets** тАФ the Party screen (**`P`**) now expands on click: full **ability block**
  (STRтАУCHA with modifiers), **AC / HP / initiative / proficiency**, and an **approval meter** showing
  how much each companion likes you (devoted тЖТ hostile), read from `companion.<id>.approval`.
- ЁЯТм **`AmbientBanter`** тАФ idle party chatter while you wander, drawn from **`PartyBanter`** and filtered
  to **who's actually in the field** (Roen, Varra, Garrow, Naeve, Ilfaeril each have voice; plus eerie
  anyone-lines about the Wall). Fades in low in the frame; **mute with `B`.**
- ЁЯФЦ **Codex hooks** тАФ `EnterVault` now sets `riddle.entered` so the Vault of Tens self-documents.
- ЁЯЯв 82 scripts / ~9.1k LOC, all clean.

## ЁЯПЫя╕П v1.0.0 тАФ *"The Saga, Made Legible"* тАФ Journey Tracker, Roster Management & the Vertical-Slice Capstone (CODE)

> The slice now reads as a *game with a spine*: a quest log that tracks the whole arc, a party
> bench, a finale that's earned rather than handed to you, and a player-facing how-to-play guide.

- ЁЯУЬ **`JourneyScreen`** (press **`J`**) тАФ a live **quest tracker** read straight out of `GameFlags`:
  the Cinderhaunt, tea with Aldric, the Breach, all **four eras**, the **Vault of Tens**, and the
  **Reader's Boon** тАФ each тЬФ/тЧЛ тАФ plus **"Endings unlocked: N/6"** and a **тШЕ golden road** indicator
  when one of the two deepest endings is reachable. The saga finally reads as a checklist.
- ЁЯЫбя╕П **`RosterScreen`** (press **`P`**) тАФ **bench/field** any recruited companion up to `maxActive`;
  the **protagonist is locked into the field.** Benched companions keep their levels and gear.
- ЁЯПЫя╕П **Finale gating tightened** тАФ the **Court of the Dead** now opens only after you've **walked at
  least one era** (`netheril.cleared`), so the ending is a *culmination*, not a shortcut. The Journey
  screen tells you exactly why it isn't open yet.
- ЁЯУШ **`docs/HOW_TO_PLAY_THE_SLICE.md`** тАФ a 20-minute guided run from the title screen to the Court of
  the Dead: the loop step-by-step, the full control map, and how to read the Journey & Party screens.
- ЁЯЯв 78 scripts / ~8.8k LOC, all clean. **Boot тЖТ New Game тЖТ play the whole arc, now with a quest log.**

## ЁЯОЫя╕П v0.9.3 тАФ *"A Front Door"* тАФ Main Menu, Continue, Roaming Tally & Sprite-Ready Units (CODE)

> The wrapper that turns a pile of demos into a *game you boot up.*

- тЦ╢я╕П **`MainMenu`** тАФ a real front end: **New Game / Continue / Quit.** Drop it in the boot scene; it
  launches `CampaignBootstrap` fresh or resumes the save.
- ЁЯТ╛ **Save & Continue, deepened** тАФ the save now captures the **hero's build** (name, class, race,
  level, ability scores); the campaign **autosaves on every return to the hub**, and **Continue**
  reconstructs the hero *and* re-recruits your roster from the `companion.*.recruited` / `.lost` flags
  (permanent losses stay lost тАФ the Wall keeps what it took, across sessions).
- ЁЯО▓ **Roaming Tally** тАФ after you've walked an era, the Lady in the Margins **pops in at the hub**
  (G-Man style) with a one-off roaming riddle; answer it for her amusement. Appears once.
- ЁЯЦ╝я╕П **Sprite-ready units** тАФ `WorldArt` + a `GridUnit` hook: drop `Resources/Sprites/<Name>.png` and
  that character renders as a sprite billboard instead of a cube тАФ *zero wiring.* No art? Cubes, as
  before. The bridge from prototype to a real CRPG look.
- ЁЯЯв 76 scripts / ~8.7k LOC, all clean. **Boot тЖТ New Game тЖТ play the whole arc тЖТ Continue later.**

## ЁЯМля╕ПЁЯМА v0.9.2 тАФ *"Where the Ink Runs"* тАФ The Last Two Eras (CODE)

> All four time-travel eras are now playable тАФ and the Spellplague makes *causality itself* a hazard.

- ЁЯзй **`SimpleEra`** тАФ a reusable, config-driven era scene (grid + floor + camera + exploration UI +
  leader + a point-of-interest + a battle trigger), so new eras are *config, not boilerplate.*
- ЁЯМля╕П **Time of Troubles** (era 3, 1358 DR) тАФ witness the **Crown of Horns forged from Myrkul's skull**;
  the Crown-is-Myrkul reveal lands in-engine (sets `act4.crown_is_myrkul`). Fight the avatar-touched.
- ЁЯМА **Spellplague** (era 4, 1385 DR) + **`SpellplagueHazard`** тАФ a *causality-optional* battlefield:
  each turn after the second may **swap two combatants' positions** (a reality skip) and lash a random
  one with **blue fire** (Force). Your positioning is never quite safe. `EncounterBuilder` gains a
  `spellplagueHazard` toggle.
- ЁЯФЧ Both wired as flag-gated hub rifts (ToT after the Crown Wars; Spellplague after ToT). The director
  is now a **10-mode** machine. Plus **`SpellplagueDemo`** for a one-click taste.
- ЁЯЯв 74 scripts / ~8.4k LOC, all clean. **All four eras of the saga are playable.**

## ЁЯМЕ v0.9.1 тАФ *"The Court of the Dead"* тАФ The Six Endings, In Code

> The capstone that makes every flag *mean* something: a finale that reads your whole playthrough.

- ЁЯза **`EndingResolver`** тАФ pure logic that reads GameFlags to decide which endings you've **earned the
  right to choose** (deeper truths gate the golden roads: *Jergal's Keyhole* needs the Lady's riddle +
  a spared Verdict; *Break the Loop* needs you to have grasped the loop), supplies each ending's prose,
  and assembles **BG2-style epilogue slides** keyed to who lived, who the Wall took, the Verdict, the
  Lady's witness, and Aldric's fate.
- ЁЯПЫя╕П **`EndingScreen`** тАФ the **Court of the Dead** finale: the convergence framing, the available
  endings as choices (golden ones starred), and on a pick the full prose + epilogue.
- ЁЯФЧ Wired in: a **Court of the Dead** exit in the hub (now an **8-mode** director), plus **`EndingDemo`**
  тАФ a one-click tour that unlocks all six to read prose + epilogues side by side.
- ЁЯЯв 70 scripts / ~8.0k LOC, all clean. The full arc тАФ create тЖТ play тЖТ *end* тАФ now exists in code.

## тЪ░я╕П v0.9.0 тАФ *"The Wall Keeps What It Takes"* тАФ The Fugue, Maerin & the Breach (CODE)

> The game's first **permanent loss** тАФ the beat that proves this story will take things and never
> give them back.

- ЁЯй╢ **`FugueEra` + `FugueContent`** тАФ descend (from the hub, after the Cinderhaunt) into the grey
  **Fugue Plane** and walk the **Wall of the Faithless**: the faces in the mortar, and the niche with
  **your own name**, a little more formed than last time.
- тЪ░я╕П **The Breach** тАФ pull **Maerin** free of the Wall, and the Wall takes its tithe: a companion is
  **removed from the party forever** (`Party.Remove`; no revival exists, by design). *Who* is decided
  by an **authored-fate** system (doc 15): **Varra** by default (her Act I 'leash' pays off), else a
  companion **volunteers** (Ilfaeril тЖТ Garrow тЖТ Naeve), else the **lowest-approval** member тАФ so the
  grief is *authored by your earlier care*, not merely inflicted.
- ЁЯзСтАНЁЯдЭтАНЁЯзС **Two more recruitable companions** тАФ **Varra** (a tiefling warlock, in the hub) and **Maerin**
  (pulled from the Wall) тАФ bringing the playable roster to six, all flag-driven.
- ЁЯОм **`BreachDemo`** тАФ a one-click harness: walk the Fugue, pull Maerin, watch Varra be taken.
- ЁЯз▒ `CampaignBootstrap` is now a **7-mode** director (hub тЗД dungeon тЗД Netheril тЗД Crown Wars тЗД Fugue тЗД
  Vault тЗД encounter). 67 scripts / ~7.7k LOC, all clean.

## ЁЯТ░ v0.8.3 тАФ *"The Margin Pays Out"* тАФ Vault Rewards (CODE)

> Solving the Lady's riddles now actually *rewards* you тАФ narrative boons, not a +2 sword.

- ЁЯкЩ **Coin of the Tenth Guest** (5 riddles solved) тАФ a usable consumable that mends you with a *nudge
  of fate* (3d8 heal). *"Spend it when fate needs a nudge."*
- ЁЯОБ **Her Favour** (10 solved, high amusement) тАФ a stronger single-use mending (6d8). *"Use it the
  moment you'd otherwise lose someone."*
- ЁЯУЬ **The Reader's Boon** (solve the secret 11th тАФ her name) тАФ a lore trophy + a flag the finale
  checks. *"Proof that, once, the margin smiled."*
- тЪЩя╕П Rewards are granted **once per milestone** (flag-guarded) by `RiddleVaultUI`, dropped straight into
  the party pouch and usable from the inventory screen.

## ЁЯзй v0.8.2 тАФ *"The Vault Made Real"* тАФ The Riddle Room, In Engine (CODE)

> The Lady in the Margins steps off the page: a playable riddle room built on the existing engine.

- ЁЯОн **`RiddleContent`** тАФ 15 symbolic **answer-tokens** (as quest items), the **10 object riddles**,
  the **brazier (spoken) riddles**, the locked *Your Name*, the secret 11th (*her* name), and **Tally's**
  hub dialogue.
- ЁЯПЫя╕П **`RiddleVault`** тАФ the **Vault of Tens** as an explorable room: ten pedestals (place a token), a
  row of braziers (speak the word), the violet **Margin Brazier** (the twist riddle), and a way out;
  she hands you the pouch of tokens on entry.
- ЁЯЦея╕П **`RiddleVaultUI`** тАФ solve riddles by **placing a token from the pouch** or **typing the spoken
  answer**; the **wit-beats-correctness** system rewards clever-wrong tokens with *amusement* instead of
  a solve, and failure costs only her interest тАФ **she never kills you, she only gets bored.**
- ЁЯФЧ Wired in: **Tally** appears in the Baldur's Gate hub; hearing her out (`vault.requested`) sends the
  director into the Vault (now a **6-mode** director). Plus **`RiddleVaultDemo`** for a one-click test.
- ЁЯз▒ A small modal guard (`RiddleVaultUI.AnyOpen`) so clicking the puzzle panel doesn't also move your
  token. 64 scripts / ~7.1k LOC, all clean.

---

## ЁЯОн v0.8.1 тАФ *"The Note in the Margin"* тАФ The Riddler & the Vault of Tens

> A surreal, chaotic-neutral fifth-dimensional entity who *monitors the situation* тАФ and a riddle
> room better than Bodhi's, with twenty original riddles.

- ЁЯОн **`22_THE_LADY_IN_THE_MARGINS.md`** тАФ the recurring riddler in the lineage of **G-Man / the
  Outsider / Gaunter O'Dimm / Mr. Door**: chaotic neutral, beyond gender/comprehension, wants only to
  be *entertained.* Her **HUGE late twist** тАФ she is the **ascended form of Naeve**, riddling you from
  the white space at the end of time (a character you've been interacting with all along,
  pre-ascension) тАФ with a full foreshadowing ledger so it's *fair.*
- ЁЯзй **The Vault of Tens** тАФ a riddle room that keeps BG2's place-the-object joy and adds four things:
  **wit beats correctness** (clever-wrong answers are rewarded), **no death тАФ only boredom**,
  **token combinations / cross-reference**, and **tiered narrative rewards** (a reroll, a truth, a
  witness тАФ never a +2 sword).
- ЁЯУЬ **20 original D&D riddles** (+ the secret 21st = her name) тАФ answers as **objects to place** or
  **words to speak**, several woven into the game's own themes (the MirrorтЖТthe Last Returned, the
  SkullтЖТthe Crown of Horns, *Your Name*тЖТthe master key, *Tomorrow*тЖТthe deathless Now, and *the Wall of
  the Faithless*, "the one she didn't write"). Includes implementation notes mapping the Vault onto the
  existing engine (pedestal Interactables + token items + flags).

---

## ЁЯкЮ v0.8.0 тАФ *"Reflections & the First Sin"* тАФ The Crown Wars, the Echoes, Tiled Floors & Aldric's Tea (CODE)

> A second era (proving the module pattern twice), the reflection-fight against yourself, a real
> isometric floor, and the marquee Act I conversation тАФ all playable.

- ЁЯМля╕П **Crown Wars era** (`CrownWarsEra` + `CrownWarsContent`) тАФ an elven high court ~10,000 years
  back, reached via a **second "Deep Skip" rift** after Netheril. Recruit **Ilfaeril**, and the
  signature **moral-hazard scene**: *The Verdict*, where you can **argue a soul-damnation down**
  with a skill check (proving the Wall was a *decision*) тАФ shifting flags + Ilfaeril's approval.
- ЁЯкЮ **The Echoes / the Mirror fight** (`MirrorResolver`, `EncounterBuilder.mirrorMode`,
  `MirrorEncounterDemo`) тАФ fight twisted **clones of your own party** (new `CharacterSheet.Clone()`)
  plus **the Last Returned**, who *kneels and yields* once its Echoes fall rather than dying by
  damage. The late-game centrepiece, in miniature.
- ЁЯЯл **Tiled isometric floor** (`TileFloorRenderer`) тАФ every scene now paints a checker-tinted
  diamond floor under the units (walls/voids drawn dark). A real visual upgrade, no art needed.
- тШХ **"Tea with a Heretic"** (`AldricContent`) тАФ Aldric's full branching conversation, in-engine;
  he comes to the Baldur's Gate hub once you've cleared the Cinderhaunt.
- ЁЯз▒ `CampaignBootstrap` now drives a **5-mode** director (hub тЗД dungeon тЗД Netheril тЗД Crown Wars тЗД
  encounter) and auto-recruits Naeve & Ilfaeril by flag. 60 scripts / ~6.6k LOC, all clean.

## ЁЯМЖ v0.7.0 тАФ *"The Falling City"* тАФ Netheril, the First Time-Travel Era (CODE)

> The saga's time-travel becomes *playable.* You step through a rift in Baldur's Gate into a
> Netherese enclave falling out of the sky тАФ and fight as the floor caves in beneath you.

- ЁЯХ░я╕П **`NetherilEra`** тАФ an explorable golden-rubble enclave (Karsus's Folly, тИТ339 DR): arrive
  out of time (auto-played fall sequence), find **Naeve** in the rubble, recruit her, and trigger
  the battle. Flag-tracked like the Cinderhaunt so it survives the round-trip to combat.
- ЁЯХ│я╕П **`FallingHazard`** тАФ the era's signature mechanic: after a short grace period, the floor
  **collapses each turn from the edges inward** тАФ voided tiles block movement and deal falling
  damage; it never collapses below a safe core, so the fight stays winnable but frantic.
  `EncounterBuilder` now has an `environmentalHazard` toggle.
- ЁЯзЩ **`NetherilContent`** тАФ arcane abilities (Arcane Bolt, Lightning Lance, **Shatterglass** AoE,
  construct slams), the **Netherese War-Construct** roster, **Naeve** (Wizard companion), and the
  era arrival + recruit dialogue.
- ЁЯМА **Rift transition** тАФ after clearing the Cinderhaunt, a **Skip rift** appears in the hub;
  `CampaignBootstrap` now drives a 4-mode director (hub тЗД dungeon тЗД era тЗД encounter) and
  auto-recruits Naeve via dialogue flag, into the roster and into the falling-city fight.
- ЁЯМЖ **`NetherilDemo`** тАФ one-click jump straight into the collapsing-floor battle.
- ЁЯУИ 54 scripts / ~5.8k LOC, all brace-balanced and namespace-clean.

## ЁЯРЙ v0.6.6 тАФ *"Monsters, Money & Act One"* тАФ Bestiary, Pitch & the Full Act I Script

> The combat-as-theme bestiary, the document that makes it fundable, and Act I scene by scene.

- ЁЯРЙ **`19_BESTIARY_AND_BOSSES.md`** тАФ enemies & bosses mapped to our combat engine: stat blocks,
  the **Lay vs. Shatter** mercy mechanic, the **Echoes** (mirror fights vs. your own party), and the
  **anti-bosses** (the Unmade and the Last Returned тАФ beaten by *not* fighting). Every enemy is *a
  question with a health bar.*
- ЁЯЪА **`20_PITCH_AND_VERTICAL_SLICE.md`** тАФ the Kickstarter-grade **pitch one-pager** (logline, 5 USPs,
  comparables) + the **one-hour vertical-slice spec** that proves the whole game + honest **scope,
  budget tiers, and risk**.
- ЁЯОм **`21_ACT_ONE_SCRIPT.md`** тАФ the **full Act I script**, Prologue + 3 chapters, scene by scene
  (purpose ┬╖ beats ┬╖ branches ┬╖ flags), with an Act-I reactivity ledger feeding the later payoffs.

## ЁЯТЮ v0.6.5 тАФ *"Hearts & Endings"* тАФ Romances, Ending Prose & the Art/Music Bible

> The game gets a heart, a curtain call, and a face & a voice.

- ЁЯТЮ **`16_ROMANCE_SCRIPTS.md`** тАФ full **romance arcs** for Garrow, Roen, Naeve, and Varra тАФ six
  stages each (Spark тЖТ Trust тЖТ Turn тЖТ Crisis тЖТ Choosing тЖТ The Last Night), with key-beat dialogue,
  approval gating, and how each romance becomes the finale's `anchor`. Each romance is an *argument
  about a theme* (faith / belonging / guilt / worth).
- ЁЯМД **`17_ENDINGS_PROSE.md`** тАФ all **six endings written as full prose epilogues** (+ the hidden
  "Husk" failure-state): the final scene, the per-companion slides, and the last image, each landing
  the cosmos on a single human face.
- ЁЯОиЁЯО╝ **`18_ART_AND_MUSIC_BIBLE.md`** тАФ the **color language** (*warmth = mortality*), per-era and
  per-character visual identity (silhouette-first), UI/diegetic design, and a **leitmotif-driven
  score** built on one unfinished six-note phrase (*The Niche*) that finally resolves on your true
  name in the finale.

---

## ЁЯзм v0.6.4 тАФ *"Engineering the Gasp"* тАФ Twist Architecture & Two Devastating Scenes

> The craft principles, baked into the structure тАФ plus the two scenes designed to make players
> say *"HOLY SHIT."*

- ЁЯзм **`13_TWIST_ARCHITECTURE.md`** тАФ the redesign: a **Foreshadowing Ledger** (every clue тЖТ its
  payoff, to pass the replay test), the **early permanent loss** design, the **weaponized-kindness**
  placement, **Mirror** visual staging, "**land the cosmos on one face**," the once-only
  **meta-crossing**, and a revised beat sheet sequencing all of it.
- ЁЯкд **`14_SCENE_WEAPONIZED_KINDNESS.md`** тАФ full scene: the reveal that the player's *compassion*
  (pulling Maerin from the Wall) is the loop's engine тАФ *mercy as the trap.* Branching, shown-not-told.
- ЁЯХ│я╕П **`15_SCENE_THE_BREACH.md`** тАФ full scene: the game's first **irreversible loss**, with an
  **authored-fate system** (who the Wall takes depends on the player's earlier care). Teaches the
  player this story will take things and keep them.

---

## ЁЯОм v0.6.3 тАФ *"Scenes & Craft"* тАФ Dialogue Scripts, Side Quests & Emotional Design

> The set-piece conversations, the living city, and a craft study of the genre's greatest twists.

- ЁЯТм **`10_DIALOGUE_SCRIPTS.md`** тАФ full branching dialogue trees (node format, with checks/flags/
  approval) for the three marquee scenes: **"Tea with a Heretic"** (Aldric), **"The Offer"** (the
  Unmade at the Wall), and **"The Mirror"** (the Last Returned).
- ЁЯЧ║я╕П **`11_SIDEQUESTS_AND_NPCS.md`** тАФ themed Baldur's Gate **side quests** (each a small echo of the
  central question), per-era side content, a roster of **memorable NPCs**, and **reactive world state**.
- ЁЯТе **`12_EMOTIONAL_DESIGN.md`** тАФ a craft study of the **20 most-remembered RPG moments** (Aerith,
  Revan, Planescape, Mordin, the Bloody Baron, Undertale, NieR, Spec OpsтАж), the anatomy of a
  "HOLY SHIT" twist, and an **honest audit** of how *The Crown of Horns* reaches that tier.

## ЁЯЦЛя╕П v0.6.2 тАФ *"Flesh and Bone"* тАФ The Story, Fully Fleshed Out

> Everything deepened: full companion arcs, villain origin novellas, the esoteric texts, and
> prose treatments of the key scenes. ~12k more words of canon.

- ЁЯОн **`06_COMPANIONS_DEEP.md`** тАФ complete dossiers for all seven: full backstories, three-chapter
  **personal quests**, **romance arcs** beat-by-beat, cross-companion **banter**, approval triggers,
  and every fate. (Garrow, Roen, Varra, Naeve, Ilfaeril, Maerin, the Mournlight.)
- ЁЯСБя╕П **`07_VILLAINS_DEEP.md`** тАФ **origin novellas**: Aldric's forty years of graves; Myrkul's long
  patience; **the Unmade told from its own point of view**; the Last Returned's burned timeline;
  Vayle's terrible honesty; Jergal's boredom.
- ЁЯУЬ **`08_CODEX.md`** тАФ the **esoteric texts in full** (*The Ledger of the Unwalled*, *Karsus's Last
  Theorem*, *The Ilfaeril Confession*, *The Doomsong of Jergal*, *The Niche*), factions, the
  time-travel **timeline**, the **bestiary**, and the **places**.
- тЬНя╕П **`09_PROSE.md`** тАФ novella-grade **prose treatments**: the Death, the Wall, the **Deathless
  Garden**, the **Mirror** (the duel with your future self), and the **Name** (the finale).
- ЁЯФЧ Story library index updated.

## ЁЯУЪ v0.6.1 тАФ *"The Deep Water"* тАФ The Complete Story Bible

> A full, novel-grade narrative library тАФ the story fleshed out to BG2 / Planescape depth.

- ЁЯУЦ New **`docs/story/`** library (6 documents, ~30k words of canon):
  - `00_OVERVIEW` тАФ tone, the central question, themes, and the **tropes we play & subvert**.
  - `01_SYNOPSIS` тАФ the **entire game**, beginning to end, every twist in order.
  - `02_CHARACTERS` тАФ deep backstories for the Returned, the **four villain masks**, Vayle, Jergal,
    and all **seven companions** (wound ┬╖ secret ┬╖ want vs. need ┬╖ arc ┬╖ personal quest ┬╖ romance ┬╖ fates).
  - `03_ACTS` тАФ Prologue + five acts: settings, quests, set-pieces, the major development & twist of each.
  - `04_ENDINGS` тАФ all **six endings** (+ a hidden failure-state) with flag requirements and per-companion
    epilogue slides.
  - `05_LORE_AND_PHILOSOPHY` тАФ the cosmology, **esoteric in-world texts** (with quotes), the philosophical
    debates each faction embodies, and the recurring symbols.
- ЁЯФЧ `STORY_BIBLE.md` and `README.md` now point into the deep library.

## ЁЯХпя╕П v0.6.0 тАФ *"The Cinderhaunt"* тАФ A Real Dungeon, Recruitment & the Time-Spanning Saga

> The world loop deepens into an actual dungeon crawl with a recruitable companion тАФ and
> the story explodes into a time-travel epic across Realms history.

### ЁЯП░ The Cinderhaunt Dungeon *(new)*
- ЁЯЧ║я╕П `Cinderhaunt`: a **two-chamber dungeon** beneath Baldur's Gate тАФ outer harvest-hall and
  inner sanctum, split by an **iron door** that needs the **Cinderhaunt Key** (found in the
  hub strongbox).
- тЪФя╕П A **guard fight** and a **boss** (the Unbound Maw), triggered from the world; your whole
  **active party** (hero + Garrow + recruits) deploys into each battle.
- ЁЯза Progress is **flag-tracked** тАФ cleared fights, the opened door, and looted chests all
  persist across the exploreтЖФcombat round-trips (new `lootFlag` on containers).
- ЁЯз▒ `CampaignBootstrap` now drives a 3-mode director: **hub тЗД dungeon тЗД encounter**, with a
  forgiving "recover at the door" on a wipe.

### ЁЯзСтАНЁЯдЭтАНЁЯзС Companion Recruitment *(new)*
- ЁЯк╢ **Roen Alleywind**, a Harper rogue, is recruitable in the hub via a branching conversation;
  a dialogue **flag** adds him to the roster and into combat. The director watches
  `companion.<id>.recruited` and recruits automatically тАФ fully data-driven.

### ЁЯУЦ The Story, Reborn *(major)*
- ЁЯММ **`STORY_BIBLE.md` rewritten as a time-spanning, existential epic** (BG2 / Planescape
  scale): the **Unmade** (the accreted nothing of every dissolved Faithless soul), **time
  travel** through **Netheril (Karsus's Folly)**, the **Crown Wars**, the **Time of Troubles**,
  and the **Spellplague**; four nested villains ending in **the Last Returned** тАФ your own
  future self; **7 companions across time**; **5 acts**; **6 endings**; and the twist that
  *you are the Unmade's origin.*

---

## ЁЯОТ v0.5.0 тАФ *"Spoils & Spellfire"* тАФ Loot, Equipment & the VFX Pipeline

> Gear up and light up: a full items/loot/equipment layer plus a combat **VFX system**
> that plays the supplied pixel-effect pack on hits and spells.

### ЁЯОТ Items, Loot & Equipment *(new)*
- ЁЯЧГя╕П `ItemDatabase` (id тЖТ item registry) + content items (swords, armor, **Potion of
  Healing**, the Cinderhaunt Key).
- ЁЯЫбя╕П `EquipmentSystem` / `Equipment`: equip weapons & armor тАФ gear drives **AC** and the
  basic attack; consumables apply effects on use.
- ЁЯОТ `InventoryScreen` (press **I**): backpack, gold, per-member equipped slots, equip/unequip/use.
- ЁЯТ░ **Loot drops**: enemies drop gold + items, auto-awarded to the party on victory.
- ЁЯУж **Lootable containers**: a hub strongbox transfers its contents to the party stash.

### ЁЯТе VFX & Asset Pipeline *(new)*
- тЬи `FxSystem` + `FxAnimator`: fire-and-forget sprite-frame effects played on hit/cast,
  **auto-loaded** from `Resources/FX/<effect>/` (no inspector wiring; no-ops if absent).
- ЁЯФе Abilities gained `hitVfx` / `castVfx`; impacts **auto-pick by damage type**
  (fire/ice/holy/тАж). Healing plays a `heal` effect.
- ЁЯУЦ New **`docs/ASSET_INTEGRATION.md`**: exactly where to drop the pixel FX pack (and
  future character sprites, portraits, tilemaps) so they plug straight in.

---

## ЁЯзн v0.4.0 тАФ *"The Gilded Gate"* тАФ Exploration, the Hub & the World Loop

> The disconnected systems become an actual game: **explore a town, take a quest, walk
> into a dungeon, fight, and return** тАФ the core Baldur's-Gate loop.

### ЁЯзн Exploration Mode *(new)*
- ЁЯЧ║я╕П `ExplorationController`: real-time **click-to-move** the party leader (A* pathing),
  plus **E**/click to interact; movement locks during conversations.
- ЁЯзй `Interactable`: **NPCs** (talk), **exits/doors** (transition), **points of interest**
  (examine) тАФ snaps to the grid and routes the party beside it.
- ЁЯЦея╕П `ExplorationHUD`: party vitals, an **interaction prompt**, examine flavor, and a
  **quest journal** whose objectives tick live from GameFlags.

### ЁЯП░ Baldur's Gate Hub *(new)*
- ЁЯПЩя╕П `BaldursGateHub`: a walkable Lower City slice тАФ the **Herald** (quest giver, branching
  convo), a **proclamation board** to examine, and the **Cinderhaunt stairs** to descend.

### ЁЯФБ Mode Director & Reusable Combat *(new)*
- ЁЯОм `CampaignBootstrap`: the flagship entry тАФ **create тЖТ explore тЖТ quest тЖТ dungeon fight тЖТ
  XP/level тЖТ return to the hub**, with persistent managers across modes.
- ЁЯз▒ `EncounterBuilder`: drop-in turn-based encounter from a roster + victory callback, so
  **any door or trigger** can start a fight. (Combat HUD now tears down cleanly per mode.)

---

## ЁЯПЫя╕П v0.3.0 тАФ *"What the Dead Owe"* тАФ Setting, Creation, Leveling & the Playable Prologue

> The project moves to the **Forgotten Realms / Sword Coast** and gains a full
> create-a-hero тЖТ dialogue тЖТ battle тЖТ level-up loop with a real uGUI HUD.

### ЁЯМН Setting & Story
- ЁЯЧ║я╕П **Story Bible rewritten for the Forgotten Realms** (`docs/STORY_BIBLE.md`): the
  **Wall of the Faithless**, villain **Aldric Morn** & the **Crown of Horns** (Myrkul),
  **Sister Vayle**, **Jergal**, 7 FR companions, factions (Harpers, Flaming Fist, Order of
  the Gauntlet, Zhentarim, church of Kelemvor), 3 acts, and **five branching endings**.

### ЁЯзЩ Character Creation *(new)*
- ЁЯзм `BackgroundDefinition` assets (skills, feature, **flag that unlocks dialogue**).
- ЁЯЫая╕П `CharacterBuilder`: **27-point point-buy** + **standard array**, racial bonuses,
  HP/AC assembly, background kit & flags, the **Returned** trait.
- ЁЯЦея╕П `CharacterCreationScreen`: race/class/background pickers + point-buy stepper.

### ЁЯУИ Leveling & XP *(new)*
- тнР `Progression`: full **5e XP table** (1тЖТ20), HP & ability grants on level-up,
  proficiency scaling, `OnLevelUp` event.
- ЁЯПЖ **XP awarded on victory** тАФ pooled from defeated foes, split among survivors
  (`EncounterController`), can trigger level-ups mid-run.

### ЁЯЦея╕П Real uGUI HUD *(new)*
- ЁЯОЫя╕П `CombatHUD`: runtime-built canvas тАФ **party portraits + live HP bars**, initiative,
  active-unit vitals/economy, a **clickable ability bar**, combat log, End Turn. Zero setup.
- ЁЯЧия╕П `DialogueScreen`: speaker/body/choices with live **skill-check** results; auto-play
  & on-finished hooks.

### ЁЯП░ Act I Content Scaffold *(new)*
- ЁЯУж `SwordCoastContent`: builds FR **races, classes, backgrounds, spells/weapons, status
  effects**, the **opening dialogue** with Aldric's herald, and the **first quest** in code.
- ЁЯОм `PrologueBootstrap`: the flagship demo тАФ **creation тЖТ dialogue тЖТ turn-based battle тЖТ
  XP/level тЖТ quest completion**, fully self-contained.

### ЁЯУЪ Docs
- тЬи New **`FEATURES.md`** (implemented + planned codex with status icons & badges).
- тЬи **README** redesigned with badges, feature grid, and quick-start tables.

## тЪФя╕П v0.2.0 тАФ Combat Depth Layer

> The systems that make combat *feel* like D&D 5e.

- тЬи **Spell slots / resources** spent by leveled spells, refreshed at combat start.
- тШая╕П **Status effects / conditions** (`StatusEffect.cs`, `Condition.cs`): duration, DoT,
  incapacitation, advantage grants, flat AC/attack/speed modifiers.
- тЪЦя╕П **Advantage / disadvantage** in `AttackResolver` (cancel per 5e).
- ЁЯОп **Saving-throw spells with save-for-half** and **healing abilities**.
- ЁЯзй **`AbilityRunner`**: one validated entry point тАФ range, slots, action economy, **AoE**,
  condition application, logging. Player input & enemy AI both use it.
- ЁЯЫбя╕П **Equipment hooks** on `CharacterSheet`.
- ЁЯФе **Demo upgrade**: wizard (Firebolt + **Fireball**), cleric (**Healing Word**), and a
  poison-clawing enemy. HUD shows conditions, slots, and a numbered ability bar.

---

## ЁЯз▒ v0.1.0 тАФ Initial Starter

> The foundation.

- ЁЯЧ║я╕П Grid + isometric projection, **A\* pathfinding**, isometric camera.
- ЁЯО▓ Turn-based combat: initiative + action economy + win/loss.
- ЁЯзЩ 5e stats: abilities, modifiers, proficiency, AC, HP, d20 attacks vs AC.
- ЁЯТм Data-driven **dialogue / quests / items** via ScriptableObjects.
- ЁЯза **GameFlags** story brain; ЁЯТ╛ JSON **save/load**.
- ЁЯХ╣я╕П One-click **playable demo** + the full **story bible**.
